FILE: main.js

'use strict';

const { app, BrowserWindow, ipcMain, dialog, shell } = require('electron');
const path = require('path');
const fs   = require('fs');

// ─── CONFIG ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
const USER_DATA  = app.getPath('userData');
const CONFIG_PATH = path.join(USER_DATA, 'config.json');

// ─── GLOBAL STATE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
let mainWindow = null;
let setupWindow = null;
let db         = null;
let SQL        = null;   // sql.js module (loaded once)
let currentUploadSession = null;

// ─── CONFIG HELPERS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function readConfig() {
  try {
    if (fs.existsSync(CONFIG_PATH)) return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(CONFIG_PATH, 'utf-8'));
  } catch {}
  return null;
}

function writeConfig(config) {
  try {
    if (!fs.existsSync(USER_DATA)) fs.mkdirSync(USER_DATA, { recursive: true });
    fs.writeFileSync(CONFIG_PATH, JSON.stringify(config, null, 2), 'utf-8');
    return true;
  } catch (e) { console.error('Config write error:', e.message); return false; }
}

// ─── SQL.JS LOADER ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function loadSqlJs() {
  if (SQL) return SQL;
  const initSqlJs = require('sql.js');
  // In packaged app: WASM is in resources/ folder.
  // In development: WASM is in node_modules/sql.js/dist/
  const wasmPath = app.isPackaged
    ? path.join(process.resourcesPath, 'sql-wasm.wasm')
    : path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'sql.js', 'dist', 'sql-wasm.wasm');

  SQL = await initSqlJs({ locateFile: () => wasmPath });
  return SQL;
}

// ─── DATABASE INIT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
async function initDatabase(dbFile) {
  try {
    const sqlJs = await loadSqlJs();
    const { Database } = require('./database/db-adapter');
    const schema = require('./database/schema');

    db = new Database(dbFile);
    await db.init(sqlJs);
    schema.initialise(db);

    global.protrackDB = db;
    console.log('[DB] Initialised at', dbFile);
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[DB] Init error:', e.message);
    return false;
  }
}

// ─── WINDOW CREATORS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function createSetupWindow() {
  setupWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 620, height: 480, resizable: false, frame: true, center: true,
    title: 'ProTrack Analytics - Setup',
    backgroundColor: '#0a0a1a',
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'preload.js'),
      contextIsolation: true, nodeIntegration: false, sandbox: false
    },
    show: false
  });
  setupWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, 'src', 'setup', 'setup.html'));
  setupWindow.once('ready-to-show', () => setupWindow.show());
  setupWindow.on('closed', () => { setupWindow = null; });
  setupWindow.setMenuBarVisibility(false);
}

function createMainWindow() {
  mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 1400, height: 900, minWidth: 1200, minHeight: 700,
    center: true, title: 'ProTrack Analytics',
    backgroundColor: '#0a0a1a',
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'preload.js'),
      contextIsolation: true, nodeIntegration: false, sandbox: false
    },
    show: false
  });
  mainWindow.loadFile(path.join(__dirname, 'src', 'landing', 'landing.html'));
  mainWindow.once('ready-to-show', () => { mainWindow.show(); mainWindow.maximize(); });
  mainWindow.on('closed', () => { mainWindow = null; });
  mainWindow.setMenuBarVisibility(false);
}

// ─── APP STARTUP ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
app.whenReady().then(async () => {
  const config = readConfig();

  if (!config || !config.dbPath || !fs.existsSync(config.dbPath)) {
    createSetupWindow();
  } else {
    const dbFile = path.join(config.dbPath, 'protrack.db');
    const ok = await initDatabase(dbFile);
    if (ok) {
      registerIpcHandlers();
      createMainWindow();
    } else {
      createSetupWindow();
    }
  }

  app.on('activate', () => {
    if (BrowserWindow.getAllWindows().length === 0) createMainWindow();
  });
});

app.on('window-all-closed', () => {
  if (db) try { db.close(); } catch {}
  if (process.platform !== 'darwin') app.quit();
});

// ─── SETUP IPC ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
ipcMain.handle('setup:select-folder', async () => {
  const result = await dialog.showOpenDialog(setupWindow || mainWindow, {
    title: 'Choose Database Folder',
    properties: ['openDirectory', 'createDirectory'],
    buttonLabel: 'Select Folder'
  });
  if (result.canceled || !result.filePaths.length) return { success: false };
  return { success: true, folderPath: result.filePaths[0] };
});

ipcMain.handle('setup:save-config', async (event, folderPath) => {
  try {
    fs.accessSync(folderPath, fs.constants.W_OK);
    const dbFile = path.join(folderPath, 'protrack.db');
    const config = { dbPath: folderPath, dbFile, createdAt: new Date().toISOString() };
    if (!writeConfig(config)) return { success: false, error: 'Could not write config file.' };
    const ok = await initDatabase(dbFile);
    if (!ok) return { success: false, error: 'Could not initialise database.' };
    registerIpcHandlers();
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, error: `Folder is not writable: ${e.message}` };
  }
});

ipcMain.handle('setup:complete', async () => {
  createMainWindow();
  if (setupWindow) setTimeout(() => { if (setupWindow) setupWindow.close(); }, 300);
});

// ─── IPC HANDLER REGISTRATION ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function registerIpcHandlers() {
  if (global.ipcHandlersRegistered) return;
  global.ipcHandlersRegistered = true;

  const handlers = require('./ipc/handlers');
  handlers.register(ipcMain, {
    getDB:         () => db,
    getSession:    () => currentUploadSession,
    setSession:    (s) => { currentUploadSession = s; },
    getMainWindow: () => mainWindow
  });
}

// ─── UTILITY IPC ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
ipcMain.handle('app:get-config',  () => readConfig() || {});
ipcMain.handle('app:get-version', () => ({
  version: app.getVersion(),
  electronVersion: process.versions.electron,
  nodeVersion: process.versions.node
}));
ipcMain.handle('app:open-folder', async (event, p) => {
  if (p && fs.existsSync(p)) shell.openPath(p);
});

ipcMain.handle('dialog:select-folder', async () => {
  const r = await dialog.showOpenDialog(mainWindow, {
    title: 'Select Folder', properties: ['openDirectory', 'createDirectory']
  });
  if (r.canceled || !r.filePaths.length) return { success: false };
  return { success: true, folderPath: r.filePaths[0] };
});

ipcMain.handle('dialog:select-file', async (event, filters) => {
  const r = await dialog.showOpenDialog(mainWindow, {
    title: 'Select File', properties: ['openFile'],
    filters: filters || [{ name: 'Excel Files', extensions: ['xlsx', 'xls'] }]
  });
  if (r.canceled || !r.filePaths.length) return { success: false };
  return { success: true, filePath: r.filePaths[0] };
});

ipcMain.handle('dialog:save-file', async (event, opts) => {
  const r = await dialog.showSaveDialog(mainWindow, {
    title: opts.title || 'Save File',
    defaultPath: opts.defaultPath || 'export',
    filters: opts.filters || [{ name: 'All Files', extensions: ['*'] }]
  });
  if (r.canceled) return { success: false };
  return { success: true, filePath: r.filePath };
});

ipcMain.handle('settings:change-db-path', async (event, newFolderPath) => {
  try {
    fs.accessSync(newFolderPath, fs.constants.W_OK);
    const config   = readConfig() || {};
    const oldFile  = path.join(config.dbPath || '', 'protrack.db');
    const newFile  = path.join(newFolderPath, 'protrack.db');
    if (db) { db.close(); db = null; global.protrackDB = null; }
    if (fs.existsSync(oldFile)) fs.copyFileSync(oldFile, newFile);
    config.dbPath = newFolderPath; config.dbFile = newFile;
    writeConfig(config);
    const ok = await initDatabase(newFile);
    if (!ok) return { success: false, error: 'Failed to open database at new path.' };
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message }; }
});

'use strict';

const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require('electron');

// ─── SAFE API EXPOSED TO RENDERER ────────────────────────────────
contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('protrack', {

  // ── SETUP ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  setup: {
    selectFolder: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('setup:select-folder'),
    saveConfig: (folderPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke('setup:save-config', folderPath),
    complete: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('setup:complete')
  },

  // ── APP ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  app: {
    getConfig: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('app:get-config'),
    getVersion: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('app:get-version'),
    openFolder: (p) => ipcRenderer.invoke('app:open-folder', p)
  },

  // ── DIALOGS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  dialog: {
    selectFolder: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('dialog:select-folder'),
    selectFile: (filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('dialog:select-file', filters),
    saveFile: (opts) => ipcRenderer.invoke('dialog:save-file', opts)
  },

  // ── UPLOAD ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  upload: {
    processFiles: (filePaths) => ipcRenderer.invoke('upload:process-files', filePaths),
    clearSession: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('upload:clear-session'),
    getSessionStats: (filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('upload:get-session-stats', filters)
  },

  // ── PIPELINE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  pipeline: {
    getStats: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('pipeline:get-stats', source, filters)
  },

  // ── EXECUTIVE SUMMARY ────────────────────────────────────────
  executive: {
    getStats: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('executive:get-stats', source, filters)
  },

  // ── UW PRODUCTIVITY ──────────────────────────────────────────
  uw: {
    getStats: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-stats', source, filters),
    getSummaryTable: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-summary-table', source, filters),
    getPendingProposals: (source, filters, page) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-pending-proposals', source, filters, page),
    getDailyOutput: (source, filters, uwName) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-daily-output', source, filters, uwName),
    getBusinessTypeMix: (source, filters, uwName) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-business-type-mix', source, filters, uwName),
    getActionTypeMix: (source, filters, uwName) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-action-type-mix', source, filters, uwName),
    getAcceptRateChart: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:get-accept-rate-chart', source, filters),
    exportPending: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('uw:export-pending', source, filters)
  },

  // ── TAT / SLA ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  tat: {
    getStats: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('tat:get-stats', source, filters),
    getDrillDown: (source, filters, page) => ipcRenderer.invoke('tat:get-drill-down', source, filters, page),
    exportDrillDown: (source, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('tat:export-drill-down', source, filters)
  },

  // ── DRILL-DOWN ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  drilldown: {
    search: (source, query) => ipcRenderer.invoke('drilldown:search', source, query),
    getDetail: (source, proposalNo) => ipcRenderer.invoke('drilldown:get-detail', source, proposalNo),
    exportExcel: (source, proposalNo) => ipcRenderer.invoke('drilldown:export-excel', source, proposalNo),
    exportPdf: (source, proposalNo) => ipcRenderer.invoke('drilldown:export-pdf', source, proposalNo)
  },

  // ── SETTINGS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  settings: {
    getAll: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:get-all'),
    save: (key, value) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:save', key, value),
    saveMultiple: (obj) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:save-multiple', obj),
    getUploadHistory: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:get-upload-history'),
    deleteBatch: (batchId) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:delete-batch', batchId),
    changeDbPath: (newPath) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:change-db-path', newPath),
    getDbStats: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:get-db-stats'),
    verifyPin: (pin) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:verify-pin', pin),
    pinRequired: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:pin-required'),
    savePin: (pin, enabled) => ipcRenderer.invoke('settings:save-pin', pin, enabled)
  },

  // ── EXPORT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  export: {
    toPdf: (tabName, filters) => ipcRenderer.invoke('export:to-pdf', tabName, filters),
    toExcel: (type, data, fileName) => ipcRenderer.invoke('export:to-excel', type, data, fileName)
  },

  // ── FILTERS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  filters: {
    getOptions: (source) => ipcRenderer.invoke('filters:get-options', source)
  }
});

FILE: database/db-adapter.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - SQLite Adapter (sql.js wrapper)
 * Pure-JS SQLite — no native compilation, works in any Electron build.
 */

const fs   = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

function toPositional(sql, params) {
  if (params === null || params === undefined) return { sql, params: [] };
  if (Array.isArray(params)) return { sql, params };
  if (typeof params === 'object') {
    const positional = [];
    const newSql = sql.replace(/@(\w+)/g, (_, key) => {
      positional.push(params[key] !== undefined ? params[key] : null);
      return '?';
    });
    if (positional.length === 0) return { sql, params: Object.values(params) };
    return { sql: newSql, params: positional };
  }
  return { sql, params: [params] };
}

function normalizeArgs(args) {
  if (args.length === 0) return null;
  if (args.length === 1) return args[0];
  return Array.from(args);
}

class Statement {
  constructor(adapter, sql) {
    this._adapter = adapter;
    this._sql     = sql;
  }
  run(...args) {
    const { sql, params } = toPositional(this._sql, normalizeArgs(args));
    this._adapter._runDml(sql, params);
    this._adapter._schedSave();
  }
  get(...args) {
    const { sql, params } = toPositional(this._sql, normalizeArgs(args));
    const rows = this._adapter._query(sql, params);
    return rows.length ? rows[0] : undefined;
  }
  all(...args) {
    const { sql, params } = toPositional(this._sql, normalizeArgs(args));
    return this._adapter._query(sql, params);
  }
}

class Database {
  constructor(filePath) {
    this._filePath  = filePath;
    this._db        = null;
    this._saveTimer = null;
  }

  async init(SQL) {
    if (fs.existsSync(this._filePath)) {
      const buf = fs.readFileSync(this._filePath);
      this._db  = new SQL.Database(buf);
    } else {
      this._db = new SQL.Database();
    }
    // Always enable FK enforcement on every connection (sql.js default is OFF)
    try { this._db.run('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON'); } catch {}
    return this;
  }

  pragma(str) {
    if (!this._db) return;
    const s = str.trim();
    // Only run FK pragma — WAL/sync/cache are no-ops in sql.js
    if (/^foreign_keys\s*=/i.test(s)) {
      try { this._db.run('PRAGMA ' + s); } catch {}
    }
  }

  exec(sql) {
    if (!this._db) return;
    // Split on semicolons and run each statement individually
    // This handles multi-statement DDL blocks from schema.js
    const stmts = sql.split(';').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    for (const stmt of stmts) {
      try { this._db.run(stmt); } catch (e) {
        console.error('[DB] exec error:', e.message, '\nStmt:', stmt.substring(0, 100));
      }
    }
    this._schedSave();
  }

  prepare(sql) { return new Statement(this, sql); }

  transaction(fn) {
    const self = this;
    return function (...args) {
      self._db.run('BEGIN');
      try {
        const result = fn(...args);
        self._db.run('COMMIT');
        self._save();
        return result;
      } catch (e) {
        try { self._db.run('ROLLBACK'); } catch {}
        throw e;
      }
    };
  }

  close() {
    clearTimeout(this._saveTimer);
    this._save();
    if (this._db) { this._db.close(); this._db = null; }
  }

  _runDml(sql, params) {
    if (!this._db) throw new Error('[DB] Database not initialised');
    try {
      this._db.run(sql, params && params.length ? params : undefined);
    } catch (e) {
      throw new Error(`[DB] DML error: ${e.message}\nSQL: ${sql.substring(0, 200)}`);
    }
  }

  _query(sql, params) {
    if (!this._db) return [];
    let stmt;
    try {
      stmt = this._db.prepare(sql);
      if (params && params.length) stmt.bind(params);
      const rows = [];
      while (stmt.step()) rows.push(stmt.getAsObject());
      return rows;
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[DB] Query error:', e.message, '\nSQL:', sql.substring(0, 200));
      return [];
    } finally {
      if (stmt) { try { stmt.free(); } catch {} }
    }
  }

  _save() {
    if (!this._db) return;
    try {
      const data = this._db.export();
      const dir  = path.dirname(this._filePath);
      if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
      fs.writeFileSync(this._filePath, Buffer.from(data));
    } catch (e) { console.error('[DB] Save error:', e.message); }
  }

  _schedSave() {
    clearTimeout(this._saveTimer);
    this._saveTimer = setTimeout(() => this._save(), 300);
  }
}

module.exports = { Database };


================================================================================
FILE: database/schema.js
================================================================================
'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Database Schema
 * Initialises all tables, indexes, and pragmas
 */
function initialise(db) {
  // ── PERFORMANCE PRAGMAS ──────────────────────────────────────
  db.pragma('journal_mode = WAL');       // Fastest for concurrent reads
  db.pragma('synchronous = NORMAL');     // Safe + fast balance
  db.pragma('cache_size = -32000');      // 32MB cache
  db.pragma('temp_store = MEMORY');      // Temp tables in memory
  db.pragma('mmap_size = 268435456');    // 256MB memory-mapped I/O
  db.pragma('foreign_keys = ON');

  // ── UPLOAD BATCHES ───────────────────────────────────────────
  db.exec(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS upload_batches (
      id              INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      batch_id        TEXT    UNIQUE NOT NULL,
      type            TEXT    NOT NULL,         -- 'audit_log' | 'uw_productivity'
      filename        TEXT    NOT NULL,
      rows            INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
      date_from       TEXT,
      date_to         TEXT,
      uploaded_at     DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
    );
  `);

  // ── AUDIT LOG ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  db.exec(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_log (
      id                          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      batch_id                    TEXT    NOT NULL,
      proposal_no                 TEXT    NOT NULL,
      partner_application_number  TEXT,
      business_type               TEXT,
      product_name                TEXT,
      proposal_inward_date        DATETIME,
      first_payment_date          DATETIME,
      coming_from_bucket          TEXT,
      coming_with_decision        TEXT,
      current_bucket              TEXT,
      current_bucket_date         DATETIME,
      current_bucket_time         DATETIME,
      no_of_days                  REAL    DEFAULT 0,
      proposal_level_status       TEXT,
      proposal_level_status_norm  TEXT,
      queue_start_date            DATETIME,
      queue_end_date              DATETIME,
      FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES upload_batches(batch_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_proposal     ON audit_log(proposal_no);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_batch        ON audit_log(batch_id);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_biz_type     ON audit_log(business_type);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_product      ON audit_log(product_name);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_bucket       ON audit_log(current_bucket);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_inward_date  ON audit_log(proposal_inward_date);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_no_days      ON audit_log(no_of_days);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_queue_start  ON audit_log(queue_start_date);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_status_norm  ON audit_log(proposal_level_status_norm);
  `);

  // ── UW PRODUCTIVITY ──────────────────────────────────────────
  db.exec(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS uw_productivity (
      id              INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
      batch_id        TEXT    NOT NULL,
      uw_name         TEXT    NOT NULL,
      proposal_no     TEXT    NOT NULL,
      action_date     DATE    NOT NULL,
      product         TEXT,
      business_type   TEXT,
      refer_to_uw     INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      accept          INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      rejected        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      counter_offer   INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      additional_info INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      additional_test INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      telemer         INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      ppc             INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      refer_to_cops   INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      rulebook_refund INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      -- Derived: computed on insert, stored for query performance
      is_final        INTEGER DEFAULT 0,  -- 1 if accept/rejected/counter_offer/rulebook_refund
      is_pending      INTEGER DEFAULT 0,  -- 1 if refer_to_uw/additional_info/etc
      FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES upload_batches(batch_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
    );

    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_proposal    ON uw_productivity(proposal_no);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_batch       ON uw_productivity(batch_id);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_name        ON uw_productivity(uw_name);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_date        ON uw_productivity(action_date);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_biz_type    ON uw_productivity(business_type);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_is_final    ON uw_productivity(is_final);
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_is_pending  ON uw_productivity(is_pending);

    -- Composite indices for the most common query patterns
    -- Speeds up pending/clear queries: MAX(CASE WHEN accept=1 OR rejected=1 ...)
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_final_cols  ON uw_productivity(accept, rejected, counter_offer, rulebook_refund);
    -- Speeds up per-UW grouping queries (perUwClearPendingSQL)
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_name_prop   ON uw_productivity(uw_name, proposal_no);
    -- Speeds up batch+proposal lookups together
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_uw_batch_prop  ON uw_productivity(batch_id, proposal_no);
    -- Speeds up audit_log TAT/SLA queries (bucket filter + no_of_days)
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_al_batch_bkt   ON audit_log(batch_id, current_bucket);
  `);

  // ── APP SETTINGS ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  db.exec(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS app_settings (
      key   TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      value TEXT NOT NULL
    );
  `);

  // ── SEED DEFAULT SETTINGS ────────────────────────────────────
  const insertSetting = db.prepare(`
    INSERT OR IGNORE INTO app_settings (key, value) VALUES (?, ?)
  `);

  const defaults = [
    ['sla_threshold_days', '1'],
    ['pending_rate_warning_pct', '10'],
    ['export_company_name', 'Tata AIG General Insurance Company'],
    ['export_logo_path', ''],
    ['export_output_path', ''],
    ['export_pdf_page_size', 'A4'],
    ['appearance_theme', 'dark'],
    ['appearance_sidebar_style', 'icons_labels'],
    ['appearance_date_format', 'DD-MM-YYYY'],
    ['security_pin_enabled', 'false'],
    ['security_pin_hash', ''],
    ['security_autolock_minutes', '0'],
    ['pin_verified_session', 'false']
  ];

  const insertMany = db.transaction(() => {
    defaults.forEach(([k, v]) => insertSetting.run(k, v));
  });
  insertMany();

  // ── DATA INTEGRITY REPAIR ─────────────────────────────────────
  // Recalculate is_final for any rows where it disagrees with the action columns.
  // Runs on every startup — safe because it only touches rows that are inconsistent.
  // Fixes data ingested by older versions where is_final may have been mis-computed.
  try {
    db.exec(`
      UPDATE uw_productivity
      SET is_final = CASE
        WHEN accept=1 OR rejected=1 OR counter_offer=1 OR rulebook_refund=1 THEN 1
        ELSE 0
      END
      WHERE is_final != (CASE
        WHEN accept=1 OR rejected=1 OR counter_offer=1 OR rulebook_refund=1 THEN 1
        ELSE 0
      END)
    `);
    db.exec(`
      UPDATE uw_productivity
      SET is_pending = CASE
        WHEN refer_to_uw=1 OR additional_info=1 OR additional_test=1
          OR telemer=1 OR ppc=1 OR refer_to_cops=1 THEN 1
        ELSE 0
      END
      WHERE is_pending != (CASE
        WHEN refer_to_uw=1 OR additional_info=1 OR additional_test=1
          OR telemer=1 OR ppc=1 OR refer_to_cops=1 THEN 1
        ELSE 0
      END)
    `);
  } catch(e) {
    // Table may not exist yet (first run) — silently skip
  }

  console.log('[DB] Schema initialised successfully');
}

// ─── QUERY HELPERS ───────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * Build SQL WHERE clause from filter object
 * source: 'session' (uses in-memory) | 'history' (uses DB)
 * filters: { businessType, productName, status, bucket, dateFrom, dateTo }
 * tableAlias: 'al' | 'uw'
 */
function buildAuditFilters(filters = {}, alias = 'al') {
  const conditions = [];
  const params = {};

  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.business_type = @businessType`);
    params.businessType = filters.businessType;
  }
  if (filters.productName && filters.productName !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.product_name = @productName`);
    params.productName = filters.productName;
  }
  if (filters.status && filters.status !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_level_status_norm = @status`);
    params.status = filters.status;
  }
  if (filters.bucket && filters.bucket !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.current_bucket = @bucket`);
    params.bucket = filters.bucket;
  }
  if (filters.dateFrom) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_inward_date >= @dateFrom`);
    params.dateFrom = filters.dateFrom;
  }
  if (filters.dateTo) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_inward_date <= @dateTo`);
    params.dateTo = filters.dateTo;
  }

  return {
    where: conditions.length ? 'WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ') : '',
    params
  };
}

function buildUwFilters(filters = {}, alias = 'uw') {
  const conditions = [];
  const params = {};

  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.business_type = @businessType`);
    params.businessType = filters.businessType;
  }
  if (filters.productName && filters.productName !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.product = @productName`);
    params.productName = filters.productName;
  }
  if (filters.dateFrom) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.action_date >= @dateFrom`);
    params.dateFrom = filters.dateFrom;
  }
  if (filters.dateTo) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.action_date <= @dateTo`);
    params.dateTo = filters.dateTo;
  }

  return {
    where: conditions.length ? 'WHERE ' + conditions.join(' AND ') : '',
    params
  };
}

// ─── NORMALISE STATUS ────────────────────────────────────────────
function normaliseStatus(raw) {
  if (!raw) return '';
  // Strip spaces, hyphens, underscores, lowercase
  const clean = raw.toString().replace(/[\s\-_]/g, '').toLowerCase();

  const map = {
    'refertouw':             'Refer to UW',
    'pendingforissuance':    'Pending for Issuance',
    'issued':                'Issued',
    'rejected':              'Rejected',
    'cancelled':             'Cancelled',
    'underwriting':          'Underwriting',
    'additionalinfopending': 'Additional Info Pending',
  };

  return map[clean] || raw.toString().trim();
}

// ─── DAY CATEGORY ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function dayCategory(days) {
  const d = Math.floor(days || 0);
  return d <= 5 ? String(d) : 'More than 5';
}

// ─── IS CLEAR ACTION ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function isClearAction(row) {
  return (row.accept || row.rejected || row.counter_offer || row.rulebook_refund) ? 1 : 0;
}

function isPendingAction(row) {
  return (row.refer_to_uw || row.additional_info || row.additional_test ||
          row.telemer || row.ppc || row.refer_to_cops) ? 1 : 0;
}

module.exports = { initialise, buildAuditFilters, buildUwFilters, normaliseStatus, dayCategory, isClearAction, isPendingAction };


================================================================================
FILE: database/ingest.js
================================================================================
'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Data Ingestion Engine
 * Handles Excel parsing, file type detection, normalisation,
 * all business calculations, and database writes.
 */

const xlsx   = require('xlsx');
const schema = require('./schema');

// ─── COLUMN NORMALISATION ────────────────────────────────────────
// Strip spaces, hyphens, underscores, slashes, parens, dots → lowercase
function normHeader(h) {
  return String(h || '').toLowerCase().replace(/[\s\-_\/\(\)\.\*#]/g, '');
}

// ─── COLUMN MAPS ────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Maps normalised header → internal DB column name
const AUDIT_COL_MAP = {
  'ipdsproposalno':               'proposal_no',
  'ipdsproposalnumber':           'proposal_no',
  'proposalno':                   'proposal_no',
  'partnerapplicationnumber':     'partner_application_number',
  'partnerapplicationno':         'partner_application_number',
  'businesstype':                 'business_type',
  'productname':                  'product_name',
  'product':                      'product_name',
  'proposalinwarddate':           'proposal_inward_date',
  'inwarddate':                   'proposal_inward_date',
  'firstpaymentdate':             'first_payment_date',
  'comingfrombucket':             'coming_from_bucket',
  'fromqueue':                    'coming_from_bucket',
  'comingwithdecision':          'coming_with_decision',
  'decision':                     'coming_with_decision',
  'currentbucket':                'current_bucket',
  'currentqueue':                 'current_bucket',
  'currentbucketdate':            'current_bucket_date',
  'currentbuckettime':            'current_bucket_time',
  'noofdays':                     'no_of_days',
  'days':                         'no_of_days',
  'proposallevelstatus':          'proposal_level_status',
  'status':                       'proposal_level_status',
  'queuestartdate':               'queue_start_date',
  'queuestart':                   'queue_start_date',
  'queueenddate':                 'queue_end_date',
  'queueend':                     'queue_end_date'
};

const UW_COL_MAP = {
  'uwname':                       'uw_name',
  'underwritername':              'uw_name',
  'name':                         'uw_name',
  'sourceproposalnumber':         'proposal_no',
  'proposalnumber':               'proposal_no',
  'proposalno':                   'proposal_no',
  'actiontakenon':                'action_date',
  'actiondate':                   'action_date',
  'date':                         'action_date',
  'product':                      'product',

  'counterofferinitiated':        'counter_offer',

  'additionalinforaised':         'additional_info',

  'additionaltestraised':         'additional_test',

  'telemervideomerraised':        'telemer',

  'ppcraised':                    'ppc',

  'rulebookrefundinitiated':      'rulebook_refund',
  'rulebookrefund':               'rulebook_refund',
  'rulebook':                     'rulebook_refund',
  // Discard these columns:
  'grandtotal':                   '__DISCARD__',
  'final':                        '__DISCARD__'
};

// Required columns for file type identification (must have ALL of these)
const AUDIT_REQUIRED = ['proposal_no', 'business_type', 'no_of_days', 'queue_start_date', 'queue_end_date'];
const UW_REQUIRED    = ['uw_name', 'proposal_no', 'action_date', 'accept', 'rejected'];

// ─── FILE TYPE DETECTION ─────────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * Detects whether a sheet's headers match Audit Log or UW Productivity schema.
 * Returns { type: 'audit_log'|'uw_productivity'|null, colMapping, missingRequired }
 */
function detectFileType(headers) {
  const normHeaders = headers.map(normHeader);

  function buildMapping(colMap) {
    const mapping = {}; // rawHeader → dbColumn
    headers.forEach((raw, i) => {
      const norm = normHeaders[i];
      const dbCol = colMap[norm];
      if (dbCol && dbCol !== '__DISCARD__') {
        mapping[raw] = dbCol;
      }
    });
    return mapping;
  }

  function checkRequired(mapping, required) {
    const presentCols = new Set(Object.values(mapping));
    return required.filter(r => !presentCols.has(r));
  }

  // Try audit log first
  const auditMapping = buildMapping(AUDIT_COL_MAP);
  const auditMissing = checkRequired(auditMapping, AUDIT_REQUIRED);

  // Try UW productivity
  const uwMapping = buildMapping(UW_COL_MAP);
  const uwMissing = checkRequired(uwMapping, UW_REQUIRED);

  // Prefer the one with fewer missing required columns
  if (auditMissing.length === 0 && uwMissing.length > 0) {
    return { type: 'audit_log', colMapping: auditMapping, missingRequired: [] };
  }
  if (uwMissing.length === 0 && auditMissing.length > 0) {
    return { type: 'uw_productivity', colMapping: uwMapping, missingRequired: [] };
  }
  if (auditMissing.length === 0 && uwMissing.length === 0) {
    // Both match: audit takes precedence (more distinctive columns)
    return { type: 'audit_log', colMapping: auditMapping, missingRequired: [] };
  }

  // Neither fully matches: return whichever is closer with missing list
  if (auditMissing.length <= uwMissing.length) {
    return { type: null, colMapping: auditMapping, missingRequired: auditMissing, attempted: 'audit_log' };
  }
  return { type: null, colMapping: uwMapping, missingRequired: uwMissing, attempted: 'uw_productivity' };
}

// ─── PARSE EXCEL FILE ────────────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * Parses an Excel buffer and finds the first sheet with matching required columns.
 * Returns { sheetName, headers, rows } or throws on failure.
 */
function parseExcelFile(buffer, fileName) {
  let workbook;
  try {
    workbook = xlsx.read(buffer, {
      type: 'buffer',
      cellDates: true,
      dateNF: 'yyyy-mm-dd',
      raw: false
    });
  } catch (e) {
    throw new Error(`Cannot read Excel file "${fileName}": ${e.message}`);
  }

  if (!workbook.SheetNames || workbook.SheetNames.length === 0) {
    throw new Error(`File "${fileName}" contains no sheets.`);
  }

  // Try each sheet and return the first one that matches either schema
  let bestResult = null;

  for (const sheetName of workbook.SheetNames) {
    const ws = workbook.Sheets[sheetName];
    if (!ws) continue;

    const rawRows = xlsx.utils.sheet_to_json(ws, { header: 1, defval: '', raw: false, dateNF: 'yyyy-mm-dd hh:mm:ss' });
    if (!rawRows || rawRows.length < 2) continue;

    // Find the header row (first non-empty row)
    let headerRowIdx = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(5, rawRows.length); i++) {
      if (rawRows[i].some(cell => cell && String(cell).trim())) {
        headerRowIdx = i;
        break;
      }
    }

    const headers = rawRows[headerRowIdx].map(h => String(h || '').trim()).filter((h, i) => h || i < 5);
    if (headers.length === 0) continue;

    const detection = detectFileType(headers);
    if (detection.type !== null) {
      // Valid sheet found
      const dataRows = rawRows.slice(headerRowIdx + 1).filter(r => r.some(c => c !== '' && c !== null && c !== undefined));
      return { sheetName, headers, rows: dataRows, detection };
    }

    // Keep as fallback if no perfect match found
    if (!bestResult) {
      bestResult = { sheetName, headers, rows: rawRows.slice(headerRowIdx + 1), detection };
    }
  }

  // No sheet matched perfectly
  if (bestResult) {
    const { detection } = bestResult;
    throw new Error(
      `File schema not recognised. Missing required columns: ${detection.missingRequired.join(', ')}. ` +
      `Expected either an Audit Log or UW Productivity Sheet.`
    );
  }

  throw new Error(`No readable data sheets found in "${fileName}".`);
}

// ─── DATE HELPERS ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function toDateStr(val) {
  if (!val) return null;
  if (val instanceof Date) {
    if (isNaN(val.getTime())) return null;
    return val.toISOString().replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 23);
  }
  const s = String(val).trim();
  if (!s || s === '0' || s === '') return null;

  // Handle DD-MM-YYYY or DD/MM/YYYY with optional time (12h or 24h)
  const dmyMatch = s.match(/^(\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{4})\s*(.*)$/);
  if (dmyMatch) {
    const [, d, m, y, time] = dmyMatch;
    let isoStr = y + '-' + m.padStart(2, '0') + '-' + d.padStart(2, '0');
    if (time) {
      const tMatch = time.match(/(\d{1,2}):(\d{2}):?(\d{2})?\s*(AM|PM)?/i);
      if (tMatch) {
        let [, h, min, sec, ampm] = tMatch;
        h = parseInt(h, 10);
        if (ampm && ampm.toUpperCase() === 'PM' && h < 12) h += 12;
        if (ampm && ampm.toUpperCase() === 'AM' && h === 12) h = 0;
        isoStr += ' ' + String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + min + ':' + (sec || '00');
      }
    }
    const d2 = new Date(isoStr);
    if (!isNaN(d2.getTime())) return isoStr;
  }

  // Excel serial number
  const n = Number(s);
  if (!isNaN(n) && n > 40000 && n < 60000) {
    const d = new Date((n - 25569) * 86400 * 1000);
    if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) return d.toISOString().replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 23);
  }

  // ISO or other standard formats
  const d = new Date(s);
  if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) return d.toISOString().replace('T', ' ').substring(0, 23);
  return null;
}

function toInt(val, def = 0) {
  if (val === null || val === undefined || val === '') return def;
  const n = parseInt(val, 10);
  return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
}

function toFloat(val, def = 0) {
  if (val === null || val === undefined || val === '') return def;
  const n = parseFloat(val);
  return isNaN(n) ? def : n;
}

// ─── ROW MAPPER: AUDIT LOG ───────────────────────────────────────
function mapAuditRow(rawRow, headers, colMapping, batchId) {
  const row = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => {
    const dbCol = colMapping[h];
    if (dbCol) row[dbCol] = rawRow[i] !== undefined ? rawRow[i] : '';
  });

  if (!row.proposal_no) return null;

  const normStatus = schema.normaliseStatus(row.proposal_level_status);
  const noOfDays   = toFloat(row.no_of_days, 0);

  return {
    batch_id:                     batchId,
    proposal_no:                  String(row.proposal_no || '').trim(),
    partner_application_number:   String(row.partner_application_number || '').trim() || null,
    business_type:                String(row.business_type || '').trim() || null,
    product_name:                 String(row.product_name || '').trim() || null,
    proposal_inward_date:         toDateStr(row.proposal_inward_date),
    first_payment_date:           toDateStr(row.first_payment_date),
    coming_from_bucket:           String(row.coming_from_bucket || '').trim() || null,
    coming_with_decision:         String(row.coming_with_decision || '').trim() || null,
    current_bucket:               String(row.current_bucket || '').trim() || null,
    current_bucket_date:          toDateStr(row.current_bucket_date),
    current_bucket_time:          toDateStr(row.current_bucket_time),
    no_of_days:                   noOfDays,
    proposal_level_status:        String(row.proposal_level_status || '').trim() || null,
    proposal_level_status_norm:   normStatus || null,
    queue_start_date:             toDateStr(row.queue_start_date),
    queue_end_date:               toDateStr(row.queue_end_date)
  };
}

// ─── ROW MAPPER: UW PRODUCTIVITY ────────────────────────────────
function mapUwRow(rawRow, headers, colMapping, batchId) {
  const row = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => {
    const dbCol = colMapping[h];
    if (dbCol && dbCol !== '__DISCARD__') row[dbCol] = rawRow[i] !== undefined ? rawRow[i] : '';
  });

  if (!row.uw_name || !row.proposal_no) return null;

  const accept          = toInt(row.accept);
  const rejected        = toInt(row.rejected);
  const counter_offer   = toInt(row.counter_offer);
  const rulebook_refund = toInt(row.rulebook_refund);
  const refer_to_uw     = toInt(row.refer_to_uw);
  const additional_info = toInt(row.additional_info);
  const additional_test = toInt(row.additional_test);
  const telemer         = toInt(row.telemer);
  const ppc             = toInt(row.ppc);
  const refer_to_cops   = toInt(row.refer_to_cops);

  const is_final   = (accept || rejected || counter_offer || rulebook_refund) ? 1 : 0;
  const is_pending = (refer_to_uw || additional_info || additional_test || telemer || ppc || refer_to_cops) ? 1 : 0;

  return {
    batch_id:        batchId,
    uw_name:         String(row.uw_name || '').trim(),
    proposal_no:     String(row.proposal_no || '').trim(),
    action_date:     toDateStr(row.action_date),
    product:         String(row.product || '').trim() || null,
    business_type:   String(row.business_type || '').trim() || null,
    refer_to_uw,
    accept,
    rejected,
    counter_offer,
    additional_info,
    additional_test,
    telemer,
    ppc,
    refer_to_cops,
    rulebook_refund,
    is_final,
    is_pending
  };
}

// ─── GENERATE BATCH ID ───────────────────────────────────────────
function generateBatchId(type, fileName) {
  const now  = new Date();
  const ts   = now.toISOString().replace(/[-:T\.Z]/g, '').substring(0, 14);
  const rand = Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 6).toUpperCase();
  const tag  = type === 'audit_log' ? 'AL' : 'UW';
  return `BATCH_${ts}_${tag}_${rand}`;
}

// ─── MAIN INGEST FUNCTION ────────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * Ingests an uploaded Excel file into the database.
 * @param {Buffer}  buffer    - Raw Excel file buffer
 * @param {string}  fileName  - Original filename
 * @param {object}  db        - better-sqlite3 db instance
 * @returns {{ success, batchId, type, rows, error }}
 */
function ingestFile(buffer, fileName, db) {
  // 1. Parse Excel
  let parsed;
  try {
    parsed = parseExcelFile(buffer, fileName);
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, error: e.message };
  }

  const { sheetName, headers, rows, detection } = parsed;
  const { type, colMapping } = detection;
  const batchId = generateBatchId(type, fileName);

  console.log(`[Ingest] File: ${fileName} | Type: ${type} | Sheet: ${sheetName} | Rows: ${rows.length}`);

  // ── PREPARE STATEMENTS (outside transaction for efficiency) ──────
  const batchStmt  = db.prepare(
    `INSERT INTO upload_batches (batch_id, type, filename, rows, date_from, date_to)
     VALUES (?, ?, ?, 0, NULL, NULL)`
  );
  const batchUpdate = db.prepare(
    `UPDATE upload_batches SET rows=?, date_from=?, date_to=? WHERE batch_id=?`
  );

  let dataStmt;
  let dupCheckStmt = null;
  if (type === 'audit_log') {
    dataStmt = db.prepare(`
      INSERT INTO audit_log (
        batch_id, proposal_no, partner_application_number, business_type, product_name,
        proposal_inward_date, first_payment_date, coming_from_bucket, coming_with_decision,
        current_bucket, current_bucket_date, current_bucket_time, no_of_days,
        proposal_level_status, proposal_level_status_norm, queue_start_date, queue_end_date
      ) VALUES (
        @batch_id, @proposal_no, @partner_application_number, @business_type, @product_name,
        @proposal_inward_date, @first_payment_date, @coming_from_bucket, @coming_with_decision,
        @current_bucket, @current_bucket_date, @current_bucket_time, @no_of_days,
        @proposal_level_status, @proposal_level_status_norm, @queue_start_date, @queue_end_date
      )
    `);
  } else {
    dataStmt = db.prepare(`
      INSERT INTO uw_productivity (
        batch_id, uw_name, proposal_no, action_date, product, business_type,
        refer_to_uw, accept, rejected, counter_offer, additional_info, additional_test,
        telemer, ppc, refer_to_cops, rulebook_refund, is_final, is_pending
      ) VALUES (
        @batch_id, @uw_name, @proposal_no, @action_date, @product, @business_type,
        @refer_to_uw, @accept, @rejected, @counter_offer, @additional_info, @additional_test,
        @telemer, @ppc, @refer_to_cops, @rulebook_refund, @is_final, @is_pending
      )
    `);
    // Dedup check: before inserting, see if an identical row already exists
    // (same UW, proposal, date, and all action columns) — catches re-uploads of same file
    dupCheckStmt = db.prepare(`
      SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM uw_productivity
      WHERE uw_name=@uw_name AND proposal_no=@proposal_no AND action_date=@action_date
        AND accept=@accept AND rejected=@rejected AND counter_offer=@counter_offer
        AND additional_info=@additional_info AND additional_test=@additional_test
        AND telemer=@telemer AND ppc=@ppc AND refer_to_cops=@refer_to_cops
        AND rulebook_refund=@rulebook_refund
    `);
  }

  // ── SINGLE ATOMIC TRANSACTION ─────────────────────────────────────
  // All three steps run in ONE transaction so there is never a moment
  // where the upload_batches row exists without its data rows, or where
  // data rows exist without their upload_batches parent (FK violation).
  let insertedCount = 0;
  let dateFrom = null, dateTo = null;

  try {
    const fullIngest = db.transaction(() => {

      // STEP 1 — Register batch FIRST (FK parent must exist before children)
      batchStmt.run(batchId, type, fileName);

      // STEP 2 — Insert all data rows (FK satisfied because parent now exists)
      if (type === 'audit_log') {
        rows.forEach(rawRow => {
          const mapped = mapAuditRow(rawRow, headers, colMapping, batchId);
          if (!mapped) return;
          if (mapped.proposal_inward_date) {
            if (!dateFrom || mapped.proposal_inward_date < dateFrom) dateFrom = mapped.proposal_inward_date;
            if (!dateTo   || mapped.proposal_inward_date > dateTo)   dateTo   = mapped.proposal_inward_date;
          }
          dataStmt.run(mapped);
          insertedCount++;
        });
      } else {
        rows.forEach(rawRow => {
          const mapped = mapUwRow(rawRow, headers, colMapping, batchId);
          if (!mapped) return;
          // Skip exact duplicate rows (same UW + proposal + date + all action cols)
          // Prevents double-counting when the same file is re-uploaded in Full History
          const dup = dupCheckStmt ? dupCheckStmt.get(mapped) : null;
          if (dup && dup.c > 0) return;
          if (mapped.action_date) {
            if (!dateFrom || mapped.action_date < dateFrom) dateFrom = mapped.action_date;
            if (!dateTo   || mapped.action_date > dateTo)   dateTo   = mapped.action_date;
          }
          dataStmt.run(mapped);
          insertedCount++;
        });
      }

      // STEP 3 — Update batch with final row count and date range
      batchUpdate.run(insertedCount, dateFrom, dateTo, batchId);
    });

    fullIngest(); // Execute — rolls back everything atomically on any error

    console.log(`[Ingest] ${type}: ${insertedCount} rows inserted (batch: ${batchId})`);
    return { success: true, batchId, type, rows: insertedCount };

  } catch (e) {
    // Transaction already rolled back automatically — no cleanup needed
    console.error('[Ingest] DB error:', e.message);
    return { success: false, error: `Database error: ${e.message}` };
  }
}

// ─── PROPOSAL STATUS LOGIC ───────────────────────────────────────
/**
 * For a set of UW rows for ONE proposal (sorted by action_date desc),
 * determines the current status (Clear/Pending) based on the latest action.
 * Applies priority: Clear > Pending, and within Clear: Accept > Rejected > Counter > Rulebook
 */
function resolveProposalStatus(uwRows) {
  if (!uwRows || uwRows.length === 0) return { status: 'unknown', action: null };

  // Get latest date
  const latestDate = uwRows[0].action_date;
  // All rows on the latest date
  const latestRows = uwRows.filter(r => r.action_date === latestDate);

  // Check for any Clear action on the latest date (Clear beats Pending)
  const clearPriority = ['accept', 'rejected', 'counter_offer', 'rulebook_refund'];
  for (const col of clearPriority) {
    if (latestRows.some(r => r[col] === 1)) {
      return { status: 'clear', action: col, date: latestDate };
    }
  }

  // Check for pending actions
  const pendingPriority = ['additional_info', 'additional_test', 'telemer', 'ppc', 'refer_to_cops', 'refer_to_uw'];
  for (const col of pendingPriority) {
    if (latestRows.some(r => r[col] === 1)) {
      return { status: 'pending', action: col, date: latestDate };
    }
  }

  return { status: 'unknown', action: null, date: latestDate };
}

/**
 * Returns label for a UW action column
 */
function actionLabel(col) {
  const map = {
    accept:          'Accept',
    rejected:        'Rejected',
    counter_offer:   'Counter Offer',
    rulebook_refund: 'Rulebook Refund',
    additional_info: 'Additional Info',
    additional_test: 'Additional Test',
    telemer:         'TeleMER/VideoMER',
    ppc:             'PPC Raised',
    refer_to_cops:   'Refer to COPs',
    refer_to_uw:     'Refer to UW'
  };
  return map[col] || col;
}

/**
 * Day category for display
 */
function dayCategory(days) {
  const d = Math.floor(Number(days) || 0);
  return d <= 5 ? String(d) : 'More than 5';
}

/**
 * SLA status based on configurable threshold
 */
function slaStatus(days, thresholdDays = 1) {
  return Number(days) <= thresholdDays ? 'Within SLA' : 'Breached';
}

/**
 * Calculate UW Queue TAT in days for a single proposal
 * Sums all UW_QUEUE queue_end - queue_start durations
 */
function calcUwQueueTat(auditRows) {
  let totalMs = 0;
  (auditRows || []).forEach(row => {
    if (row.current_bucket === 'UW_QUEUE' && row.queue_start_date && row.queue_end_date) {
      const start = new Date(row.queue_start_date);
      const end   = new Date(row.queue_end_date);
      if (!isNaN(start) && !isNaN(end) && end > start) {
        totalMs += (end - start);
      }
    }
  });
  return totalMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24); // Convert ms to days
}

module.exports = {
  ingestFile,
  detectFileType,
  parseExcelFile,
  resolveProposalStatus,
  actionLabel,
  dayCategory,
  slaStatus,
  calcUwQueueTat,
  normHeader
};

'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Query Context
 * Shared helper used by all tab IPC handlers to resolve
 * source filtering (Current Upload session vs Full History)
 */

/**
 * Builds SQL WHERE clause fragments for batch filtering.
 * source: 'current' | 'history'
 * session: the current upload session object
 * Returns { auditWhere, uwWhere, auditParams, uwParams, hasAudit, hasUw }
 */
function buildQueryContext(source, session) {
  const ctx = {
    hasAudit: true,
    hasUw:    true,
    auditWhere:  '',
    uwWhere:     '',
    auditParams: [],
    uwParams:    []
  };

  if (source === 'current') {
    if (!session || !session.batchIds || session.batchIds.length === 0) {
      ctx.hasAudit = false;
      ctx.hasUw    = false;
      return ctx;
    }
    ctx.hasAudit = session.hasAuditData || false;
    ctx.hasUw    = session.hasUwData    || false;

    if (session.auditBatchId) {
      ctx.auditWhere  = `batch_id = ?`;
      ctx.auditParams = [session.auditBatchId];
    } else if (session.batchIds.length > 0) {
      const ph = session.batchIds.map(() => '?').join(',');
      ctx.auditWhere  = `batch_id IN (${ph})`;
      ctx.auditParams = session.batchIds;
    }

    if (session.uwBatchId) {
      ctx.uwWhere  = `batch_id = ?`;
      ctx.uwParams = [session.uwBatchId];
    } else if (session.batchIds.length > 0) {
      const ph = session.batchIds.map(() => '?').join(',');
      ctx.uwWhere  = `batch_id IN (${ph})`;
      ctx.uwParams = session.batchIds;
    }
  }
  // For 'history': no batch filter, show everything

  return ctx;
}

/**
 * Appends audit log filter conditions from global filter object.
 * Mutates conditions[] and params[] passed in.
 */
function applyAuditFilters(filters, conditions, params, alias = 'al') {
  if (!filters) return;
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.business_type = ?`);
    params.push(filters.businessType);
  }
  if (filters.productName && filters.productName !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.product_name = ?`);
    params.push(filters.productName);
  }
  if (filters.status && filters.status !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_level_status_norm = ?`);
    params.push(filters.status);
  }
  if (filters.bucket && filters.bucket !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.current_bucket = ?`);
    params.push(filters.bucket);
  }
  if (filters.dateFrom) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_inward_date >= ?`);
    params.push(filters.dateFrom);
  }
  if (filters.dateTo) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.proposal_inward_date <= ?`);
    params.push(filters.dateTo + ' 23:59:59');
  }
}

/**
 * Appends UW productivity filter conditions.
 */
function applyUwFilters(filters, conditions, params, alias = 'uw') {
  if (!filters) return;
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.business_type = ?`);
    params.push(filters.businessType);
  }
  if (filters.productName && filters.productName !== 'all') {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.product = ?`);
    params.push(filters.productName);
  }
  if (filters.dateFrom) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.action_date >= ?`);
    params.push(filters.dateFrom);
  }
  if (filters.dateTo) {
    conditions.push(`${alias}.action_date <= ?`);
    params.push(filters.dateTo + ' 23:59:59');
  }
}

/**
 * Builds a complete WHERE clause string from conditions array.
 * Prepends batch condition if present.
 */
function buildWhere(batchCondition, batchParams, additionalConditions, additionalParams) {
  const all = [];
  const params = [];

  if (batchCondition) {
    all.push(`(${batchCondition})`);
    params.push(...batchParams);
  }
  if (additionalConditions && additionalConditions.length > 0) {
    all.push(...additionalConditions);
    params.push(...additionalParams);
  }

  return {
    where: all.length > 0 ? 'WHERE ' + all.join(' AND ') : '',
    params
  };
}

/**
 * Safe run wrapper - returns empty array on error
 */
function safeAll(db, sql, params = []) {
  try {
    return db.prepare(sql).all(...params);
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Query] Error:', e.message, '\nSQL:', sql.substring(0, 200));
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Safe get wrapper - returns null on error
 */
function safeGet(db, sql, params = []) {
  try {
    return db.prepare(sql).get(...params);
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('[Query] Error:', e.message, '\nSQL:', sql.substring(0, 200));
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Get SLA threshold from DB settings
 */
function getSlaThreshold(db) {
  try {
    const row = db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key = 'sla_threshold_days'").get();
    return parseInt(row ? row.value : '1', 10);
  } catch { return 1; }
}

/**
 * Day category helper (mirrors client-side utils.js)
 */
function dayCategory(days) {
  const d = Math.floor(Number(days) || 0);
  return d <= 5 ? String(d) : 'More than 5';
}

const DAY_CATS = ['0', '1', '2', '3', '4', '5', 'More than 5'];

module.exports = {
  buildQueryContext,
  applyAuditFilters,
  applyUwFilters,
  buildWhere,
  safeAll,
  safeGet,
  getSlaThreshold,
  dayCategory,
  DAY_CATS
};

'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - IPC Handler Registration Hub
 */

function register(ipcMain, context) {
  const { getDB, getSession, setSession, getMainWindow } = context;

  // ── UPLOAD ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/upload');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession, setSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] upload:', e.message); }

  // ── PIPELINE ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/pipeline');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] pipeline:', e.message); }

  // ── EXECUTIVE ────────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/executive');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] executive:', e.message); }

  // ── UW PRODUCTIVITY ──────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/uw');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] uw:', e.message); }

  // ── TAT / SLA ────────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/tat');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] tat:', e.message); }

  // ── DRILL-DOWN ───────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/drilldown');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] drilldown:', e.message); }

  // ── SETTINGS (PIN + DB stats) ────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/settings');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] settings:', e.message); }

  // ── EXPORT ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  try {
    const h = require('./handlers/export');
    h.register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('[IPC] export:', e.message); }

  // ── FILTERS ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('filters:get-options', async (event, source) => {
    try {
      const db = getDB(); const session = getSession();
      if (!db) return { businessTypes:[], products:[], statuses:[], buckets:[] };
      // Build WHERE clause correctly: batch filter AND not-null filter
      const batchCond = source==='current' && session && session.auditBatchId
        ? `batch_id='${session.auditBatchId.replace(/'/g,"''")}'`
        : null;
      const w = (extra) => batchCond
        ? `WHERE ${batchCond} AND ${extra}`
        : `WHERE ${extra}`;
      return {
        businessTypes: db.prepare(`SELECT DISTINCT business_type FROM audit_log ${w('business_type IS NOT NULL')} ORDER BY business_type`).all().map(r=>r.business_type),
        products:      db.prepare(`SELECT DISTINCT product_name FROM audit_log ${w('product_name IS NOT NULL')} ORDER BY product_name`).all().map(r=>r.product_name),
        statuses:      db.prepare(`SELECT DISTINCT proposal_level_status_norm FROM audit_log ${w('proposal_level_status_norm IS NOT NULL')} ORDER BY proposal_level_status_norm`).all().map(r=>r.proposal_level_status_norm),
        buckets:       db.prepare(`SELECT DISTINCT current_bucket FROM audit_log ${w('current_bucket IS NOT NULL')} ORDER BY current_bucket`).all().map(r=>r.current_bucket)
      };
    } catch(e) { return { businessTypes:[], products:[], statuses:[], buckets:[] }; }
  });

  // ── UPLOAD CLEAR SESSION ─────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('upload:clear-session', async () => {
    setSession(null); return { success: true };
  });

  // ── SETTINGS CRUD (simple get/save) ──────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('settings:get-all', async () => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {};
      return Object.fromEntries(db.prepare('SELECT key,value FROM app_settings').all().map(r=>[r.key,r.value]));
    } catch { return {}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:save', async (event, key, value) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {success:false};
      db.prepare('INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_settings (key,value) VALUES (?,?)').run(key,String(value));
      return {success:true};
    } catch(e) { return {success:false,error:e.message}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:save-multiple', async (event, obj) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {success:false};
      const stmt=db.prepare('INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_settings (key,value) VALUES (?,?)');
      const tx=db.transaction(()=>Object.entries(obj).forEach(([k,v])=>stmt.run(k,String(v))));
      tx(); return {success:true};
    } catch(e) { return {success:false,error:e.message}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:get-upload-history', async () => {
    try { const db=getDB(); if (!db) return []; return db.prepare('SELECT * FROM upload_batches ORDER BY uploaded_at DESC').all(); }
    catch { return []; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:delete-batch', async (event, batchId) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {success:false};
      // Delete child rows first — sql.js ON DELETE CASCADE is not guaranteed
      const tx = db.transaction(() => {
        db.prepare('DELETE FROM audit_log WHERE batch_id=?').run(batchId);
        db.prepare('DELETE FROM uw_productivity WHERE batch_id=?').run(batchId);
        db.prepare('DELETE FROM upload_batches WHERE batch_id=?').run(batchId);
      });
      tx();
      return {success:true};
    } catch(e) { return {success:false,error:e.message}; }
  });

  console.log('[IPC] All handlers registered successfully');
}

module.exports = { register };

'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Upload IPC Handlers
 */

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession, setSession) {

  ipcMain.handle('upload:process-files', async (event, payload) => {
    const { fileName, data, mode } = payload;
    try {
      const db = getDB();
      if (!db) return { success: false, error: 'Database not initialised.' };

      const ingest = require('../../database/ingest');
      const buffer = Buffer.from(data);
      const result = ingest.ingestFile(buffer, fileName, db);
      if (!result.success) return result;

      const session = getSession() || { batchIds: [], hasAuditData: false, hasUwData: false };
      session.batchIds = session.batchIds || [];
      session.batchIds.push(result.batchId);

      if (result.type === 'audit_log') {
        session.auditBatchId = result.batchId;
        session.hasAuditData = true;
      } else {
        session.uwBatchId  = result.batchId;
        session.hasUwData  = true;
      }
      session.lastUploadAt = new Date().toISOString();
      setSession(session);

      return { success: true, batchId: result.batchId, type: result.type, rows: result.rows, fileName };
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('[Upload] Error:', e.message);
      return { success: false, error: e.message };
    }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('upload:get-session-stats', async (event, filters) => {
    try {
      const db      = getDB();
      const session = getSession();
      if (!db || !session || !session.batchIds || session.batchIds.length === 0) {
        return { hasData: false };
      }
      const ph = session.batchIds.map(() => '?').join(',');
      const auditCount = session.hasAuditData
        ? db.prepare(`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log WHERE batch_id IN (${ph})`).get(...session.batchIds)
        : { cnt: 0 };
      const uwCount = session.hasUwData
        ? db.prepare(`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM uw_productivity WHERE batch_id IN (${ph})`).get(...session.batchIds)
        : { cnt: 0 };
      return {
        hasData: true,
        hasAuditData: session.hasAuditData,
        hasUwData: session.hasUwData,
        auditProposals: auditCount.cnt,
        uwProposals: uwCount.cnt,
        batchIds: session.batchIds,
        lastUploadAt: session.lastUploadAt
      };
    } catch (e) {
      return { hasData: false, error: e.message };
    }
  });
}

module.exports = { register };
