FILE: ipc/handlers/executive.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { buildQueryContext, safeAll, safeGet } = require('../../database/query');

// Build condition arrays - safe WHERE construction
function buildAudit(ctx, filters) {
  const c=[], p=[];
  if (ctx.auditWhere) { c.push(ctx.auditWhere); p.push(...ctx.auditParams); }
  if (!filters) return {c,p};
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType!=='all') { c.push('business_type=?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName !=='all') { c.push('product_name=?');  p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.status && filters.status!=='all') { c.push('proposal_level_status_norm=?'); p.push(filters.status); }
  if (filters.bucket && filters.bucket!=='all') { c.push('current_bucket=?'); p.push(filters.bucket); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('proposal_inward_date>=?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('proposal_inward_date<=?'); p.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
  return {c,p};
}
function buildUw(ctx, filters) {
  const c=[], p=[];
  if (ctx.uwWhere) { c.push(ctx.uwWhere); p.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
  if (!filters) return {c,p};
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType!=='all') { c.push('business_type=?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName !=='all') { c.push('product=?');       p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('action_date>=?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('action_date<=?'); p.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
  return {c,p};
}

// Always-safe WHERE builder: pass extra conditions to append
function where(base_c, ...extra) {
  const all = [...base_c, ...extra.filter(Boolean)];
  return all.length ? 'WHERE '+all.join(' AND ') : '';
}
function g(db,sql,p) { return safeGet(db,sql,p||[]); }
function q(db,sql,p) { return safeAll(db,sql,p||[]); }

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {
  ipcMain.handle('executive:get-stats', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db = getDB(); if (!db) return { error:'DB not ready' };
      const ctx = buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const a = buildAudit(ctx, filters);
      const u = buildUw(ctx, filters);
      const aw = where(a.c), uw = where(u.c);

      // SLA threshold
      const sla = parseInt(((g(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'")||{}).value||'1'),10);

      // Proposal counts
      const auditCnt = ctx.hasAudit ? (g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM audit_log ${aw}`,a.p)||{c:0}).c : 0;
      const uwCnt    = ctx.hasUw    ? (g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${uw}`,u.p)||{c:0}).c : 0;

      // Total unique proposals: use UNION to deduplicate across both tables.
      // The old inclusion-exclusion (A + B - A∩B) produced negative numbers when
      // filters like productName were missing from the intersection query.
      // UNION is simpler and always correct — each side uses its own filter columns
      // (audit: product_name / uw: product), so every filter is applied correctly.
      let totalProposals = auditCnt;
      if (ctx.hasAudit && ctx.hasUw) {
        const unionCnt = g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM (SELECT proposal_no FROM audit_log ${aw} UNION SELECT proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${uw})`,[...a.p,...u.p]);
        totalProposals = (unionCnt||{c:0}).c;
      } else if (!ctx.hasAudit && ctx.hasUw) {
        totalProposals = uwCnt;
      }

      // Journey TAT (worst no_of_days per proposal)
      let journeyBreaches=0, journeyCompliance=0;
      if (ctx.hasAudit) {
        const jr = g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as tot, SUM(CASE WHEN max_days<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws, SUM(CASE WHEN max_days>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no, MAX(no_of_days) as max_days FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no)`,a.p);
        if (jr) { journeyBreaches=jr.br||0; journeyCompliance=jr.tot>0?Math.round(jr.ws/jr.tot*1000)/10:0; }
      }

      // UW Queue TAT (sum per proposal of queue_end - queue_start where bucket=UW_QUEUE)
      let uwQueueBreaches=0, uwQueueCompliance=0;
      if (ctx.hasAudit) {
        const qw = where(a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL');
        const qp = [...a.p,'UW_QUEUE'];
        const qr = g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as tot, SUM(CASE WHEN uw_tat<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws, SUM(CASE WHEN uw_tat>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no, SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as uw_tat FROM audit_log ${qw} GROUP BY proposal_no)`,qp);
        if (qr) { uwQueueBreaches=qr.br||0; uwQueueCompliance=qr.tot>0?Math.round(qr.ws/qr.tot*1000)/10:0; }
      }

      // Accept Rate
      let teamAcceptRate=0;
      if (ctx.hasUw) {
        const aw2=where(u.c,'accept=1'), co2=where(u.c,'counter_offer=1');
        const ap=(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${aw2}`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
        const cp=(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${co2}`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
        const clrW = where(u.c);
        const clr=(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(is_final) as mf FROM uw_productivity ${clrW} GROUP BY proposal_no HAVING MAX(is_final)=1)`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
        teamAcceptRate=clr>0?Math.round((ap+cp)/clr*1000)/10:0;
      }

      // Pending Cases
      let pendingCases=0;
      if (ctx.hasUw) {
        const latestWhere = where(u.c); // for inner subquery
        const outerConds  = u.c.map(c=>'p.'+c);
        const outerWhere  = outerConds.length ? 'WHERE '+outerConds.join(' AND ') : '';
        const pr=g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM (SELECT p.proposal_no,MAX(p.is_final) as mf FROM uw_productivity p INNER JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(action_date) as md FROM uw_productivity ${latestWhere} GROUP BY proposal_no) ld ON p.proposal_no=ld.proposal_no AND p.action_date=ld.md ${outerWhere} GROUP BY p.proposal_no HAVING MAX(p.is_final)=0)`,[...u.p,...u.p]);
        pendingCases=(pr||{c:0}).c;
      }

      // Daily UW Output
      const dailyOutput = ctx.hasUw
        ? q(db,`SELECT action_date as date, COUNT(*) as actions FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY action_date ORDER BY action_date`,u.p).filter(r=>r.date)
        : [];

      // Action Type Mix
      let actionMix={};
      if (ctx.hasUw) {
        const mx=g(db,`SELECT SUM(accept) as accept,SUM(rejected) as rejected,SUM(counter_offer) as counter_offer,SUM(additional_info) as additional_info,SUM(additional_test) as additional_test,SUM(telemer) as telemer,SUM(ppc) as ppc,SUM(refer_to_cops) as refer_to_cops,SUM(rulebook_refund) as rulebook_refund FROM uw_productivity ${uw}`,u.p);
        actionMix=mx||{};
      }

      // Monthly data
      let monthlyData=[];
      if (ctx.hasAudit||ctx.hasUw) {
        const amW=where(a.c,'proposal_inward_date IS NOT NULL');
        const amRows=ctx.hasAudit?q(db,`SELECT strftime('%Y-%m',proposal_inward_date) as month,COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as proposals FROM audit_log ${amW} GROUP BY month ORDER BY month`,a.p):[];
        const umW=where(u.c,'action_date IS NOT NULL');
        const umRows=ctx.hasUw?q(db,`SELECT strftime('%Y-%m',action_date) as month,COUNT(*) as actioned FROM uw_productivity ${umW} GROUP BY month ORDER BY month`,u.p):[];
        const jmW=where(a.c,'proposal_inward_date IS NOT NULL');
        const jmRows=ctx.hasAudit?q(db,`SELECT month,COUNT(*) as tot,SUM(CASE WHEN md<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws,SUM(CASE WHEN md>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(no_of_days) as md,strftime('%Y-%m',MIN(proposal_inward_date)) as month FROM audit_log ${jmW} GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY month ORDER BY month`,a.p):[];
        const qmW=where(a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL');
        const qmRows=ctx.hasAudit?q(db,`SELECT month,COUNT(*) as tot,SUM(CASE WHEN ut<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws,SUM(CASE WHEN ut>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as ut,strftime('%Y-%m',MIN(queue_start_date)) as month FROM audit_log ${qmW} GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY month ORDER BY month`,[...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']):[];
        const months=[...new Set([...amRows.map(r=>r.month),...umRows.map(r=>r.month)])].filter(Boolean).sort();
        monthlyData=months.map(m=>{
          const am=amRows.find(r=>r.month===m)||{proposals:0};
          const um=umRows.find(r=>r.month===m)||{actioned:0};
          const jm=jmRows.find(r=>r.month===m)||{br:0,ws:0,tot:0};
          const qm=qmRows.find(r=>r.month===m)||{br:0,ws:0,tot:0};
          return {month:m,proposals:am.proposals,uwActioned:um.actioned,journeyBreaches:jm.br||0,journeyCompliancePct:jm.tot>0?Math.round(jm.ws/jm.tot*1000)/10:0,uwQueueBreaches:qm.br||0,uwQueueCompliancePct:qm.tot>0?Math.round(qm.ws/qm.tot*1000)/10:0};
        });
      }

      const dr=ctx.hasAudit?(g(db,`SELECT MIN(proposal_inward_date) as f,MAX(proposal_inward_date) as t FROM audit_log ${aw}`,a.p)||{}): {};
      return { kpi:{totalProposals,journeyBreaches,journeyCompliance,uwQueueBreaches,uwQueueCompliance,teamAcceptRate,pendingCases}, charts:{dailyOutput,actionMix,monthlyData}, datePeriod:{from:dr.f,to:dr.t}, hasAudit:ctx.hasAudit&&auditCnt>0, hasUw:ctx.hasUw&&uwCnt>0, slaThreshold:sla };
    } catch(e) { console.error('[Executive]',e.message,e.stack); return { error:e.message }; }
  });
}
module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/pipeline.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { buildQueryContext, safeAll, safeGet } = require('../../database/query');

// Build audit filter WHERE clause and params array
function auditFilters(ctx, filters) {
  const c = [], p = [];
  if (ctx.auditWhere) { c.push(ctx.auditWhere); p.push(...ctx.auditParams); }
  if (!filters) return { c, p };
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') { c.push('business_type = ?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName  !== 'all') { c.push('product_name = ?');  p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.status && filters.status !== 'all') { c.push('proposal_level_status_norm = ?'); p.push(filters.status); }
  if (filters.bucket && filters.bucket !== 'all') { c.push('current_bucket = ?'); p.push(filters.bucket); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('proposal_inward_date >= ?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('proposal_inward_date <= ?'); p.push(filters.dateTo + ' 23:59:59'); }
  return { c, p };
}

function uwFilters(ctx, filters) {
  const c = [], p = [];
  if (ctx.uwWhere) { c.push(ctx.uwWhere); p.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
  if (!filters) return { c, p };
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') { c.push('business_type = ?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName  !== 'all') { c.push('product = ?');       p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('action_date >= ?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('action_date <= ?'); p.push(filters.dateTo + ' 23:59:59'); }
  return { c, p };
}

function q(db, sql, params) { return safeAll(db, sql, params || []); }
function g(db, sql, params) { return safeGet(db, sql, params || []); }
function w(conds) { return conds.length ? 'WHERE ' + conds.join(' AND ') : ''; }
function wa(conds) { return conds.length ? 'AND ' + conds.join(' AND ') : ''; }

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {
  ipcMain.handle('pipeline:get-stats', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db = getDB(); if (!db) return { error: 'DB not ready' };
      const ctx = buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const af = auditFilters(ctx, filters);
      const uf = uwFilters(ctx, filters);
      const aw = w(af.c), uw2 = w(uf.c);

      // KPI counts
      const auditCnt = ctx.hasAudit ? (g(db, `SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM audit_log ${aw}`, af.p)||{c:0}).c : 0;
      const uwCnt    = ctx.hasUw    ? (g(db, `SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${uw2}`, uf.p)||{c:0}).c : 0;

      let totalProposals=0, fullyTracked=0, auditPending=0, uwActionPending=0;

      if (ctx.hasAudit && ctx.hasUw) {
        // Intersection using JOIN with separate batch filters
        const ic = [], ip = [];
        if (ctx.auditWhere) { ic.push('al.' + ctx.auditWhere); ip.push(...ctx.auditParams); }
        if (ctx.uwWhere)    { ic.push('uw.' + ctx.uwWhere);    ip.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
        if (filters && filters.businessType && filters.businessType !== 'all') { ic.push('al.business_type = ?'); ip.push(filters.businessType); }
        if (filters && filters.dateFrom) { ic.push('al.proposal_inward_date >= ?'); ip.push(filters.dateFrom); }
        if (filters && filters.dateTo)   { ic.push('al.proposal_inward_date <= ?'); ip.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
        const iw = ic.length ? 'WHERE ' + ic.join(' AND ') : '';
        const inter = (g(db, `SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT al.proposal_no) as c FROM audit_log al INNER JOIN uw_productivity uw ON al.proposal_no = uw.proposal_no ${iw}`, ip)||{c:0}).c;
        fullyTracked = inter;
        auditPending = Math.max(0, uwCnt - inter);
        uwActionPending = Math.max(0, auditCnt - inter);
        totalProposals = auditCnt + uwCnt - inter;
      } else if (ctx.hasAudit) {
        totalProposals = auditCnt; uwActionPending = auditCnt;
      } else if (ctx.hasUw) {
        totalProposals = uwCnt; auditPending = uwCnt;
      }

      // Chart queries - all from audit_log
      const and = af.c.length ? wa(af.c) : '';

      const bizTypeData       = ctx.hasAudit ? q(db, `SELECT business_type, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${and ? (aw?and:'WHERE '+and.replace('AND ','')) : ''} GROUP BY business_type ORDER BY cnt DESC`, af.p).filter(r=>r.business_type) : [];
      // Simpler: just rebuild each query cleanly
      const [btd, fbd, cbd, sd, dtd, pd, dr] = ctx.hasAudit ? [
        q(db, `SELECT business_type, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY business_type HAVING business_type IS NOT NULL ORDER BY cnt DESC`, af.p),
        q(db, `SELECT coming_from_bucket as bucket, COUNT(*) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${aw?'AND':'WHERE'} coming_from_bucket IS NOT NULL GROUP BY coming_from_bucket ORDER BY cnt DESC`, af.p),
        q(db, `SELECT current_bucket as bucket, COUNT(*) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${aw?'AND':'WHERE'} current_bucket IS NOT NULL GROUP BY current_bucket ORDER BY cnt DESC`, af.p),
        q(db, `SELECT proposal_level_status_norm as status, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${aw?'AND':'WHERE'} proposal_level_status_norm IS NOT NULL GROUP BY proposal_level_status_norm ORDER BY cnt DESC`, af.p),
        q(db, `SELECT DATE(proposal_inward_date) as date, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${aw?'AND':'WHERE'} proposal_inward_date IS NOT NULL GROUP BY DATE(proposal_inward_date) ORDER BY date`, af.p),
        q(db, `SELECT product_name, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM audit_log ${aw} ${aw?'AND':'WHERE'} product_name IS NOT NULL GROUP BY product_name ORDER BY cnt DESC LIMIT 10`, af.p),
        g(db, `SELECT MIN(proposal_inward_date) as minDate, MAX(proposal_inward_date) as maxDate FROM audit_log ${aw}`, af.p)
      ] : [[],[],[],[],[],[],{}];

      return {
        kpi: { totalProposals, fullyTracked, auditPending, uwActionPending },
        hasAudit: ctx.hasAudit && auditCnt > 0,
        hasUw:    ctx.hasUw    && uwCnt    > 0,
        charts: { bizTypeData: btd.filter(r=>r.business_type), fromBucketData: fbd, currentBucketData: cbd, statusData: sd, dailyTrendData: dtd.filter(r=>r.date), productData: pd.filter(r=>r.product_name) },
        dateRange: { from: (dr||{}).minDate, to: (dr||{}).maxDate }
      };
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[Pipeline]', e.message);
      return { error: e.message };
    }
  });
}

module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/uw.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { buildQueryContext, safeAll, safeGet } = require('../../database/query');

function buildUw(ctx, filters) {
  const c=[], p=[];
  if (ctx.uwWhere) { c.push(ctx.uwWhere); p.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
  if (!filters) return {c,p};
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType!=='all') { c.push('business_type=?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName !=='all') { c.push('product=?');       p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('action_date>=?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('action_date<=?'); p.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
  return {c,p};
}

const w  = c => c.length ? 'WHERE '+c.join(' AND ') : '';
const g  = (db,sql,p) => safeGet(db,sql,p||[]);
const q  = (db,sql,p) => safeAll(db,sql,p||[]);

// ── PENDING/CLEAR DETECTION ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
// IMPORTANT: We deliberately compute the final-decision flag from the RAW ACTION
// COLUMNS (accept, rejected, counter_offer, rulebook_refund) rather than the
// stored is_final column. This makes every query correct regardless of whether
// is_final was stored correctly during ingestion (older versions had edge cases).
const FINAL_EXPR = `(CASE WHEN accept=1 OR rejected=1 OR counter_offer=1 OR rulebook_refund=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)`;

// CTE: proposal_no list of proposals with no final decision yet
function pendingCTE(uw) {
  return `(SELECT proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${w(uw.c)} GROUP BY proposal_no HAVING MAX(${FINAL_EXPR})=0)`;
}

// CTE: proposal_no list of proposals that have received a final decision
function clearCTE(uw) {
  return `(SELECT proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${w(uw.c)} GROUP BY proposal_no HAVING MAX(${FINAL_EXPR})=1)`;
}

// Per-UW clear/pending counts — single CTE pass instead of two full table scans + LEFT JOIN
function perUwClearPendingSQL(uw) {
  const baseWhere = w(uw.c);
  // Step 1: per-proposal has_final flag (one scan)
  // Step 2: join back to uw_productivity for uw_name (one scan)
  // vs old approach: two separate subquery scans + LEFT JOIN
  return `
    WITH proposal_status AS (
      SELECT proposal_no,
        MAX(CASE WHEN accept=1 OR rejected=1 OR counter_offer=1 OR rulebook_refund=1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as has_final
      FROM uw_productivity ${baseWhere}
      GROUP BY proposal_no
    )
    SELECT up.uw_name,
      COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN ps.has_final=1 THEN up.proposal_no END) as clear_c,
      COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN ps.has_final=0 THEN up.proposal_no END) as pending_c
    FROM (SELECT DISTINCT uw_name, proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${baseWhere}) up
    JOIN proposal_status ps ON up.proposal_no = ps.proposal_no
    GROUP BY up.uw_name`;
}

// ── PENDING PROPOSAL ROWS (shared between stats and paginated list) ────────────
const PENDING_SELECT = (uw, extra='') => `
  SELECT p.proposal_no, MIN(p.uw_name) as uw_name, MIN(p.business_type) as business_type,
         MIN(p.action_date) as in_queue_since
  FROM uw_productivity p
  ${w(uw.c)}
  GROUP BY p.proposal_no
  HAVING MAX(${FINAL_EXPR})=0
  ORDER BY in_queue_since ASC ${extra}`;

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {

  // ── MAIN STATS (KPI + summary table + chart data) ────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-stats', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {error:'DB not ready'};
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx, filters);
      const uw=w(u.c);
      if (!ctx.hasUw) return {hasUw:false, kpi:{}, summaryRows:[], uwNames:[], pendingTotal:0};

      // ── KPI ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const totalActioned=(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} (is_final=1 OR is_pending=1)`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      const pendingTeam  =(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM ${pendingCTE(u)}`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      const clearTeam    =(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM ${clearCTE(u)}`,  u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      const acceptP =(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} accept=1`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      const coP     =(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as c FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} counter_offer=1`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      const acceptRate = clearTeam>0 ? Math.round((acceptP+coP)/clearTeam*1000)/10 : 0;

      // ── UW SUMMARY TABLE ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const actionTotals = q(db,`
        SELECT uw_name, COUNT(*) as total_actions, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as unique_proposals,
          SUM(accept) as accept, SUM(rejected) as rejected, SUM(counter_offer) as counter_offer,
          SUM(additional_info) as additional_info, SUM(additional_test) as additional_test,
          SUM(telemer) as telemer, SUM(ppc) as ppc, SUM(refer_to_cops) as refer_to_cops,
          SUM(rulebook_refund) as rulebook_refund
        FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY uw_name`,u.p);

      const clearPendingRows = q(db, perUwClearPendingSQL(u), [...u.p, ...u.p]);
      const cpMap = Object.fromEntries(clearPendingRows.map(r=>[r.uw_name,r]));

      const acceptPerUw = q(db,`
        SELECT uw_name,
          COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN accept=1 THEN proposal_no END) as ap,
          COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN counter_offer=1 THEN proposal_no END) as cop
        FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY uw_name`,u.p);
      const apMap = Object.fromEntries(acceptPerUw.map(r=>[r.uw_name,r]));

      const pendingThreshold = parseInt(((g(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='pending_rate_warning_pct'")||{}).value||'10'),10);

      const summaryRows = actionTotals.map(row => {
        const cp = cpMap[row.uw_name]||{clear_c:0,pending_c:0};
        const ap = apMap[row.uw_name]||{ap:0,cop:0};
        const clear   = cp.clear_c||0;
        const pending = cp.pending_c||0;
        const unique  = row.unique_proposals;
        const pendingRate = unique>0 ? Math.round(pending/unique*1000)/10 : 0;
        const uwAcceptRate= clear>0  ? Math.round((ap.ap+ap.cop)/clear*1000)/10 : 0;
        return { uw_name:row.uw_name, total_actions:row.total_actions, unique_proposals:unique,
          clear, pending, pending_rate:pendingRate, accept:row.accept, rejected:row.rejected,
          counter_offer:row.counter_offer, additional_info:row.additional_info,
          additional_test:row.additional_test, telemer:row.telemer, ppc:row.ppc,
          refer_to_cops:row.refer_to_cops, rulebook_refund:row.rulebook_refund,
          accept_rate:uwAcceptRate };
      });

      const mostActive = [...summaryRows].sort((a,b)=>b.total_actions-a.total_actions)[0]||{};
      summaryRows.sort((a,b)=>b.total_actions-a.total_actions);

      // ── ACCEPT RATE CHART ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const acceptRateChart = summaryRows
        .filter(r=>r.clear>0)
        .map(r=>({uw_name:r.uw_name,accept_rate:r.accept_rate,clear:r.clear}))
        .sort((a,b)=>a.accept_rate-b.accept_rate);

      // ── ACTION TYPE MIX ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const mx=g(db,`SELECT SUM(accept) as accept,SUM(rejected) as rejected,SUM(counter_offer) as counter_offer,SUM(additional_info) as additional_info,SUM(additional_test) as additional_test,SUM(telemer) as telemer,SUM(ppc) as ppc,SUM(refer_to_cops) as refer_to_cops,SUM(rulebook_refund) as rulebook_refund FROM uw_productivity ${uw}`,u.p)||{};

      // ── BUSINESS TYPE ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const bizByUw = q(db,`SELECT uw_name, business_type, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} business_type IS NOT NULL GROUP BY uw_name,business_type ORDER BY uw_name,cnt DESC`,u.p);

      // ── DAILY OUTPUT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      const dailyAll = q(db,`SELECT action_date as date, COUNT(*) as actions, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as proposals FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} action_date IS NOT NULL GROUP BY action_date ORDER BY date`,u.p);

      // ── PENDING PROPOSALS (first page) ────────────────────────────────────
      const pendingProposals = q(db, PENDING_SELECT(u, 'LIMIT 10'), u.p);
      const uwNames = [...new Set(summaryRows.map(r=>r.uw_name))].sort();

      return { hasUw:true,
        kpi:{totalActioned,pendingTeam,clearTeam,acceptRate,mostActive:{name:mostActive.uw_name||'', actions:mostActive.total_actions||0, acceptRate:mostActive.accept_rate||0}},
        summaryRows, acceptRateChart, actionMix:mx, bizByUw, dailyAll, pendingProposals,
        pendingTotal:pendingTeam, pendingThreshold, uwNames };
    } catch(e) { console.error('[UW:stats]',e.message,e.stack); return {error:e.message}; }
  });

  // ── PER-UW DRILLDOWNS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-action-type-mix', async (event, source, filters, uwName) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const extra = uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.c,'uw_name=?'] : u.c;
      const extraP= uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.p,uwName] : u.p;
      const uw=w(extra);
      return safeGet(db,`SELECT SUM(accept) as accept,SUM(rejected) as rejected,SUM(counter_offer) as counter_offer,SUM(additional_info) as additional_info,SUM(additional_test) as additional_test,SUM(telemer) as telemer,SUM(ppc) as ppc,SUM(refer_to_cops) as refer_to_cops,SUM(rulebook_refund) as rulebook_refund FROM uw_productivity ${uw}`,extraP)||{};
    } catch(e) { return {}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-business-type-mix', async (event, source, filters, uwName) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const extra = uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.c,'uw_name=?'] : u.c;
      const extraP= uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.p,uwName] : u.p;
      const uw=w(extra);
      const rows=safeAll(db,`SELECT uw_name, business_type, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as cnt FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} business_type IS NOT NULL GROUP BY uw_name,business_type ORDER BY uw_name,cnt DESC`,extraP);
      return {rows, isAll: !uwName||uwName==='ALL'};
    } catch(e) { return {rows:[],isAll:true}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-daily-output', async (event, source, filters, uwName) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const extra = uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.c,'uw_name=?'] : u.c;
      const extraP= uwName && uwName!=='ALL' ? [...u.p,uwName] : u.p;
      const uw=w(extra);
      const rows=safeAll(db,`SELECT action_date as date, COUNT(*) as actions, COUNT(DISTINCT proposal_no) as proposals FROM uw_productivity ${uw} ${uw?'AND':'WHERE'} action_date IS NOT NULL GROUP BY action_date ORDER BY date`,extraP);
      let teamAvg=null;
      if (uwName && uwName!=='ALL') {
        const tw=w(u.c);
        const teamRows=safeAll(db,`SELECT action_date as date, COUNT(*) as actions FROM uw_productivity ${tw} ${tw?'AND':'WHERE'} action_date IS NOT NULL GROUP BY action_date ORDER BY date`,u.p);
        if (teamRows.length) teamAvg=Math.round(teamRows.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.actions,0)/teamRows.length);
      }
      return {rows, teamAvg};
    } catch(e) { return {rows:[],teamAvg:null}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-pending-proposals', async (event, source, filters, page) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const perPage=10, offset=((page||1)-1)*perPage;
      const rows=q(db, PENDING_SELECT(u, `LIMIT ${perPage} OFFSET ${offset}`), u.p);
      const total=(g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM ${pendingCTE(u)}`,u.p)||{c:0}).c;
      return {rows, total, page:page||1, totalPages:Math.ceil(total/perPage), perPage};
    } catch(e) { return {rows:[],total:0,page:1,totalPages:1,perPage:10}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:export-pending', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      return q(db, PENDING_SELECT(u), u.p);
    } catch(e) { return []; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-accept-rate-chart', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const uw=w(u.c);
      const clearPending=safeAll(db, perUwClearPendingSQL(u), [...u.p, ...u.p]);
      const acceptD=safeAll(db,`SELECT uw_name,COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN accept=1 THEN proposal_no END) as ap,COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN counter_offer=1 THEN proposal_no END) as cop FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY uw_name`,u.p);
      const aMap=Object.fromEntries(acceptD.map(r=>[r.uw_name,r]));
      return clearPending.filter(r=>(r.clear_c||0)>0).map(r=>{
        const a=aMap[r.uw_name]||{ap:0,cop:0};
        return {uw_name:r.uw_name,accept_rate:Math.round((a.ap+a.cop)/(r.clear_c||1)*1000)/10,clear:r.clear_c};
      }).sort((a,b)=>a.accept_rate-b.accept_rate);
    } catch(e) { return []; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('uw:get-summary-table', async () => safeGet(getDB(),'SELECT 1',[]));
}

module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/tat.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { buildQueryContext, safeAll, safeGet } = require('../../database/query');

function buildAudit(ctx, filters) {
  const c=[], p=[];
  if (ctx.auditWhere) { c.push(ctx.auditWhere); p.push(...ctx.auditParams); }
  if (!filters) return {c,p};
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType!=='all') { c.push('business_type=?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.productName  && filters.productName !=='all') { c.push('product_name=?');  p.push(filters.productName); }
  if (filters.status && filters.status!=='all') { c.push('proposal_level_status_norm=?'); p.push(filters.status); }
  if (filters.bucket && filters.bucket!=='all') { c.push('current_bucket=?'); p.push(filters.bucket); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('proposal_inward_date>=?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('proposal_inward_date<=?'); p.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
  return {c,p};
}
function buildUw(ctx, filters) {
  const c=[], p=[];
  if (ctx.uwWhere) { c.push(ctx.uwWhere); p.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
  if (!filters) return {c,p};
  if (filters.businessType && filters.businessType!=='all') { c.push('business_type=?'); p.push(filters.businessType); }
  if (filters.dateFrom) { c.push('action_date>=?'); p.push(filters.dateFrom); }
  if (filters.dateTo)   { c.push('action_date<=?'); p.push(filters.dateTo+' 23:59:59'); }
  return {c,p};
}
const w = c => c.length ? 'WHERE '+c.join(' AND ') : '';
const g = (db,sql,p) => safeGet(db,sql,p||[]);
const q = (db,sql,p) => safeAll(db,sql,p||[]);

const DAY_ORDER = "CASE day_cat WHEN '0' THEN 0 WHEN '1' THEN 1 WHEN '2' THEN 2 WHEN '3' THEN 3 WHEN '4' THEN 4 WHEN '5' THEN 5 ELSE 6 END";
const DAY_CAT_SQL = "CASE WHEN CAST(v AS INTEGER)<=5 THEN CAST(CAST(v AS INTEGER) AS TEXT) ELSE 'More than 5' END";

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {

  ipcMain.handle('tat:get-stats', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {error:'DB not ready'};
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const a=buildAudit(ctx,filters);
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const aw=w(a.c), uw=w(u.c);
      if (!ctx.hasAudit) return {hasAudit:false,hasUw:ctx.hasUw};

      const slaRow=g(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'");
      const sla=parseInt((slaRow||{}).value||'1',10);

      // ── JOURNEY TAT ──────────────────────────────────────
      const jRow=g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as tot, SUM(CASE WHEN md<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws, SUM(CASE WHEN md>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(no_of_days) as md FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no)`,a.p);
      const journeyBreaches=jRow?jRow.br||0:0, journeyCompliance=jRow&&jRow.tot>0?Math.round(jRow.ws/jRow.tot*1000)/10:0;

      // ── UW QUEUE TAT ─────────────────────────────────────
      const qw=w([...a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL']);
      const qRow=g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as tot, SUM(CASE WHEN ut<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as ws, SUM(CASE WHEN ut>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as br FROM (SELECT proposal_no,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as ut FROM audit_log ${qw} GROUP BY proposal_no)`,[...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']);
      const uwQueueBreaches=qRow?qRow.br||0:0, uwQueueCompliance=qRow&&qRow.tot>0?Math.round(qRow.ws/qRow.tot*1000)/10:0;

      // ── UNATTRIBUTED ──────────────────────────────────────
      let unattributed=0;
      if (ctx.hasUw) {
        const ic=[],ip=[];
        if (ctx.auditWhere) { ic.push('al.'+ctx.auditWhere); ip.push(...ctx.auditParams); }
        if (ctx.uwWhere)    { ic.push('uw.'+ctx.uwWhere);    ip.push(...ctx.uwParams); }
        ic.push("al.current_bucket='UW_QUEUE'");
        const uiw=ic.length?'WHERE '+ic.join(' AND '):'WHERE al.current_bucket=\'UW_QUEUE\'';
        const r=g(db,`SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT al.proposal_no) as c FROM audit_log al ${uiw} AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM uw_productivity uw WHERE uw.proposal_no=al.proposal_no ${ctx.uwWhere?'AND uw.'+ctx.uwWhere:''})`,ip.length?ip:[...ip]);
        unattributed=(r||{c:0}).c;
      }

      // ── JOURNEY TAT MATRIX ───────────────────────────────
      const jMatrix=q(db,`SELECT business_type, CASE WHEN CAST(md AS INTEGER)<=5 THEN CAST(CAST(md AS INTEGER) AS TEXT) ELSE 'More than 5' END as day_cat, COUNT(*) as cnt FROM (SELECT proposal_no,business_type,MAX(no_of_days) as md FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY business_type,day_cat ORDER BY business_type,${DAY_ORDER}`.replace('${DAY_ORDER}',DAY_ORDER),a.p).filter(r=>r.business_type);

      // ── UW QUEUE TAT MATRIX ──────────────────────────────
      const qmw=w([...a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL']);
      const uwMatrix=q(db,`SELECT business_type, CASE WHEN CAST(ut AS INTEGER)<=5 THEN CAST(CAST(ut AS INTEGER) AS TEXT) ELSE 'More than 5' END as day_cat, COUNT(*) as cnt FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MIN(business_type) as business_type,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as ut FROM audit_log ${qmw} GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY business_type,day_cat ORDER BY business_type`,[...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']).filter(r=>r.business_type);

      // ── SLA COMPLIANCE TREND ─────────────────────────────
      const dateW=w([...a.c,'proposal_inward_date IS NOT NULL']);
      const jTrend=q(db,`SELECT date,SUM(within_sla) as ws,COUNT(*) as tot FROM (SELECT DATE(MIN(pid)) as date,CASE WHEN MAX(md)<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END as within_sla FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(no_of_days) as md,MIN(proposal_inward_date) as pid FROM audit_log ${dateW} GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY date ORDER BY date`,a.p);
      const qTrend=q(db,`SELECT date,SUM(within_sla) as ws,COUNT(*) as tot FROM (SELECT DATE(MIN(pid)) as date,CASE WHEN SUM(ut)<=${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END as within_sla FROM (SELECT proposal_no,CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL) as ut, proposal_inward_date as pid FROM audit_log ${qmw} ) GROUP BY proposal_no) GROUP BY date ORDER BY date`,[...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']);

      // ── PRODUCT-WISE UW QUEUE TAT ────────────────────────
      const prodTat=q(db,`SELECT product_name,ROUND(AVG(ut),2) as avg_tat,COUNT(*) as proposals FROM (SELECT product_name,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as ut FROM audit_log ${qmw} GROUP BY proposal_no) WHERE product_name IS NOT NULL GROUP BY product_name ORDER BY avg_tat DESC LIMIT 15`,[...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']);

      // ── UW PERFORMANCE TABLE ─────────────────────────────
      let uwPerfTable=[];
      if (ctx.hasUw) {
        const perfRows=q(db,`
          SELECT uw.uw_name,
            COUNT(DISTINCT uw.proposal_no) as total_proposals,
            SUM(CASE WHEN at.max_days IS NOT NULL AND at.max_days>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as journey_breaches,
            SUM(CASE WHEN uq.uw_tat IS NOT NULL AND uq.uw_tat>${sla} THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as uw_queue_breaches,
            ROUND(COALESCE(AVG(uq.uw_tat),0),2) as avg_uw_tat,
            ROUND(COALESCE(MAX(uq.uw_tat),0),1) as max_uw_tat
          FROM (SELECT DISTINCT uw_name,proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${uw}) uw
          LEFT JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(no_of_days) as max_days FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no) at ON uw.proposal_no=at.proposal_no
          LEFT JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as uw_tat FROM audit_log ${qmw} GROUP BY proposal_no) uq ON uw.proposal_no=uq.proposal_no
          GROUP BY uw.uw_name`,
          [...u.p,...a.p,...a.p,'UW_QUEUE']);
        uwPerfTable=perfRows.map(r=>{
          const tp=r.total_proposals||0;
          return {...r,journey_breach_rate:tp>0?Math.round(r.journey_breaches/tp*1000)/10:0,uw_queue_breach_rate:tp>0?Math.round(r.uw_queue_breaches/tp*1000)/10:0};
        }).sort((a,b)=>b.uw_queue_breach_rate-a.uw_queue_breach_rate);
      }

      const highestBreachUw = uwPerfTable[0]||{uw_name:'',uw_queue_breach_rate:0,total_proposals:0};

      const dr=g(db,`SELECT MIN(proposal_inward_date) as f,MAX(proposal_inward_date) as t FROM audit_log ${aw}`,a.p)||{};
      return { hasAudit:true, hasUw:ctx.hasUw&&uwPerfTable.length>0, slaThreshold:sla,
        kpi:{journeyBreaches,journeyCompliance,uwQueueBreaches,uwQueueCompliance,unattributed,highestBreachUw},
        jMatrix, uwMatrix, jTrend, qTrend, prodTat, uwPerfTable,
        datePeriod:{from:dr.f,to:dr.t} };
    } catch(e) { console.error('[TAT]',e.message,e.stack); return {error:e.message}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('tat:get-drill-down', async (event, source, filters, opts) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {rows:[],total:0,page:1,totalPages:1};
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const a=buildAudit(ctx,filters);
      const u=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const aw=w(a.c), uw=w(u.c);
      const sla=parseInt(((g(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'")||{}).value||'1'),10);
      const {page=1, perPage=10, dayBucket='all', bizType='all'} = opts||{};
      const offset=(page-1)*perPage;

      const qmw=w([...a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL']);

      // Extra filters for drill-down
      const extraConds=[];
      if (bizType && bizType!=='all') { extraConds.push(`at.business_type='${bizType.replace(/'/g,"''")}'`); }
      if (dayBucket && dayBucket!=='all' && dayBucket!=='More than 5') {
        extraConds.push(`CAST(at.max_days AS INTEGER)=${parseInt(dayBucket)}`);
      } else if (dayBucket==='More than 5') {
        extraConds.push('at.max_days>5');
      }
      const extraWhere = extraConds.length ? 'WHERE '+extraConds.join(' AND ') : '';

      const baseSql=`FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MIN(business_type) as business_type,MIN(product_name) as product_name,MAX(no_of_days) as max_days FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no) at
        LEFT JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as uw_tat FROM audit_log ${qmw} GROUP BY proposal_no) uq ON at.proposal_no=uq.proposal_no
        LEFT JOIN (SELECT uw.proposal_no,uw.uw_name FROM uw_productivity uw INNER JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(action_date) as md FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY proposal_no) lm ON uw.proposal_no=lm.proposal_no AND uw.action_date=lm.md GROUP BY uw.proposal_no) last_uw ON at.proposal_no=last_uw.proposal_no
        ${extraWhere}`;

      const totalR=g(db,`SELECT COUNT(*) as c ${baseSql}`,[...a.p,...a.p,'UW_QUEUE',...u.p]);
      const total=(totalR||{c:0}).c;
      const rows=q(db,`SELECT at.proposal_no,at.business_type,at.product_name,at.max_days as journey_days,COALESCE(uq.uw_tat,0) as uw_queue_days,CASE WHEN at.max_days>${sla} OR COALESCE(uq.uw_tat,0)>${sla} THEN 'Breached' ELSE 'Within SLA' END as sla_status,last_uw.uw_name ${baseSql} ORDER BY at.max_days DESC LIMIT ${perPage} OFFSET ${offset}`,[...a.p,...a.p,'UW_QUEUE',...u.p]);

      return {rows,total,page,totalPages:Math.ceil(total/perPage),perPage};
    } catch(e) { console.error('[TAT:drilldown]',e.message,e.stack); return {rows:[],total:0,page:1,totalPages:1}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('tat:export-drill-down', async (event, source, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return [];
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const a=buildAudit(ctx,filters);
      const uf=buildUw(ctx,filters);
      const aw=w(a.c), uw=w(uf.c);
      const sla=parseInt(((g(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'")||{value:'1'}).value),10);
      const qmw=w([...a.c,'current_bucket=?','queue_start_date IS NOT NULL','queue_end_date IS NOT NULL']);
      const sql=`SELECT at.proposal_no,at.business_type,at.product_name,at.max_days as journey_days,COALESCE(uq.uw_tat,0) as uw_queue_days,CASE WHEN at.max_days>${sla} OR COALESCE(uq.uw_tat,0)>${sla} THEN 'Breached' ELSE 'Within SLA' END as sla_status,last_uw.uw_name
        FROM (SELECT proposal_no,MIN(business_type) as business_type,MIN(product_name) as product_name,MAX(no_of_days) as max_days FROM audit_log ${aw} GROUP BY proposal_no) at
        LEFT JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,SUM(CAST((julianday(queue_end_date)-julianday(queue_start_date)) AS REAL)) as uw_tat FROM audit_log ${qmw} GROUP BY proposal_no) uq ON at.proposal_no=uq.proposal_no
        LEFT JOIN (SELECT uw2.proposal_no,uw2.uw_name FROM uw_productivity uw2 INNER JOIN (SELECT proposal_no,MAX(action_date) as md FROM uw_productivity ${uw} GROUP BY proposal_no) lm ON uw2.proposal_no=lm.proposal_no AND uw2.action_date=lm.md GROUP BY uw2.proposal_no) last_uw ON at.proposal_no=last_uw.proposal_no
        ORDER BY at.max_days DESC`;
      return q(db,sql,[...a.p,...a.p,'UW_QUEUE',...uf.p]);
    } catch(e) { console.error('[TAT:export]',e.message); return []; }
  });
}
module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/drilldown.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { buildQueryContext, safeAll, safeGet } = require('../../database/query');

const ACTION_COLS = ['accept','rejected','counter_offer','additional_info','additional_test','telemer','ppc','refer_to_cops','rulebook_refund','refer_to_uw'];
const ACTION_LABELS = { accept:'Accept',rejected:'Rejected',counter_offer:'Counter Offer',additional_info:'Additional Info',additional_test:'Additional Test',telemer:'TeleMER/VideoMER',ppc:'PPC Raised',refer_to_cops:'Refer to COPs',rulebook_refund:'Rulebook Refund',refer_to_uw:'Refer to UW' };

function getActionType(row) {
  const types = ACTION_COLS.filter(k=>row[k]).map(k=>ACTION_LABELS[k]);
  return types.length ? types.join(', ') : 'Refer to UW';
}

function getStatusOverride(uwRows) {
  if (!uwRows || !uwRows.length) return null;
  const sorted = [...uwRows].sort((a,b)=>b.action_date.localeCompare(a.action_date)||(b.id-a.id));
  const latest = sorted[0];
  if (!latest.is_final) return null;
  if (latest.accept)          return 'Accepted';
  if (latest.rejected)        return 'Rejected';
  if (latest.counter_offer)   return 'Counter Offer Issued';
  if (latest.rulebook_refund) return 'Rulebook Refund Initiated';
  return null;
}

const w = c => c.length ? 'WHERE '+c.join(' AND ') : '';

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {

  ipcMain.handle('drilldown:search', async (event, source, query) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db||!query||query.trim().length<2) return [];
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const q=`%${query.trim()}%`;
      const auditW=w(ctx.auditWhere?[ctx.auditWhere,'proposal_no LIKE ?']:['proposal_no LIKE ?']);
      const uwW   =w(ctx.uwWhere   ?[ctx.uwWhere,   'proposal_no LIKE ?']:['proposal_no LIKE ?']);
      const auditR=safeAll(db,`SELECT DISTINCT proposal_no FROM audit_log ${auditW} ORDER BY proposal_no LIMIT 15`,[...ctx.auditParams,q]);
      const uwR   =safeAll(db,`SELECT DISTINCT proposal_no FROM uw_productivity ${uwW} ORDER BY proposal_no LIMIT 15`,[...ctx.uwParams,q]);
      return [...new Set([...auditR.map(r=>r.proposal_no),...uwR.map(r=>r.proposal_no)])].sort().slice(0,20);
    } catch(e) { console.error('[Drilldown:search]',e.message); return []; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('drilldown:get-detail', async (event, source, proposalNo) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db||!proposalNo) return null;
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const sla=parseInt(((safeGet(db,"SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'")||{}).value||'1'),10);

      const aW=w(ctx.auditWhere?[ctx.auditWhere,'proposal_no=?']:['proposal_no=?']);
      const uW=w(ctx.uwWhere   ?[ctx.uwWhere,   'proposal_no=?']:['proposal_no=?']);

      const auditTrail=safeAll(db,`SELECT * FROM audit_log ${aW} ORDER BY queue_start_date ASC, id ASC`,[...ctx.auditParams,proposalNo]);
      // Use DISTINCT on content columns (excludes batch_id/id) so uploading the same
      // file twice in Full History mode doesn't show duplicate UW decision rows
      const uwDecisions=safeAll(db,`
        SELECT DISTINCT uw_name, action_date, product, business_type,
          refer_to_uw, accept, rejected, counter_offer, additional_info,
          additional_test, telemer, ppc, refer_to_cops, rulebook_refund,
          is_final, is_pending
        FROM uw_productivity ${uW}
        ORDER BY action_date ASC, uw_name ASC`,
        [...ctx.uwParams,proposalNo]);

      if (!auditTrail.length && !uwDecisions.length) return { notFound:true };

      // Header info from audit
      const firstAudit = auditTrail[0]||{};
      const lastAudit  = [...auditTrail].sort((a,b)=>b.queue_start_date?.localeCompare(b.queue_start_date)||0).pop()||firstAudit;
      const bizType    = firstAudit.business_type||uwDecisions[0]?.business_type||'-';
      const product    = firstAudit.product_name||'-';
      const inwardDate = firstAudit.proposal_inward_date;
      const currentBucket=firstAudit.current_bucket||'-';
      const auditStatus  =firstAudit.proposal_level_status_norm||firstAudit.proposal_level_status||'-';

      // Current status: UW override if final decision exists
      const statusOverride=getStatusOverride(uwDecisions);
      const currentStatus=statusOverride||auditStatus;

      // Journey TAT
      const journeyTat=auditTrail.length?Math.max(...auditTrail.map(r=>Number(r.no_of_days)||0)):0;

      // UW Queue TAT
      const uwQueueRows=auditTrail.filter(r=>r.current_bucket==='UW_QUEUE'&&r.queue_start_date&&r.queue_end_date);
      const uwQueueTat=uwQueueRows.reduce((s,r)=>{
        const d=(new Date(r.queue_end_date)-new Date(r.queue_start_date))/(1000*60*60*24);
        return s+(isNaN(d)?0:d);
      },0);

      // Last UW
      const sortedUw=[...uwDecisions].sort((a,b)=>b.action_date?.localeCompare(a.action_date)||(b.id-a.id));
      const lastUw=sortedUw[0]||null;

      // Augment UW decisions with action type and status derived from RAW action columns
      // (not the stored is_final — which may be stale in older ingested data)
      const uwDecisionsAugmented=uwDecisions.map(r=>({
        ...r,
        action_type: getActionType(r),
        is_status: (r.accept || r.rejected || r.counter_offer || r.rulebook_refund) ? 'Clear' : 'Pending'
      }));

      return {
        proposalNo, bizType, product, inwardDate, currentBucket, currentStatus,
        queueMovements:auditTrail.length,
        journeyTat, uwQueueTat:Math.round(uwQueueTat*100)/100,
        journeyBreached:journeyTat>sla, uwQueueBreached:uwQueueTat>sla,
        lastUw:lastUw?{name:lastUw.uw_name,date:lastUw.action_date,entryDate:lastUw.action_date}:null,
        auditTrail, uwDecisions:uwDecisionsAugmented, sla
      };
    } catch(e) { console.error('[Drilldown:detail]',e.message,e.stack); return {error:e.message}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('drilldown:export-excel', async (event, source, proposalNo) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db||!proposalNo) return [];
      const ctx=buildQueryContext(source, getSession());
      const aW=w(ctx.auditWhere?[ctx.auditWhere,'proposal_no=?']:['proposal_no=?']);
      const uW=w(ctx.uwWhere   ?[ctx.uwWhere,   'proposal_no=?']:['proposal_no=?']);
      const auditRows=safeAll(db,`SELECT * FROM audit_log ${aW} ORDER BY queue_start_date ASC`,[...ctx.auditParams,proposalNo]);
      const uwRows   =safeAll(db,`SELECT * FROM uw_productivity ${uW} ORDER BY action_date ASC`,[...ctx.uwParams,proposalNo]);
      const auditSheet=auditRows.map(r=>({'Proposal No':r.proposal_no,'Bucket':r.current_bucket,'From':r.coming_from_bucket,'Decision':r.coming_with_decision,'Queue Start':r.queue_start_date,'Queue End':r.queue_end_date,'Days':r.no_of_days,'Status':r.proposal_level_status_norm}));
      const uwSheet  =uwRows.map(r=>({'UW Name':r.uw_name,'Action Date':r.action_date,'Accept':r.accept,'Rejected':r.rejected,'Counter Offer':r.counter_offer,'Additional Info':r.additional_info,'Additional Test':r.additional_test,'TeleMER':r.telemer,'PPC':r.ppc,'Refer to COPs':r.refer_to_cops,'Rulebook Refund':r.rulebook_refund}));
      return { auditSheet, uwSheet };
    } catch(e) { return {auditSheet:[],uwSheet:[]}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('drilldown:export-pdf', async () => { return { info: 'Use Export PDF button in topbar' }; });
}

module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/settings.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
const { safeGet, safeAll } = require('../../database/query');
const { app } = require('electron');
const path = require('path');
const fs   = require('fs');
const crypto = require('crypto');

function register(ipcMain, getDB) {

  // PIN helpers
  function hashPin(pin) { return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(pin).digest('hex'); }

  // ── PIN VERIFY ──────────────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('settings:verify-pin', async (event, pin) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return { success:false, error:'DB not ready' };
      const enabledRow=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='security_pin_enabled'").get();
      if (!enabledRow||enabledRow.value!=='true') return { success:true, pinRequired:false };
      const hashRow=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='security_pin_hash'").get();
      if (!hashRow||!hashRow.value) return { success:true, pinRequired:false };
      const match = hashPin(pin)===hashRow.value;
      if (match) {
        db.prepare("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_settings (key,value) VALUES (?,?)").run('pin_verified_session','true');
      }
      return { success:match, pinRequired:true, error:match?null:'Incorrect PIN' };
    } catch(e) { return {success:false,error:e.message}; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:pin-required', async () => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return false;
      const r=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='security_pin_enabled'").get();
      if (!r||r.value!=='true') return false;
      const verified=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='pin_verified_session'").get();
      return !(verified&&verified.value==='true');
    } catch { return false; }
  });

  ipcMain.handle('settings:save-pin', async (event, newPin, enabled) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {success:false};
      const stmt=db.prepare("INSERT OR REPLACE INTO app_settings (key,value) VALUES (?,?)");
      stmt.run('security_pin_enabled', enabled?'true':'false');
      if (newPin && newPin.length>=4) stmt.run('security_pin_hash', hashPin(newPin));
      else if (!enabled) stmt.run('security_pin_hash','');
      return {success:true};
    } catch(e) { return {success:false,error:e.message}; }
  });

  // ── DB STATS ────────────────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('settings:get-db-stats', async () => {
    try {
      const db=getDB(); if (!db) return {};
      const proposals = db.prepare('SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM audit_log').get();
      const uwActions = db.prepare('SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM uw_productivity').get();
      const batches   = db.prepare('SELECT COUNT(*) as c FROM upload_batches').get();
      const dateRange = db.prepare('SELECT MIN(proposal_inward_date) as minDate, MAX(proposal_inward_date) as maxDate FROM audit_log').get();
      const config    = readConfig();
      const dbFile    = (config||{}).dbFile||'';
      let dbSize = '-';
      try { if (dbFile&&fs.existsSync(dbFile)) { const s=fs.statSync(dbFile); dbSize=formatBytes(s.size); } } catch {}
      return {
        totalProposalRows: proposals.c, totalUwActions: uwActions.c,
        totalBatches: batches.c, dateFrom: dateRange.minDate, dateTo: dateRange.maxDate,
        dbPath: (config||{}).dbPath||'', dbFile, dbSize,
        appVersion: app.getVersion()
      };
    } catch(e) { return {error:e.message}; }
  });

  function readConfig() {
    const CONFIG_PATH = path.join(app.getPath('userData'),'config.json');
    try { if (fs.existsSync(CONFIG_PATH)) return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(CONFIG_PATH,'utf-8')); } catch {}
    return null;
  }
  function formatBytes(b) {
    if (b<1024) return b+' B';
    if (b<1024*1024) return (b/1024).toFixed(1)+' KB';
    return (b/(1024*1024)).toFixed(2)+' MB';
  }
}

module.exports = { register };


================================================================================
FILE: ipc/handlers/export.js
================================================================================
'use strict';

function register(ipcMain, getDB, getSession) {
  const { app, shell, BrowserWindow } = require('electron');
  const path = require('path');
  const fs   = require('fs');

  function getExportPath(db) {
    try {
      const r=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='export_output_path'").get();
      return (r&&r.value)?r.value:app.getPath('downloads');
    } catch { return app.getPath('downloads'); }
  }

  function getPdfPageSize(db) {
    try {
      const r=db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='export_pdf_page_size'").get();
      return (r&&r.value)||'A4';
    } catch { return 'A4'; }
  }

  function ensureDir(p) {
    if (!fs.existsSync(p)) fs.mkdirSync(p,{recursive:true});
  }

  // ── EXCEL EXPORT ────────────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('export:to-excel', async (event, type, data, fileName) => {
    try {
      const xlsx=require('xlsx');
      const db=getDB();
      const exportPath=db?getExportPath(db):app.getPath('downloads');
      ensureDir(exportPath);

      // data can be array or {auditSheet, uwSheet} for dual-sheet export
      const ts=new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g,'-').substring(0,19);
      const safe=(fileName||'ProTrack_Export').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_\-]/g,'_');
      const filePath=path.join(exportPath,`${safe}_${ts}.xlsx`);
      const wb=xlsx.utils.book_new();

      if (Array.isArray(data)) {
        xlsx.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,xlsx.utils.json_to_sheet(data||[]),'Data');
      } else if (data && typeof data==='object') {
        if (data.auditSheet) xlsx.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,xlsx.utils.json_to_sheet(data.auditSheet),'Audit Trail');
        if (data.uwSheet)    xlsx.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,xlsx.utils.json_to_sheet(data.uwSheet),'UW Decisions');
      } else {
        xlsx.utils.book_append_sheet(wb,xlsx.utils.json_to_sheet([]),'Data');
      }

      xlsx.writeFile(wb,filePath);
      shell.openPath(filePath);
      return {success:true,filePath};
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[Export:excel]',e.message);
      return {success:false,error:e.message};
    }
  });

  // ── PDF EXPORT ──────────────────────────────────────────
  ipcMain.handle('export:to-pdf', async (event, tabName, filters) => {
    try {
      const db=getDB();
      const win=BrowserWindow.getFocusedWindow()||BrowserWindow.getAllWindows()[0];
      if (!win) return {success:false,error:'No window found for PDF export.'};

      const exportPath=db?getExportPath(db):app.getPath('downloads');
      const pageSize  =db?getPdfPageSize(db):'A4';
      ensureDir(exportPath);

      const pdfBuffer=await win.webContents.printToPDF({
        printBackground:true, landscape:true, pageSize, marginsType:0
      });

      const ts=new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g,'-').substring(0,19);
      const safe=(tabName||'report').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_\-]/g,'_');
      const filePath=path.join(exportPath,`ProTrack_${safe}_${ts}.pdf`);
      fs.writeFileSync(filePath,pdfBuffer);
      shell.openPath(filePath);
      return {success:true,filePath};
    } catch(e) {
      console.error('[Export:pdf]',e.message);
      return {success:false,error:e.message};
    }
  });
}

module.exports = { register };

'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Main App Controller
 * Handles navigation, mode switching, upload triggers, filter orchestration
 */
(function () {

  // ── STATE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const state = {
    mode: 'current',        // 'current' | 'history'
    activeTab: 'executive',
    hasAuditData: false,
    hasUwData: false,
    filters: {
      businessType: 'all',
      productName: 'all',
      status: 'all',
      bucket: 'all',
      dateFrom: '',
      dateTo: ''
    },
    settings: {},
    filterDebounceTimer: null,
    chartInstances: {}
  };

  // ── DOM REFS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const dom = {
    sidebarNav:       document.getElementById('sidebarNav'),
    modeBadge:        document.getElementById('modeBadge'),
    topbarMeta:       document.getElementById('topbarMeta'),
    uploadBtns:       document.getElementById('uploadBtns'),
    viewPeriodSelect: document.getElementById('viewPeriodSelect'),
    filterbar:        document.getElementById('filterbar'),
    content:          document.getElementById('content'),
    uploadPrompt:     document.getElementById('uploadPrompt'),
    processingOverlay:document.getElementById('processingOverlay'),
    processingTitle:  document.getElementById('processingTitle'),
    processingDetail: document.getElementById('processingDetail'),
    btnHome:          document.getElementById('btnHome'),
    btnRefresh:       document.getElementById('btnRefresh'),
    btnExportPdf:     document.getElementById('btnExportPdf'),
    btnClearFilters:  document.getElementById('btnClearFilters'),
    fltBizType:       document.getElementById('fltBizType'),
    fltProduct:       document.getElementById('fltProduct'),
    fltStatus:        document.getElementById('fltStatus'),
    fltBucket:        document.getElementById('fltBucket'),
    fltDateFrom:      document.getElementById('fltDateFrom'),
    fltDateTo:        document.getElementById('fltDateTo'),
    auditFileInput:   document.getElementById('auditFileInput'),
    uwFileInput:      document.getElementById('uwFileInput')
  };

  // ── TABS CONFIG ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  const TABS_WITH_FILTERS = ['executive', 'pipeline', 'uw', 'tat'];
  const TABS_NO_FILTERS   = ['drilldown', 'settings'];

  // ── INIT ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  async function init() {
    await loadSettings();
    detectMode();
    setupNavigation();
    setupFilters();
    setupFileUploads();
    setupTopbarButtons();
    navigateTo('executive');
    if (state.mode === 'history') {
      loadFilterOptions();
      updateTopbarMeta();
    }
  }

  // ── MODE DETECTION ────────────────────────────────────────────
  function detectMode() {
    // Mode is passed via URL hash: index.html#history or index.html#current
    const hash = window.location.hash.replace('#', '');
    state.mode = (hash === 'history') ? 'history' : 'current';
    dom.modeBadge.textContent  = state.mode === 'history' ? 'FULL HISTORY' : 'CURRENT UPLOAD';
    dom.modeBadge.className    = `mode-badge ${state.mode === 'history' ? 'history' : 'current'}`;

    if (state.mode === 'current') {
      dom.uploadBtns.classList.remove('hidden');
      dom.viewPeriodSelect.classList.add('hidden');
      showUploadPrompt();
    } else {
      dom.uploadBtns.classList.add('hidden');
      dom.viewPeriodSelect.classList.remove('hidden');
    }
  }

  // ── NAVIGATION ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function setupNavigation() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item[data-tab]').forEach(item => {
      item.addEventListener('click', () => navigateTo(item.dataset.tab));
    });
    dom.btnHome.addEventListener('click', () => {
      // Clear session if going home from Current Upload
      if (state.mode === 'current') {
        window.protrack.upload.clearSession();
      }
      window.location.href = '../landing/landing.html';
    });
  }

  // ── TAB RENDER CACHE ─────────────────────────────────────────
  // Avoids re-fetching data when switching between already-loaded tabs.
  // Key = mode + filters hash. Cleared on data change/upload/refresh.
  const _tabCache = {};
  function _cacheKey() {
    return state.mode + '|' + JSON.stringify(state.filters || {});
  }
  window._invalidateTabCache = () => Object.keys(_tabCache).forEach(k => delete _tabCache[k]);

  function navigateTo(tab) {
    state.activeTab = tab;

    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item[data-tab]').forEach(item => {
      item.classList.toggle('active', item.dataset.tab === tab);
    });

    if (TABS_NO_FILTERS.includes(tab)) {
      dom.filterbar.classList.add('hidden');
    } else {
      dom.filterbar.classList.remove('hidden');
    }

    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(panel => {
      panel.classList.toggle('hidden', panel.id !== `tab-${tab}`);
    });

    // Skip full re-render if already rendered with the same data
    const key = _cacheKey();
    if (_tabCache[tab] === key) return;

    _tabCache[tab] = key; // claim the slot immediately (prevents double-render on fast clicks)
    renderActiveTab();
  }

  // ── RENDER ACTIVE TAB ─────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderActiveTab() {
    const tab = state.activeTab;
    const source = state.mode;
    const filters = state.filters;
    const hasData = state.hasAuditData || state.hasUwData;

    delete _tabCache[tab]; // bust cache so this forced render is fresh

    if (state.mode === 'current' && !hasData && !TABS_NO_FILTERS.includes(tab)) {
      showUploadPrompt();
      return;
    }
    hideUploadPrompt();

    switch (tab) {
      case 'executive': window.tabExecutive && window.tabExecutive.render(source, filters); break;
      case 'pipeline':  window.tabPipeline  && window.tabPipeline.render(source, filters);  break;
      case 'uw':        window.tabUw        && window.tabUw.render(source, filters);        break;
      case 'tat':       window.tabTat       && window.tabTat.render(source, filters);       break;
      case 'drilldown': window.tabDrilldown && window.tabDrilldown.render(source);          break;
      case 'settings':  window.tabSettings  && window.tabSettings.render();                 break;
    }

    _tabCache[tab] = _cacheKey(); // mark as rendered with current data
  }

  // ── FILTER SETUP ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  function setupFilters() {
    dom.fltBizType.addEventListener('change', onFilterChange);
    dom.fltProduct.addEventListener('change', onFilterChange);
    dom.fltStatus.addEventListener('change', onFilterChange);
    dom.fltBucket.addEventListener('change', onFilterChange);

    // Date range: auto-apply when both dates are set
    dom.fltDateFrom.addEventListener('change', () => {
      if (dom.fltDateTo.value) onFilterChange();
    });
    dom.fltDateTo.addEventListener('change', () => {
      if (dom.fltDateFrom.value) onFilterChange();
    });

    dom.btnClearFilters.addEventListener('click', clearFilters);

    // Quick date buttons
    document.querySelectorAll('.btn-quick').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
        document.querySelectorAll('.btn-quick').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
        btn.classList.add('active');
        applyQuickDate(btn.dataset.quick);
      });
    });
  }

  function onFilterChange() {
    state.filters.businessType = dom.fltBizType.value;
    state.filters.productName  = dom.fltProduct.value;
    state.filters.status       = dom.fltStatus.value;
    state.filters.bucket       = dom.fltBucket.value;
    state.filters.dateFrom     = dom.fltDateFrom.value;
    state.filters.dateTo       = dom.fltDateTo.value;

    // 200ms debounce for dropdown changes
    clearTimeout(state.filterDebounceTimer);
    state.filterDebounceTimer = setTimeout(() => renderActiveTab(), 200);
  }

  function clearFilters() {
    dom.fltBizType.value  = 'all';
    dom.fltProduct.value  = 'all';
    dom.fltStatus.value   = 'all';
    dom.fltBucket.value   = 'all';
    dom.fltDateFrom.value = '';
    dom.fltDateTo.value   = '';
    document.querySelectorAll('.btn-quick').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    state.filters = { businessType: 'all', productName: 'all', status: 'all', bucket: 'all', dateFrom: '', dateTo: '' };
    renderActiveTab();
  }

  function applyQuickDate(quick) {
    const now = new Date();
    const fmt = d => d.toISOString().split('T')[0];
    let from, to;

    switch (quick) {
      case 'today':
        from = to = fmt(now);
        break;
      case 'this_week': {
        const day = now.getDay();
        const mon = new Date(now); mon.setDate(now.getDate() - (day === 0 ? 6 : day - 1));
        from = fmt(mon); to = fmt(now);
        break;
      }
      case 'this_month':
        from = fmt(new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), 1));
        to   = fmt(now);
        break;
      case 'last_month': {
        const lm = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth() - 1, 1);
        const le = new Date(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), 0);
        from = fmt(lm); to = fmt(le);
        break;
      }
      case 'this_year':
        from = fmt(new Date(now.getFullYear(), 0, 1));
        to   = fmt(now);
        break;
      default: return;
    }

    dom.fltDateFrom.value = from;
    dom.fltDateTo.value   = to;
    state.filters.dateFrom = from;
    state.filters.dateTo   = to;
    renderActiveTab();
  }

  async function loadFilterOptions() {
    try {
      const opts = await window.protrack.filters.getOptions(state.mode);
      populateSelect(dom.fltBizType, opts.businessTypes, 'Business Type');
      populateSelect(dom.fltProduct,  opts.products,      'Product Name');
      populateSelect(dom.fltStatus,   opts.statuses,      'Status');
      populateSelect(dom.fltBucket,   opts.buckets,       'Bucket');
    } catch (e) {
      console.error('Filter options error:', e);
    }
  }

  function populateSelect(sel, items, label) {
    const val = sel.value;
    sel.innerHTML = `<option value="all">${label}</option>`;
    (items || []).forEach(item => {
      const opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = item;
      opt.textContent = item;
      sel.appendChild(opt);
    });
    // Restore previous selection if still valid
    if (items && items.includes(val)) sel.value = val;
  }

  // ── FILE UPLOADS ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  function setupFileUploads() {
    dom.auditFileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      if (e.target.files[0]) handleFileUpload(e.target.files[0], 'audit');
      e.target.value = '';
    });
    dom.uwFileInput.addEventListener('change', (e) => {
      if (e.target.files[0]) handleFileUpload(e.target.files[0], 'uw');
      e.target.value = '';
    });
  }

  async function handleFileUpload(fileOrInput, type) {
    const file = fileOrInput instanceof File ? fileOrInput : fileOrInput.files[0];
    if (!file) return;

    showProcessing(`Processing ${type === 'audit' ? 'Audit Log' : 'UW Productivity Sheet'}...`, `Reading ${file.name}`);

    try {
      const arrayBuffer = await file.arrayBuffer();
      const uint8 = new Uint8Array(arrayBuffer);
      const result = await window.protrack.upload.processFiles({
        fileName: file.name,
        fileType: type,
        data: Array.from(uint8),
        mode: state.mode
      });

      hideProcessing();

      if (result.success) {
        if (type === 'audit') state.hasAuditData = true;
        else state.hasUwData = true;

        window.utils.toast(`${file.name} loaded successfully — ${result.rows} rows processed.`, 'success');
        await loadFilterOptions();
        updateTopbarMeta();
        window._invalidateTabCache(); // new data = all tab caches stale
        renderActiveTab();
      } else {
        window.utils.toast(`Upload failed: ${result.error}`, 'error');
      }
    } catch (e) {
      hideProcessing();
      window.utils.toast(`Error processing file: ${e.message}`, 'error');
    }
  }

  // Expose for inline use in HTML
  window.protrackApp = { handleFileUpload };

  // ── TOPBAR BUTTONS ────────────────────────────────────────────
  function setupTopbarButtons() {
    dom.btnRefresh.addEventListener('click', () => {
      if (state.mode === 'history') loadFilterOptions();
      renderActiveTab();
      window.utils.toast('View refreshed', 'info');
    });

    dom.btnExportPdf.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      window.utils.toast('Generating PDF...', 'info');
      await window.protrack.export.toPdf(state.activeTab, state.filters);
    });

    dom.viewPeriodSelect.addEventListener('change', () => {
      renderActiveTab();
    });
  }

  async function updateTopbarMeta() {
    if (state.mode === 'history') {
      const stats = await window.protrack.settings.getDbStats();
      if (stats.dateFrom && stats.dateTo) {
        dom.topbarMeta.textContent = `${window.utils.fmtDate(stats.dateFrom)} → ${window.utils.fmtDate(stats.dateTo)}  ·  ${(stats.totalProposalRows || 0).toLocaleString()} proposals in DB`;
      }
    }
  }

  // ── SETTINGS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  async function loadSettings() {
    try {
      state.settings = await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
      window.appSettings = state.settings;
      applyTheme(state.settings.appearance_theme);
      applySidebar(state.settings.appearance_sidebar_style);
    } catch (e) { console.warn('Settings load error:', e); }
  }

  // Apply theme immediately by setting a data-theme attribute on <html>
  // The CSS has [data-theme="light"] and [data-theme="system"] overrides
  function applyTheme(theme) {
    const t = theme || 'dark';
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', t);
    // Update meta/background for system theme immediate effect
    if (t === 'system') {
      const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
      document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme-effective', prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light');
    }
  }

  // Apply sidebar style immediately
  function applySidebar(style) {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-sidebar', style || 'icons_labels');
    const labels = document.querySelectorAll('.sidebar-label');
    labels.forEach(el => {
      el.style.display = (style === 'icons_only') ? 'none' : '';
    });
  }

  // Expose for settings tab to call on save
  window.applyTheme   = applyTheme;
  window.applySidebar = applySidebar;

  // ── OVERLAY HELPERS ───────────────────────────────────────────
  function showUploadPrompt() {
    dom.uploadPrompt.classList.remove('hidden');
    document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.add('hidden'));
  }

  function hideUploadPrompt() {
    dom.uploadPrompt.classList.add('hidden');
    const active = document.getElementById(`tab-${state.activeTab}`);
    if (active) active.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function showProcessing(title, detail) {
    dom.processingTitle.textContent  = title  || 'Processing...';
    dom.processingDetail.textContent = detail || '';
    dom.processingOverlay.classList.remove('hidden');
  }

  function hideProcessing() {
    dom.processingOverlay.classList.add('hidden');
  }

  // ── EXPOSE APP STATE FOR TAB MODULES ─────────────────────────
  window.appState    = state;
  window.appNavigate = navigateTo;

  // ── START ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);

})();


================================================================================
FILE: src/app/utils.js
