'use strict';

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Renderer Utilities
 * Shared helper functions for all tab modules
 */
window.utils = (function () {

  // ── DATE FORMAT ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  function fmtDate(dateStr, format) {
    if (!dateStr) return '-';
    const fmt = (window.appSettings && window.appSettings.appearance_date_format) || 'DD-MM-YYYY';
    try {
      const d = new Date(dateStr);
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return dateStr;
      const day  = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
      const mon  = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
      const year = d.getFullYear();
      const hrs  = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
      const min  = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');

      switch (fmt) {
        case 'MM-DD-YYYY': return `${mon}-${day}-${year}`;
        case 'YYYY-MM-DD': return `${year}-${mon}-${day}`;
        default:           return `${day}-${mon}-${year}`;
      }
    } catch { return dateStr; }
  }

  function fmtDateTime(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return '-';
    try {
      const d = new Date(dateStr);
      if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return dateStr;
      return `${fmtDate(dateStr)} ${String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0')}:${String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0')}`;
    } catch { return dateStr; }
  }

  function fmtMonthYear(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return '-';
    try {
      const d = new Date(dateStr);
      const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
      return `${months[d.getMonth()]} ${d.getFullYear()}`;
    } catch { return dateStr; }
  }

  // ── NUMBER FORMAT ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  function fmtNum(n) {
    if (n === null || n === undefined) return '-';
    return Number(n).toLocaleString();
  }

  function fmtPct(n, decimals = 1) {
    if (n === null || n === undefined) return '-';
    return `${Number(n).toFixed(decimals)}%`;
  }

  function fmtDays(n) {
    if (n === null || n === undefined) return '-';
    const d = Number(n);
    return d === 1 ? '1d' : `${d.toFixed(1)}d`;
  }

  // ── DAY CATEGORY ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  function dayCategory(days) {
    const d = Math.floor(Number(days) || 0);
    return d <= 5 ? String(d) : 'More than 5';
  }

  const DAY_CATS = ['0', '1', '2', '3', '4', '5', 'More than 5'];

  // ── COLOUR HELPERS ────────────────────────────────────────────
  const CHART_COLOURS = [
    '#3b82f6','#22c55e','#f59e0b','#ef4444','#8b5cf6',
    '#06b6d4','#ec4899','#f97316','#84cc16','#a78bfa'
  ];

  const BIZ_COLOURS = {
    'New Business':       '#3b82f6',
    'NB with Portability':'#06b6d4',
    'Renewal':            '#f59e0b',
    'Endorsement':        '#ef4444',
    'Cancel and Rebook':  '#22c55e'
  };

  const ACTION_COLOURS = {
    'Accept':              '#22c55e',
    'Rejected':            '#ef4444',
    'Counter Offer':       '#f59e0b',
    'Additional Info':     '#3b82f6',
    'Additional Test':     '#8b5cf6',
    'TeleMER/VideoMER':    '#06b6d4',
    'PPC Raised':          '#ec4899',
    'Refer to COPs':       '#f97316',
    'Rulebook Refund':     '#a78bfa'
  };

  function getColour(key, idx) {
    return BIZ_COLOURS[key] || ACTION_COLOURS[key] || CHART_COLOURS[idx % CHART_COLOURS.length];
  }

  function slaColour(days) {
    const d = Number(days);
    const threshold = Number((window.appSettings && window.appSettings.sla_threshold_days) || 1);
    if (d <= threshold) return '#22c55e';
    if (d <= 3) return '#f59e0b';
    return '#ef4444';
  }

  function pendingRateColour(pct) {
    const threshold = Number((window.appSettings && window.appSettings.pending_rate_warning_pct) || 10);
    if (pct === 0) return 'green';
    if (pct <= threshold) return 'amber';
    return 'red';
  }

  function breachRateColour(pct) {
    if (pct < 20) return 'green';
    if (pct <= 40) return 'amber';
    return 'red';
  }

  // ── SLA THRESHOLD ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  function getSlaThreshold() {
    return Number((window.appSettings && window.appSettings.sla_threshold_days) || 1);
  }

  function isWithinSla(days) {
    return Number(days) <= getSlaThreshold();
  }

  // ── TOAST ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function toast(message, type = 'info') {
    const container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
    if (!container) return;

    const icons = { success: '✅', error: '❌', info: 'ℹ️' };
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = `toast ${type}`;
    el.innerHTML = `<span>${icons[type] || 'ℹ️'}</span><span>${message}</span>`;
    container.appendChild(el);

    setTimeout(() => {
      el.style.animation = 'slideOut 0.25s ease forwards';
      setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 250);
    }, 3500);
  }

  // ── MODAL ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function modal({ title, body, confirmText, cancelText, danger, onConfirm }) {
    const container = document.getElementById('modal-container');
    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'modal-overlay';
    overlay.innerHTML = `
      <div class="modal">
        <div class="modal-title">${title}</div>
        <div class="modal-body">${body}</div>
        <div class="modal-actions">
          <button class="btn btn-secondary" id="modalCancel">${cancelText || 'Cancel'}</button>
          <button class="btn ${danger ? 'btn-danger' : 'btn-primary'}" id="modalConfirm">${confirmText || 'Confirm'}</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
    container.appendChild(overlay);

    overlay.querySelector('#modalCancel').addEventListener('click', () => overlay.remove());
    overlay.querySelector('#modalConfirm').addEventListener('click', () => {
      overlay.remove();
      if (onConfirm) onConfirm();
    });
    overlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === overlay) overlay.remove(); });
  }

  // ── CHART DESTROY HELPER ──────────────────────────────────────
  function destroyChart(canvasId) {
    const existing = Chart.getChart(canvasId);
    if (existing) existing.destroy();
  }

  // ── EMPTY STATE HTML ──────────────────────────────────────────
  function emptyState(icon, title, sub) {
    return `
      <div class="empty-state">
        <div class="empty-icon">${icon}</div>
        <div class="empty-title">${title}</div>
        ${sub ? `<div class="empty-sub">${sub}</div>` : ''}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function uploadRequired(fileType) {
    return `
      <div class="upload-required">
        <div class="ur-icon">📂</div>
        <div class="ur-title">Upload ${fileType} to see this data</div>
        <div class="ur-sub">This section requires the ${fileType} file to be uploaded.</div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function loading() {
    return `<div class="loading-wrap"><div class="spinner"></div> Loading...</div>`;
  }

  // ── SORT TABLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function makeSortable(tableId) {
    const table = document.getElementById(tableId);
    if (!table) return;
    const headers = table.querySelectorAll('thead th');
    let sortCol = -1, sortDir = 1;

    headers.forEach((th, idx) => {
      th.addEventListener('click', () => {
        if (sortCol === idx) sortDir *= -1;
        else { sortCol = idx; sortDir = 1; }

        headers.forEach(h => h.classList.remove('sort-asc', 'sort-desc'));
        th.classList.add(sortDir === 1 ? 'sort-asc' : 'sort-desc');

        const tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
        const rows  = Array.from(tbody.querySelectorAll('tr'));
        rows.sort((a, b) => {
          const av = a.cells[idx] ? a.cells[idx].textContent.trim() : '';
          const bv = b.cells[idx] ? b.cells[idx].textContent.trim() : '';
          const an = parseFloat(av.replace(/[%,]/g, ''));
          const bn = parseFloat(bv.replace(/[%,]/g, ''));
          if (!isNaN(an) && !isNaN(bn)) return (an - bn) * sortDir;
          return av.localeCompare(bv) * sortDir;
        });
        rows.forEach((r, i) => {
          r.classList.toggle('alt', i % 2 === 1);
          tbody.appendChild(r);
        });
      });
    });
  }

  // ── PAGINATION ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderPagination(containerId, { page, totalPages, totalRows, perPage }, onPageChange) {
    const c = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!c) return;
    const start = (page - 1) * perPage + 1;
    const end   = Math.min(page * perPage, totalRows);

    let btns = '';
    for (let i = 1; i <= totalPages; i++) {
      if (i === 1 || i === totalPages || Math.abs(i - page) <= 2) {
        btns += `<button class="page-btn ${i === page ? 'active' : ''}" data-page="${i}">${i}</button>`;
      } else if (Math.abs(i - page) === 3) {
        btns += `<button class="page-btn" disabled>…</button>`;
      }
    }

    c.innerHTML = `
      <div class="pagination">
        <div class="pagination-info">Showing ${start}–${end} of ${fmtNum(totalRows)}</div>
        <div class="pagination-controls">
          <button class="page-btn" data-page="${page - 1}" ${page === 1 ? 'disabled' : ''}>‹</button>
          ${btns}
          <button class="page-btn" data-page="${page + 1}" ${page === totalPages ? 'disabled' : ''}>›</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;

    c.querySelectorAll('.page-btn[data-page]:not([disabled])').forEach(btn => {
      btn.addEventListener('click', () => onPageChange(parseInt(btn.dataset.page)));
    });
  }

  // ── DEFAULT CHART CONFIG ──────────────────────────────────────
  const defaultChartOptions = {
    responsive: true,
    maintainAspectRatio: false,
    plugins: {
      legend: {
        labels: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { size: 11, family: 'Segoe UI' }, padding: 16 }
      },
      tooltip: {
        backgroundColor: '#1e1e3c',
        borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',
        borderWidth: 1,
        titleColor: '#f1f5f9',
        bodyColor: '#94a3b8',
        padding: 10,
        cornerRadius: 8
      }
    },
    scales: {
      x: {
        ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 11 } },
        grid:  { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }
      },
      y: {
        ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 11 } },
        grid:  { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }
      }
    }
  };

  // ── ESCAPE HTML ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  function esc(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    return String(str).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
  }

  // ── PUBLIC API ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  return {
    fmtDate, fmtDateTime, fmtMonthYear,
    fmtNum, fmtPct, fmtDays,
    dayCategory, DAY_CATS,
    getColour, slaColour, pendingRateColour, breachRateColour,
    BIZ_COLOURS, ACTION_COLOURS, CHART_COLOURS,
    getSlaThreshold, isWithinSla,
    toast, modal,
    destroyChart,
    emptyState, uploadRequired, loading,
    makeSortable, renderPagination,
    defaultChartOptions,
    esc
  };
})();

window.appFilters = { current: {} };

'use strict';
/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Executive Summary Tab Renderer
 */
window.tabExecutive = (function () {

  async function render(source, filters) {
    const el = document.getElementById('tab-executive');
    if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML = window.utils.loading();

    let data;
    try { data = await window.protrack.executive.getStats(source, filters); }
    catch (e) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',e.message); return; }
    if (data.error) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Query Error',data.error); return; }

    const u = window.utils;
    const { kpi, charts, datePeriod, hasAudit, hasUw, slaThreshold } = data;

    // ── DATE SUBTITLE ─────────────────────────────────────
    const dateSub = datePeriod && datePeriod.from
      ? `Data period: <span>${u.fmtDate(datePeriod.from)} → ${u.fmtDate(datePeriod.to)}</span>`
      : source === 'current' ? '<span>Current Upload Session</span>' : '<span>Full History</span>';

    // ── SLA BADGE ─────────────────────────────────────────
    const slaBadge = (pct, breaches) => `
      <span style="font-size:26px;font-weight:800;color:${pct>=70?'#22c55e':pct>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444'}">${u.fmtPct(pct)}</span>
      <div class="kpi-sub">${u.fmtNum(breaches)} breaches · SLA = ${slaThreshold} day${slaThreshold!==1?'s':''}</div>`;

    el.innerHTML = `
<div class="page-header">
  <div class="page-title">📊 Executive Summary</div>
  <div class="page-subtitle">${dateSub}</div>
</div>

<!-- 5 KPI Cards -->
<div class="kpi-grid kpi-grid-5">
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Total Proposals <span class="kpi-icon">📋</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value">${u.fmtNum(kpi.totalProposals)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Unique proposal IDs in dataset</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card ${kpi.journeyCompliance>=70?'':''}">
    <div class="kpi-label">Journey TAT Compliance <span class="kpi-icon">🛣️</span></div>
    ${hasAudit ? slaBadge(kpi.journeyCompliance, kpi.journeyBreaches) : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:18px;color:#475569">No data</div><div class="kpi-sub">Upload Audit Log</div>`}
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">UW Queue TAT Compliance <span class="kpi-icon">⏱️</span></div>
    ${hasAudit ? slaBadge(kpi.uwQueueCompliance, kpi.uwQueueBreaches) : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:18px;color:#475569">No data</div><div class="kpi-sub">Upload Audit Log</div>`}
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Team Accept Rate <span class="kpi-icon">✅</span></div>
    ${hasUw ? `<span style="font-size:26px;font-weight:800;color:${kpi.teamAcceptRate>=50?'#22c55e':'#f59e0b'}">${u.fmtPct(kpi.teamAcceptRate)}</span>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Accept + Counter Offer / Clear</div>` : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:18px;color:#475569">No data</div><div class="kpi-sub">Upload UW Sheet</div>`}
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Pending Cases <span class="kpi-icon">⏳</span></div>
    ${hasUw ? `<div class="kpi-value amber">${u.fmtNum(kpi.pendingCases)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Awaiting final UW decision</div>` : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:18px;color:#475569">No data</div><div class="kpi-sub">Upload UW Sheet</div>`}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Row 2: Daily Output + Action Mix -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Daily UW Output</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Daily team actions · ${u.fmtNum(charts.dailyOutput.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.actions,0))} total recorded actions</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasUw ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:240px"><canvas id="execDailyOut"></canvas></div>` : u.uploadRequired('UW Productivity Sheet')}
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Action Type Distribution</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Team-wide · ${u.fmtNum(Object.values(charts.actionMix).reduce((s,v)=>s+(v||0),0))} total actions · 9 types</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasUw ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:220px"><canvas id="execActionMix"></canvas></div><div id="execActionLegend" style="margin-top:10px;font-size:11px"></div>` : u.uploadRequired('UW Productivity Sheet')}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Row 3: Month-over-Month -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2" style="margin-bottom:14px">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Volume Trend (Month-over-Month)</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Total proposals vs UW actioned by month</div>
    </div></div>
    ${(hasAudit||hasUw) && charts.monthlyData.length
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:200px"><canvas id="execMomVol"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log or UW Sheet')}
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">SLA Compliance Trend (Month-over-Month)</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Journey TAT % vs UW Queue TAT % by month</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit && charts.monthlyData.length
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:200px"><canvas id="execMomSla"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Month-over-Month Table -->
<div class="data-table-wrap">
  <div class="data-table-header">
    <div><div class="data-table-title">Month-over-Month Summary</div><div class="data-table-meta">Performance breakdown by period</div></div>
  </div>
  ${charts.monthlyData.length ? `
  <div class="data-table-scroll">
    <table class="dt" id="execMomTable">
      <thead><tr>
        <th>Period</th><th>Total Proposals</th><th>UW Actioned</th>
        <th>Journey TAT Breaches</th><th>Journey Compliance%</th>
        <th>UW Queue Breaches</th><th>UW Queue Compliance%</th>
      </tr></thead>
      <tbody>
        ${charts.monthlyData.map((r,i) => `
        <tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
          <td style="font-weight:600">${fmtMonth(r.month)}</td>
          <td>${u.fmtNum(r.proposals)}</td>
          <td>${u.fmtNum(r.uwActioned)}</td>
          <td><span class="badge red">${u.fmtNum(r.journeyBreaches)}</span></td>
          <td><span style="color:${r.journeyCompliancePct>=70?'#22c55e':r.journeyCompliancePct>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444'};font-weight:700">${u.fmtPct(r.journeyCompliancePct)}</span></td>
          <td><span class="badge red">${u.fmtNum(r.uwQueueBreaches)}</span></td>
          <td><span style="color:${r.uwQueueCompliancePct>=70?'#22c55e':r.uwQueueCompliancePct>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444'};font-weight:700">${u.fmtPct(r.uwQueueCompliancePct)}</span></td>
        </tr>`).join('')}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>` : `<div style="padding:30px;text-align:center;color:#64748b;font-size:12px">No monthly data available</div>`}
</div>`;

    // ── RENDER CHARTS ────────────────────────────────────────
    if (hasUw) {
      renderDailyOutput(charts.dailyOutput);
      renderActionMix(charts.actionMix);
    }
    if ((hasAudit || hasUw) && charts.monthlyData.length) {
      renderMomVolume(charts.monthlyData);
    }
    if (hasAudit && charts.monthlyData.length) {
      renderMomSla(charts.monthlyData);
    }
    window.utils.makeSortable('execMomTable');
  }

  // ── HELPER ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  function fmtMonth(m) {
    if (!m) return '-';
    const [y, mo] = m.split('-');
    const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
    return `${months[parseInt(mo,10)-1]} ${y}`;
  }

  // ── CHART: DAILY UW OUTPUT ────────────────────────────────
  function renderDailyOutput(data) {
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('execDailyOut');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('execDailyOut'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r=>r.date);
    const values = data.map(r=>r.actions);
    // 7-day rolling average
    const avg7 = values.map((_,i) => {
      const slice = values.slice(Math.max(0,i-6), i+1);
      return Math.round(slice.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0)/slice.length);
    });
    const peakVal = Math.max(...values);
    const peakIdx = values.indexOf(peakVal);
    // Weekend detection (0=Sun, 6=Sat)
    const wkend = labels.map(d => { const day = new Date(d).getDay(); return (day===0||day===6) ? 1 : 0; });
    const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(labels.length/12));
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type: 'line',
      data: { labels, datasets: [
        { label:'Daily Actions', data:values, borderColor:'#3b82f6', backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.07)', borderWidth:2, pointRadius: wkend.map(w=>w?4:2), pointBackgroundColor: wkend.map(w=>w?'rgba(100,116,139,0.4)':'#3b82f6'), fill:true, tension:0.3 },
        { label:'7-day Avg', data:avg7, borderColor:'rgba(245,158,11,0.7)', borderWidth:1.5, borderDash:[5,4], pointRadius:0, fill:false }
      ]},
      options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false, interaction:{intersect:false,mode:'index'},
        plugins: { legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11},padding:14}},
          tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,
            callbacks:{title:i=>u.fmtDate(i[0].label),
              label:c=>c.datasetIndex===0?` ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} actions${c.dataIndex===peakIdx?' 🔝 Peak':''}`+( wkend[c.dataIndex]?' (Weekend)':'')
                :` 7-day avg: ${c.raw}`}}},
        scales: {
          x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:10},maxRotation:45,callback:(v,i)=>i%step===0?u.fmtDate(labels[i]):''}},
          y:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}},beginAtZero:true}
        }
      }
    });
  }

  // ── CHART: ACTION TYPE MIX DONUT ──────────────────────────
  function renderActionMix(mix) {
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('execActionMix');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('execActionMix'); if (!cvs) return;
    const keys = ['accept','rejected','counter_offer','additional_info','additional_test','telemer','ppc','refer_to_cops','rulebook_refund'];
    const labels = ['Accept','Rejected','Counter Offer','Additional Info','Additional Test','TeleMER/VideoMER','PPC Raised','Refer to COPs','Rulebook Refund'];
    const values = keys.map(k=>mix[k]||0);
    const total  = values.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);
    const colors = labels.map(l=>u.ACTION_COLOURS[l]||'#64748b');

    new Chart(cvs, {
      type:'doughnut',
      data:{labels,datasets:[{data:values,backgroundColor:colors,borderWidth:0,hoverBorderWidth:2,hoverBorderColor:'#fff'}]},
      options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,cutout:'60%',plugins:{
        legend:{display:false},
        tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,
          callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} (${total?Math.round(c.raw/total*100):0}%)`}}
      }}
    });

    const leg = document.getElementById('execActionLegend');
    if (leg) {
      const topItems = keys.map((k,i)=>({label:labels[i],val:values[i],color:colors[i]})).filter(x=>x.val>0).sort((a,b)=>b.val-a.val);
      leg.innerHTML = `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:4px 16px">` +
        topItems.map(x=>`
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px">
            <span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:${x.color};flex-shrink:0;display:inline-block"></span>
            <span style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;flex:1;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${x.label}</span>
            <span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary)">${u.fmtNum(x.val)}</span>
            <span style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;width:32px;text-align:right">${total?Math.round(x.val/total*100):0}%</span>
          </div>`).join('') + '</div>';
    }
  }

  // ── CHART: MONTH-OVER-MONTH VOLUME ────────────────────────
  function renderMomVolume(data) {
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('execMomVol');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('execMomVol'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r=>fmtMonth(r.month));
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type:'bar',
      data:{labels,datasets:[
        {label:'Total Proposals',data:data.map(r=>r.proposals),backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.7)',borderColor:'#3b82f6',borderWidth:1,borderRadius:4},
        {label:'UW Actioned',    data:data.map(r=>r.uwActioned), backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.7)', borderColor:'#22c55e',borderWidth:1,borderRadius:4}
      ]},
      options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,interaction:{intersect:false,mode:'index'},
        plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11},padding:14}},
          tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.dataset.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)}`}}},
        scales:{x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}}},
          y:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}},beginAtZero:true}}}
    });
  }

  // ── CHART: MONTH-OVER-MONTH SLA ───────────────────────────
  function renderMomSla(data) {
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('execMomSla');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('execMomSla'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r=>fmtMonth(r.month));
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type:'line',
      data:{labels,datasets:[
        {label:'Journey TAT Compliance%',   data:data.map(r=>r.journeyCompliancePct),  borderColor:'#3b82f6',backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)',borderWidth:2,pointRadius:4,fill:true,tension:0.3},
        {label:'UW Queue TAT Compliance%',  data:data.map(r=>r.uwQueueCompliancePct), borderColor:'#22c55e',backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.05)',  borderWidth:2,pointRadius:4,fill:false,tension:0.3}
      ]},
      options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,interaction:{intersect:false,mode:'index'},
        plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11},padding:14}},
          tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.dataset.label}: ${u.fmtPct(c.raw)}`}}},
        scales:{
          x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}}},
          y:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11},callback:v=>v+'%'},min:0,max:100,beginAtZero:true}
        }}
    });
  }

  return { render };
})();

FILE: src/app/tabs/pipeline.js

'use strict';
/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Pipeline Tab Renderer
 */
window.tabPipeline = (function () {

  async function render(source, filters) {
    const el = document.getElementById('tab-pipeline');
    if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML = window.utils.loading();

    let data;
    try { data = await window.protrack.pipeline.getStats(source, filters); }
    catch (e) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error loading Pipeline data',e.message); return; }
    if (data.error) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',data.error); return; }

    const { kpi, hasAudit, hasUw, charts, dateRange } = data;
    const u = window.utils;

    const dateSub = dateRange && dateRange.from
      ? `Data period: <span>${u.fmtDate(dateRange.from)} → ${u.fmtDate(dateRange.to)}</span>`
      : '<span>Current Upload Session</span>';

    const showAP = kpi.auditPending > 0;
    const showUP = kpi.uwActionPending > 0;
    const ncards = 2 + (showAP?1:0) + (showUP?1:0);

    el.innerHTML = `
<div class="page-header">
  <div class="page-title">🔄 Pipeline / Funnel</div>
  <div class="page-subtitle">${dateSub}</div>
</div>

<div class="kpi-grid kpi-grid-${ncards}">
  <div class="kpi-card highlight">
    <div class="kpi-label">Total Proposals <span class="kpi-icon">📋</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value">${u.fmtNum(kpi.totalProposals)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Unique proposal IDs in dataset</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Fully Tracked <span class="kpi-icon">✅</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value green">${u.fmtNum(kpi.fullyTracked)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Present in both files</div>
  </div>
  ${showAP ? `<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">Audit Pending <span class="kpi-icon">📋</span></div><div class="kpi-value amber">${u.fmtNum(kpi.auditPending)}</div><div class="kpi-sub">In UW file · no audit trail yet</div></div>` : ''}
  ${showUP ? `<div class="kpi-card"><div class="kpi-label">UW Action Pending <span class="kpi-icon">👤</span></div><div class="kpi-value amber">${u.fmtNum(kpi.uwActionPending)}</div><div class="kpi-sub">In audit · no UW action recorded</div></div>` : ''}
</div>

<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Business Type Distribution</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Proposal volume split by business category</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:240px"><canvas id="chartBizType"></canvas></div><div id="bizLegend" style="margin-top:12px"></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Queue Origin Distribution</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Where proposals arrive from before reaching UW Queue</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(160, charts.fromBucketData.length * 40)}px"><canvas id="chartFromBucket"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
</div>

<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Current Queue Distribution</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Where proposals currently sit in the pipeline</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(120, charts.currentBucketData.length * 40)}px"><canvas id="chartCurrBucket"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Proposal Level Status</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Current standing of proposals in the system</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(120, charts.statusData.length * 40)}px"><canvas id="chartStatus"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
</div>

<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-1">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Daily Proposal Inward Trend</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Daily intake volume${dateRange&&dateRange.from?' · '+u.fmtDate(dateRange.from)+' to '+u.fmtDate(dateRange.to):''}</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:220px"><canvas id="chartDailyTrend"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
</div>

<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-1">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Product Breakdown (Top 10)</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Ranked proposal volume by insurance product</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasAudit
      ? `<div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(220, charts.productData.length * 36)}px"><canvas id="chartProduct"></canvas></div>`
      : u.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}
  </div>
</div>`;

    if (!hasAudit) return;

    // Render all charts
    renderBizDonut(charts.bizTypeData, kpi.totalProposals);
    renderHBar('chartFromBucket', charts.fromBucketData, 'bucket');
    renderHBar('chartCurrBucket', charts.currentBucketData, 'bucket');
    renderHBar('chartStatus', charts.statusData, 'status');
    renderDailyLine(charts.dailyTrendData, dateRange);
    renderProductHBar(charts.productData, kpi.totalProposals);
  }

  // ── DONUT: BUSINESS TYPE ──────────────────────────────────
  function renderBizDonut(data, total) {
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('chartBizType');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('chartBizType'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r => r.business_type);
    const counts = data.map(r => r.cnt);
    const colors = labels.map((l,i) => u.BIZ_COLOURS[l] || u.CHART_COLOURS[i % u.CHART_COLOURS.length]);
    const tot = data.reduce((s,r) => s+r.cnt, 0);
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type: 'doughnut',
      data: { labels, datasets: [{ data: counts, backgroundColor: colors, borderWidth: 0, hoverBorderWidth: 2, hoverBorderColor: '#fff' }] },
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, cutout: '62%',
        plugins: {
          legend: { display: false },
          tooltip: { backgroundColor: '#1e1e3c', borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderWidth: 1,
            callbacks: { label: c => ` ${c.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} (${(c.raw/tot*100).toFixed(1)}%)` } }
        }
      }
    });
    const leg = document.getElementById('bizLegend');
    if (leg) leg.innerHTML = data.map((r,i) => `
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04)">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
          <span style="width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:50%;background:${colors[i]};display:inline-block;flex-shrink:0"></span>
          <span style="font-size:12px;color:#94a3b8">${u.esc(r.business_type)}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
          <span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary)">${u.fmtNum(r.cnt)}</span>
          <div style="width:50px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.06);border-radius:2px;height:3px">
            <div style="width:${Math.round(r.cnt/tot*100)}%;height:100%;border-radius:2px;background:${colors[i]}"></div>
          </div>
          <span style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;width:36px;text-align:right">${(r.cnt/tot*100).toFixed(1)}%</span>
        </div>
      </div>`).join('');
  }

  // ── HORIZONTAL BAR ────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderHBar(id, data, labelKey) {
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart(id);
    const cvs = document.getElementById(id); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r => r[labelKey]);
    const values = data.map(r => r.cnt);
    const colors = labels.map((l,i) => u.CHART_COLOURS[i % u.CHART_COLOURS.length]);
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type: 'bar',
      data: { labels, datasets: [{ label: 'Proposals', data: values, backgroundColor: colors.map(c=>c+'cc'), borderColor: colors, borderWidth: 1, borderRadius: 4, borderSkipped: false }] },
      options: {
        indexAxis: 'y', responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        plugins: { legend: { display: false }, tooltip: { backgroundColor: '#1e1e3c', borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderWidth: 1, callbacks: { label: c => ` ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} proposals` } } },
        scales: { x: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }, ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 11 } } }, y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { size: 11 } } } }
      }
    });
  }

  // ── LINE: DAILY TREND ─────────────────────────────────────
  function renderDailyLine(data, dateRange) {
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('chartDailyTrend');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('chartDailyTrend'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r => r.date);
    const values = data.map(r => r.cnt);
    const avg = Math.round(values.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0)/values.length);
    const peakVal = Math.max(...values);
    const peakIdx = values.indexOf(peakVal);
    const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(labels.length / 10));
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type: 'line',
      data: { labels, datasets: [
        { label: 'Daily Proposals', data: values, borderColor: '#3b82f6', backgroundColor: 'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)', borderWidth: 2, pointRadius: 2, pointHoverRadius: 5, fill: true, tension: 0.3 },
        { label: `Avg ${avg}/day`, data: values.map(()=>avg), borderColor: 'rgba(148,163,184,0.4)', borderWidth: 1, borderDash: [6,4], pointRadius: 0, fill: false }
      ]},
      options: {
        responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false, interaction: { intersect: false, mode: 'index' },
        plugins: {
          legend: { labels: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { size: 11 }, padding: 16 } },
          tooltip: { backgroundColor: '#1e1e3c', borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderWidth: 1,
            callbacks: { title: i => u.fmtDate(i[0].label), label: c => c.datasetIndex===0 ? ` ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} proposals${c.dataIndex===peakIdx?' 🔝 Peak':''}` : ` Avg: ${avg}` } }
        },
        scales: {
          x: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }, ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 10 }, maxRotation: 45, callback: (v,i) => i%step===0 ? u.fmtDate(labels[i]) : '' } },
          y: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }, ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 11 } }, beginAtZero: true }
        }
      }
    });
  }

  // ── HORIZONTAL BAR: PRODUCT TOP 10 ───────────────────────
  function renderProductHBar(data, total) {
    if (!data || !data.length) return;
    const u = window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('chartProduct');
    const cvs = document.getElementById('chartProduct'); if (!cvs) return;
    const labels = data.map(r => r.product_name);
    const values = data.map(r => r.cnt);
    new Chart(cvs, {
      type: 'bar',
      data: { labels, datasets: [{ label: 'Proposals', data: values, backgroundColor: 'rgba(59,130,246,0.7)', borderColor: '#3b82f6', borderWidth: 1, borderRadius: 4, borderSkipped: false }] },
      options: {
        indexAxis: 'y', responsive: true, maintainAspectRatio: false,
        plugins: { legend: { display: false }, tooltip: { backgroundColor: '#1e1e3c', borderColor: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)', borderWidth: 1, callbacks: { label: c => ` ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} (${(c.raw/total*100).toFixed(1)}%)` } } },
        scales: { x: { grid: { color: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)' }, ticks: { color: '#64748b', font: { size: 11 } } }, y: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { color: '#94a3b8', font: { size: 11 } } } }
      }
    });
  }

  return { render };
})();


================================================================================
FILE: src/app/tabs/uw.js

'use strict';
/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - UW Productivity Tab Renderer
 */
window.tabUw = (function () {
  let _state = { source:'history', filters:{}, uwNames:[], pendingPage:1, pendingTotal:0, pendingThreshold:10 };

  async function render(source, filters) {
    const el = document.getElementById('tab-uw'); if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML = window.utils.loading();
    _state.source=source; _state.filters=filters;

    let data;
    try { data = await window.protrack.uw.getStats(source, filters); }
    catch(e) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',e.message); return; }
    if (data.error) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Query Error',data.error); return; }
    if (!data.hasUw) { el.innerHTML = buildShell(false) + window.utils.uploadRequired('UW Productivity Sheet'); return; }

    const u=window.utils;
    const { kpi, summaryRows, acceptRateChart, actionMix, bizByUw, dailyAll, pendingProposals, pendingTotal, pendingThreshold, uwNames } = data;
    _state.uwNames=uwNames; _state.pendingTotal=pendingTotal; _state.pendingThreshold=pendingThreshold;

    const ptColor = pct => pct===0?'green':pct<=pendingThreshold?'amber':'red';
    const arColor = pct => pct>=50?'#22c55e':pct>=30?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444';

    // UW dropdown HTML
    const uwOpts = ['<option value="ALL">All UWs (Team Total)</option>', ...uwNames.map(n=>`<option value="${u.esc(n)}">${u.esc(n)}</option>`)].join('');

    el.innerHTML = `
<div class="page-header"><div class="page-title">👥 UW Productivity</div><div class="page-subtitle"><span>Source: ${source==='current'?'Current Upload':'Full History'}</span></div></div>

<!-- KPI Row -->
<div class="kpi-grid kpi-grid-4">
  <div class="kpi-card highlight">
    <div class="kpi-label">Total Cases Actioned <span class="kpi-icon">⚡</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value">${u.fmtNum(kpi.totalActioned)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">${u.fmtNum(kpi.clearTeam)} clear · ${u.fmtNum(kpi.pendingTeam)} pending</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Pending Cases <span class="kpi-icon">⏳</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value amber">${u.fmtNum(kpi.pendingTeam)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">Awaiting final UW decision</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Team Accept Rate <span class="kpi-icon">✅</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value" style="color:${arColor(kpi.acceptRate)}">${u.fmtPct(kpi.acceptRate)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">(Accept + Counter Offer) / Clear</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Most Active UW <span class="kpi-icon">🏆</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:20px;line-height:1.2;padding-top:2px">${u.esc(kpi.mostActive.name||'-')}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">${u.fmtNum(kpi.mostActive.actions)} actions · ${u.fmtPct(kpi.mostActive.acceptRate)} accept rate</div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- UW Summary Table -->
<div class="data-table-wrap" style="margin-bottom:20px">
  <div class="data-table-header"><div><div class="data-table-title">UW Summary</div><div class="data-table-meta">${summaryRows.length} underwriters · Click columns to sort</div></div></div>
  <div class="data-table-scroll">
    <table class="dt" id="uwSummaryTable">
      <thead><tr>
        <th>UW Name</th><th>Total Actions</th><th>Unique Proposals</th>
        <th>Clear</th><th>Pending</th><th>Pending Rate%</th>
        <th>Accept</th><th>Rejected</th><th>Counter Offer</th>
        <th>Add. Info</th><th>Add. Test</th><th>TeleMER</th>
        <th>PPC</th><th>Ref. COPs</th><th>Rulebook Ref.</th><th>Accept Rate%</th>
      </tr></thead>
      <tbody>
        ${summaryRows.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
          <td style="font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap">${u.esc(r.uw_name)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.total_actions)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.unique_proposals)}</td>
          <td class="text-right"><span class="badge green">${u.fmtNum(r.clear)}</span></td>
          <td class="text-right"><span class="badge ${r.pending>0?'amber':'green'}">${u.fmtNum(r.pending)}</span></td>
          <td class="text-right"><span class="badge ${ptColor(r.pending_rate)}">${u.fmtPct(r.pending_rate)}</span></td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.accept)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.rejected)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.counter_offer)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.additional_info)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.additional_test)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.telemer)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.ppc)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.refer_to_cops)}</td>
          <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.rulebook_refund)}</td>
          <td class="text-right" style="font-weight:700;color:${arColor(r.accept_rate)}">${u.fmtPct(r.accept_rate)}</td>
        </tr>`).join('')}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Accept Rate + Action Mix -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Accept Rate by UW</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">${summaryRows.length} underwriters · Team avg ${u.fmtPct(kpi.acceptRate)} · Ranked lowest to highest</div>
    </div></div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-bottom:12px">
      <span class="badge green">≥ 50%</span><span class="badge amber">30–49%</span><span class="badge red">&lt; 30%</span>
    </div>
    <div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(220,acceptRateChart.length*28)}px"><canvas id="uwAcceptRate"></canvas></div>
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header">
      <div><div class="chart-card-title">Action Type Mix</div><div class="chart-card-subtitle" id="actionMixSub">Team-wide</div></div>
      <div class="chart-card-controls"><select class="ctrl-select" id="actionMixUw">${uwOpts}</select></div>
    </div>
    <div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:220px"><canvas id="uwActionMix"></canvas></div>
    <div id="uwActionLegend" style="margin-top:10px;font-size:11px"></div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Business Type + Daily Output -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header">
      <div><div class="chart-card-title">Business Type Mix</div><div class="chart-card-subtitle" id="bizTypeSub">All UWs</div></div>
      <div class="chart-card-controls"><select class="ctrl-select" id="bizTypeUw">${uwOpts}</select></div>
    </div>
    <div id="bizTypeChartWrap" style="height:260px;position:relative"><canvas id="uwBizType"></canvas></div>
    <div id="uwBizLegend" style="margin-top:10px"></div>
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header">
      <div><div class="chart-card-title">Daily Team Output</div><div class="chart-card-subtitle" id="dailyOutSub">All UWs</div></div>
      <div class="chart-card-controls">
        <div class="toggle-group">
          <button class="toggle-btn active" id="toggleActions">Actions</button>
          <button class="toggle-btn" id="toggleProposals">Proposals</button>
        </div>
        <select class="ctrl-select" id="dailyOutUw" style="margin-left:8px">${uwOpts}</select>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:240px"><canvas id="uwDailyOut"></canvas></div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Pending Proposals Table -->
<div class="data-table-wrap">
  <div class="data-table-header">
    <div>
      <div class="data-table-title" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
        ⚠️ ${u.fmtNum(pendingTotal)} Pending Proposals
        <span class="badge amber">No UW action taken yet</span>
      </div>
      <div class="data-table-meta">Proposals awaiting a final decision</div>
    </div>
    <button class="btn btn-download btn-sm" id="btnDownloadPending">⬇ Download Excel</button>
  </div>
  <div class="data-table-scroll">
    <table class="dt"><thead><tr>
      <th>Proposal No.</th><th>UW Name</th><th>Business Type</th><th>In Queue Since</th>
    </tr></thead>
    <tbody id="pendingTbody">${renderPendingRows(pendingProposals)}</tbody></table>
  </div>
  <div id="pendingPagination"></div>
</div>`;

    // Render charts
    u.makeSortable('uwSummaryTable');
    renderAcceptRate(acceptRateChart, kpi.acceptRate);
    renderActionMixDonut('uwActionMix','uwActionLegend','actionMixSub', actionMix,'Team-wide');
    renderBizType(bizByUw, 'ALL');
    renderDailyOut(dailyAll, 'ALL', 'actions');
    renderPendingPagination(1, pendingTotal);

    // Wire interactive controls
    document.getElementById('actionMixUw').addEventListener('change', async function() {
      const uwName = this.value;
      const mix = await window.protrack.uw.getActionTypeMix(_state.source, _state.filters, uwName);
      renderActionMixDonut('uwActionMix','uwActionLegend','actionMixSub', mix, uwName==='ALL'?'Team-wide':uwName);
    });

    document.getElementById('bizTypeUw').addEventListener('change', async function() {
      const uwName = this.value;
      const result = await window.protrack.uw.getBusinessTypeMix(_state.source, _state.filters, uwName);
      renderBizType(result.rows, uwName);
    });

    // ── DAILY OUTPUT — set cache BEFORE wiring event listeners ────────
    // So the cache is guaranteed warm when any toggle fires
    _state._dailyRows    = dailyAll;
    _state._dailyTeamAvg = null;     // actions-based team avg (populated when UW is selected)
    _state.dailyMetric   = 'actions';
    _state._currentDailyUw = 'ALL';

    document.getElementById('toggleActions').addEventListener('click', function() {
      this.classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('toggleProposals').classList.remove('active');
      _state.dailyMetric = 'actions';
      // Actions: show team avg line (it's an actions metric so the scale matches)
      renderDailyOut(_state._dailyRows, _state._currentDailyUw, 'actions', _state._dailyTeamAvg);
    });
    document.getElementById('toggleProposals').addEventListener('click', function() {
      this.classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('toggleActions').classList.remove('active');
      _state.dailyMetric = 'proposals';
      // Proposals: pass null for teamAvg — _dailyTeamAvg is an actions count (e.g. 1142),
      // showing it on a proposals chart (max ~115) collapses the line to near-zero
      renderDailyOut(_state._dailyRows, _state._currentDailyUw, 'proposals', null);
    });

    document.getElementById('dailyOutUw').addEventListener('change', async function() {
      const uwName = this.value;
      _state._currentDailyUw = uwName;
      const result = await window.protrack.uw.getDailyOutput(_state.source, _state.filters, uwName);
      _state._dailyRows    = result.rows;
      _state._dailyTeamAvg = result.teamAvg;  // actions avg — only valid for Actions metric
      // Only include teamAvg when metric is 'actions' (avoids scale distortion on proposals)
      const teamAvg = _state.dailyMetric === 'proposals' ? null : result.teamAvg;
      renderDailyOut(result.rows, uwName, _state.dailyMetric, teamAvg);
    });

    document.getElementById('btnDownloadPending').addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const rows = await window.protrack.uw.exportPending(_state.source, _state.filters);
      await window.protrack.export.toExcel('pending_proposals', rows, 'Pending_Proposals');
    });
  }

  // ── PENDING HELPERS ──────────────────────────────────────
  function renderPendingRows(rows) {
    if (!rows||!rows.length) return '<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#64748b">No pending proposals</td></tr>';
    return rows.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
      <td class="mono">${window.utils.esc(r.proposal_no)}</td>
      <td>${window.utils.esc(r.uw_name)}</td>
      <td><span class="badge blue">${window.utils.esc(r.business_type||'-')}</span></td>
      <td>${window.utils.fmtDate(r.in_queue_since)}</td>
    </tr>`).join('');
  }

  function renderPendingPagination(page, total) {
    const perPage=10, totalPages=Math.ceil(total/perPage);
    window.utils.renderPagination('pendingPagination',{page,totalPages,totalRows:total,perPage}, async (p)=>{
      _state.pendingPage=p;
      const result = await window.protrack.uw.getPendingProposals(_state.source,_state.filters,p);
      document.getElementById('pendingTbody').innerHTML = renderPendingRows(result.rows);
      renderPendingPagination(p, total);
    });
  }

  // ── CHART: ACCEPT RATE BAR ───────────────────────────────
  function renderAcceptRate(data, teamAvg) {
    const u=window.utils; u.destroyChart('uwAcceptRate');
    const cvs=document.getElementById('uwAcceptRate'); if (!cvs||!data.length) return;
    const labels=data.map(r=>r.uw_name);
    const values=data.map(r=>r.accept_rate);
    const colors=values.map(v=>v>=50?'rgba(34,197,94,0.75)':v>=30?'rgba(245,158,11,0.75)':'rgba(239,68,68,0.75)');
    new Chart(cvs,{type:'bar',data:{labels,datasets:[{label:'Accept Rate%',data:values,backgroundColor:colors,borderColor:colors.map(c=>c.replace('0.75','1')),borderWidth:1,borderRadius:3,borderSkipped:false}]},
      options:{indexAxis:'y',responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{
        legend:{display:false},
        tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${u.fmtPct(c.raw)} (${data[c.dataIndex].clear} clear cases)`}},
        annotation:{annotations:{target:{type:'line',xMin:50,xMax:50,borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.3)',borderWidth:1.5,borderDash:[4,4],label:{content:'Target 50%',display:true,color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:10}}}}}
      },
      scales:{x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11},callback:v=>v+'%'},min:0,max:100},
              y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11}}}}
    }});
  }

  // ── CHART: ACTION TYPE MIX DONUT ─────────────────────────
  function renderActionMixDonut(canvasId, legendId, subId, mix, label) {
    const u=window.utils; u.destroyChart(canvasId);
    const cvs=document.getElementById(canvasId); if (!cvs) return;
    const sub=document.getElementById(subId); if (sub) sub.textContent=label;
    const keys=['accept','rejected','counter_offer','additional_info','additional_test','telemer','ppc','refer_to_cops','rulebook_refund'];
    const labels=['Accept','Rejected','Counter Offer','Additional Info','Additional Test','TeleMER/VideoMER','PPC Raised','Refer to COPs','Rulebook Refund'];
    const values=keys.map(k=>mix[k]||0);
    const total=values.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);
    const colors=labels.map(l=>u.ACTION_COLOURS[l]||'#64748b');
    new Chart(cvs,{type:'doughnut',data:{labels,datasets:[{data:values,backgroundColor:colors,borderWidth:0,hoverBorderWidth:2,hoverBorderColor:'#fff'}]},
      options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,cutout:'60%',plugins:{legend:{display:false},
        tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} (${total?Math.round(c.raw/total*100):0}%)`}}}}});
    const leg=document.getElementById(legendId);
    if (leg) leg.innerHTML=`<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:3px 12px">`+
      keys.map((k,i)=>({label:labels[i],val:values[i],color:colors[i]})).filter(x=>x.val>0).sort((a,b)=>b.val-a.val)
      .map(x=>`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:${x.color};flex-shrink:0;display:inline-block"></span><span style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:10px;flex:1;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">${x.label}</span><span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary)">${u.fmtNum(x.val)}</span></div>`)
      .join('')+'</div>';
  }

  // ── CHART: BUSINESS TYPE (Stacked bar or Donut) ──────────
  function renderBizType(rows, uwName) {
    const u=window.utils;
    u.destroyChart('uwBizType');
    const cvs=document.getElementById('uwBizType'); if (!cvs||!rows||!rows.length) return;
    const sub=document.getElementById('bizTypeSub'); if (sub) sub.textContent=uwName==='ALL'?'All UWs (stacked)':uwName;
    const leg=document.getElementById('uwBizLegend');

    if (uwName==='ALL') {
      // Stacked horizontal bar: each row = one UW, segments = business types
      const uwList=[...new Set(rows.map(r=>r.uw_name))].sort();
      const bizTypes=[...new Set(rows.map(r=>r.business_type))];
      const datasets=bizTypes.map(bt=>({
        label:bt, data:uwList.map(un=>(rows.find(r=>r.uw_name===un&&r.business_type===bt)||{cnt:0}).cnt),
        backgroundColor:(u.BIZ_COLOURS[bt]||'#64748b')+'cc', borderColor:u.BIZ_COLOURS[bt]||'#64748b', borderWidth:1, borderRadius:2, borderSkipped:false
      }));
      const h=Math.max(200,uwList.length*32);
      cvs.parentElement.style.height=h+'px';
      new Chart(cvs,{type:'bar',data:{labels:uwList,datasets},
        options:{indexAxis:'y',responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
          plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:10},padding:10}},tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,mode:'index',callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.dataset.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)}`}}},
          scales:{x:{stacked:true,grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:10}}},y:{stacked:true,grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11}}}}}});
      if (leg) leg.innerHTML='';
    } else {
      // Donut for single UW
      const filtered=rows.filter(r=>r.uw_name===uwName);
      const labels=filtered.map(r=>r.business_type);
      const values=filtered.map(r=>r.cnt);
      const total=values.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);
      const colors=labels.map(l=>u.BIZ_COLOURS[l]||'#64748b');
      cvs.parentElement.style.height='240px';
      new Chart(cvs,{type:'doughnut',data:{labels,datasets:[{data:values,backgroundColor:colors,borderWidth:0,hoverBorderWidth:2,hoverBorderColor:'#fff'}]},
        options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,cutout:'62%',plugins:{legend:{display:false},
          tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${c.label}: ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)} (${Math.round(c.raw/total*100)}%)`}}}}});
      if (leg) leg.innerHTML=labels.map((l,i)=>`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;padding:3px 0"><span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:${colors[i]};display:inline-block"></span><span style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8">${u.esc(l)}</span><span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-left:auto">${u.fmtNum(values[i])}</span></div>`).join('');
    }
  }

  // ── CHART: DAILY OUTPUT ───────────────────────────────────
  function renderDailyOut(rows, uwName, metric, teamAvg) {
    const u=window.utils; u.destroyChart('uwDailyOut');
    const cvs=document.getElementById('uwDailyOut'); if (!cvs) return;
    // Use passed rows if provided, fall back to cached rows, then empty array
    const data = (rows || _state._dailyRows || []).filter(r=>r.date);
    if (!data.length) return;
    const sub=document.getElementById('dailyOutSub'); if (sub) sub.textContent=uwName==='ALL'?'All UWs':uwName;
    const labels=data.map(r=>r.date);
    const values=data.map(r=>metric==='proposals'?r.proposals:r.actions);
    const avg7=values.map((_,i)=>{const sl=values.slice(Math.max(0,i-6),i+1);return Math.round(sl.reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0)/sl.length);});
    const peak=Math.max(...values), peakIdx=values.indexOf(peak);
    const wkend=labels.map(d=>{const day=new Date(d).getDay();return(day===0||day===6)?1:0;});
    const step=Math.max(1,Math.floor(labels.length/12));
    const datasets=[
      {label:metric==='proposals'?'Unique Proposals':'Cases Actioned',data:values,borderColor:'#3b82f6',backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)',borderWidth:2,pointRadius:wkend.map(w=>w?4:2),pointBackgroundColor:wkend.map(w=>w?'rgba(100,116,139,0.4)':'#3b82f6'),fill:true,tension:0.3},
      {label:'7-day Avg',data:avg7,borderColor:'rgba(245,158,11,0.7)',borderWidth:1.5,borderDash:[5,4],pointRadius:0,fill:false}
    ];
    if (teamAvg!==null&&teamAvg!==undefined) {
      datasets.push({label:`Team Avg ${teamAvg}`,data:values.map(()=>teamAvg),borderColor:'rgba(148,163,184,0.4)',borderWidth:1,borderDash:[3,3],pointRadius:0,fill:false});
    }
    new Chart(cvs,{type:'line',data:{labels,datasets},
      options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,interaction:{intersect:false,mode:'index'},
        plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:10},padding:12}},
          tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,
            callbacks:{title:i=>u.fmtDate(i[0].label),label:c=>c.datasetIndex===0?` ${u.fmtNum(c.raw)}${c.dataIndex===peakIdx?' 🔝 Peak':''}`+(wkend[c.dataIndex]?' (Weekend)':'')
              :` ${c.dataset.label}: ${c.raw}`}}},
        scales:{x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:10},maxRotation:45,callback:(v,i)=>i%step===0?u.fmtDate(labels[i]):''}},
                y:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}},beginAtZero:true}}}});
  }

  function buildShell(hasData) {
    return `<div class="page-header"><div class="page-title">👥 UW Productivity</div></div>`;
  }

  return { render };
})();
