FILE: src/app/tabs/tat.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - TAT / SLA Tab Renderer
 */
window.tabTat = (function () {
  const DAY_CATS = ['0','1','2','3','4','5','More than 5'];
  let _state = { source:'history', filters:{}, matrixType:'journey', dayFilter:'all', drillPage:1, drillDayBucket:'all', drillBizType:'all' };

  async function render(source, filters) {
    const el = document.getElementById('tab-tat'); if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML = window.utils.loading();
    _state.source=source; _state.filters=filters;

    let data;
    try { data = await window.protrack.tat.getStats(source, filters); }
    catch(e) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',e.message); return; }
    if (data.error) { el.innerHTML = window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',data.error); return; }
    if (!data.hasAudit) { el.innerHTML = `<div class="page-header"><div class="page-title">⏱️ TAT / SLA Analysis</div></div>${window.utils.uploadRequired('Audit Log Report')}`; return; }

    const u = window.utils;
    const { kpi, jMatrix, uwMatrix, jTrend, qTrend, prodTat, uwPerfTable, datePeriod, slaThreshold, hasUw } = data;

    const dateSub = datePeriod && datePeriod.from
      ? `Data period: <span>${u.fmtDate(datePeriod.from)} → ${u.fmtDate(datePeriod.to)}</span>`
      : '<span>Current Upload Session</span>';

    const brc = pct => pct<20?'green':pct<=40?'amber':'red';
    const slaC = pct => pct>=70?'#22c55e':pct>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444';

    el.innerHTML = `
<div class="page-header"><div class="page-title">⏱️ TAT / SLA Analysis</div><div class="page-subtitle">${dateSub}</div></div>

<!-- KPI Cards -->
<div class="kpi-grid kpi-grid-4">
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Journey TAT Breaches <span class="kpi-icon">🛣️</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value red">${u.fmtNum(kpi.journeyBreaches)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub" style="color:${slaC(kpi.journeyCompliance)}">${u.fmtPct(kpi.journeyCompliance)} compliant · SLA = ${slaThreshold}d</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">UW Queue TAT Breaches <span class="kpi-icon">⏱️</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value red">${u.fmtNum(kpi.uwQueueBreaches)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub" style="color:${slaC(kpi.uwQueueCompliance)}">${u.fmtPct(kpi.uwQueueCompliance)} compliant · SLA = ${slaThreshold}d</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Highest Breach Rate UW <span class="kpi-icon">⚠️</span></div>
    ${hasUw&&kpi.highestBreachUw.uw_name
      ? `<div class="kpi-value red" style="font-size:18px;line-height:1.2">${u.esc(kpi.highestBreachUw.uw_name)}</div><div class="kpi-sub">${u.fmtPct(kpi.highestBreachUw.uw_queue_breach_rate)} breach rate · ${u.fmtNum(kpi.highestBreachUw.total_proposals)} proposals</div>`
      : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:16px;color:#475569">No data</div><div class="kpi-sub">Upload UW Sheet</div>`}
  </div>
  ${kpi.unattributed>0 ? `
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Unattributed Queue TAT <span class="kpi-icon">❓</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value amber">${u.fmtNum(kpi.unattributed)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">In UW Queue · no UW productivity record</div>
  </div>` : `
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Data Coverage <span class="kpi-icon">✅</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value green">100%</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">All UW Queue proposals attributed</div>
  </div>`}
</div>

<!-- TAT Matrix -->
<div class="chart-card" style="margin-bottom:20px">
  <div class="chart-card-header">
    <div><div class="chart-card-title">TAT Matrix</div><div class="chart-card-subtitle">Rows: Day Buckets · Cols: Business Types · Cells: Count (% of column)</div></div>
    <div class="chart-card-controls">
      <div class="toggle-group">
        <button class="toggle-btn active" id="matrixToggleJourney">Journey TAT</button>
        <button class="toggle-btn" id="matrixToggleUwQueue">UW Queue TAT</button>
      </div>
      <select class="ctrl-select" id="matrixDayFilter" style="margin-left:8px">
        <option value="all">All Days</option>
        ${DAY_CATS.map(d=>`<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`).join('')}
      </select>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div id="tatMatrixWrap" style="overflow-x:auto"></div>
</div>

<!-- SLA Compliance Trend -->
<div class="chart-card" style="margin-bottom:20px">
  <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
    <div class="chart-card-title">SLA Compliance Trend</div>
    <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Daily compliance % · Journey TAT vs UW Queue TAT</div>
  </div></div>
  <div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:220px"><canvas id="tatTrend"></canvas></div>
</div>

<!-- Product TAT + UW Performance -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2">
  <div class="chart-card">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">Product-wise Avg UW Queue TAT</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Average days in UW Queue by product (top 15)</div>
    </div></div>
    <div class="chart-canvas-wrap" style="height:${Math.max(200,prodTat.length*32)}px"><canvas id="tatProductBar"></canvas></div>
  </div>
  <div class="chart-card" style="overflow:auto">
    <div class="chart-card-header"><div>
      <div class="chart-card-title">UW Queue TAT Performance</div>
      <div class="chart-card-subtitle">Sorted by UW Queue Breach Rate% descending · Click to sort</div>
    </div></div>
    ${hasUw ? `
    <div style="overflow-x:auto">
      <table class="dt" id="uwPerfTable" style="font-size:11px">
        <thead><tr>
          <th>UW Name</th><th>Proposals</th>
          <th>Journey Breaches</th><th>Journey Rate%</th>
          <th>UW Queue Breaches</th><th>UW Queue Rate%</th>
          <th>Avg TAT</th><th>Max TAT</th>
        </tr></thead>
        <tbody>
          ${uwPerfTable.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
            <td style="font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap">${u.esc(r.uw_name)}</td>
            <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.total_proposals)}</td>
            <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.journey_breaches)}</td>
            <td class="text-right"><span class="badge ${brc(r.journey_breach_rate)}">${u.fmtPct(r.journey_breach_rate)}</span></td>
            <td class="text-right">${u.fmtNum(r.uw_queue_breaches)}</td>
            <td class="text-right"><span class="badge ${brc(r.uw_queue_breach_rate)}">${u.fmtPct(r.uw_queue_breach_rate)}</span></td>
            <td class="text-right">${u.fmtDays(r.avg_uw_tat)}</td>
            <td class="text-right">${u.fmtDays(r.max_uw_tat)}</td>
          </tr>`).join('')}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>` : u.uploadRequired('UW Productivity Sheet')}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Proposal Drill-Down -->
<div class="data-table-wrap" style="margin-top:20px">
  <div class="data-table-header">
    <div><div class="data-table-title">Proposal Drill-Down</div><div class="data-table-meta" id="drillMeta">All proposals</div></div>
    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
      <select class="ctrl-select" id="drillDayBucket">
        <option value="all">All Days</option>
        ${DAY_CATS.map(d=>`<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`).join('')}
      </select>
      <select class="ctrl-select" id="drillBizType">
        <option value="all">All Business Types</option>
      </select>
      <button class="btn btn-download btn-sm" id="btnDrillExport">⬇ Excel</button>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div style="overflow-x:auto">
    <table class="dt">
      <thead><tr><th>Proposal No.</th><th>Business Type</th><th>Product</th><th>Journey TAT</th><th>UW Queue TAT</th><th>SLA Status</th><th>Last UW</th></tr></thead>
      <tbody id="drillTbody"></tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  <div id="drillPagination"></div>
</div>`;

    // Render charts
    renderMatrix(jMatrix, uwMatrix, 'journey', 'all', slaThreshold);
    renderTrend(jTrend, qTrend, slaThreshold);
    renderProductBar(prodTat);
    u.makeSortable('uwPerfTable');
    loadDrillDown(1);

    // Populate business type dropdown for drill-down
    const bizTypes=[...new Set([...jMatrix.map(r=>r.business_type),...uwMatrix.map(r=>r.business_type)])].filter(Boolean).sort();
    const drillBiz=document.getElementById('drillBizType');
    bizTypes.forEach(bt=>{ const o=document.createElement('option'); o.value=o.textContent=bt; drillBiz.appendChild(o); });

    // Wire matrix toggle
    document.getElementById('matrixToggleJourney').addEventListener('click', function() {
      this.classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('matrixToggleUwQueue').classList.remove('active');
      _state.matrixType='journey';
      renderMatrix(jMatrix, uwMatrix, 'journey', _state.dayFilter, slaThreshold);
    });
    document.getElementById('matrixToggleUwQueue').addEventListener('click', function() {
      this.classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('matrixToggleJourney').classList.remove('active');
      _state.matrixType='uwqueue';
      renderMatrix(jMatrix, uwMatrix, 'uwqueue', _state.dayFilter, slaThreshold);
    });
    document.getElementById('matrixDayFilter').addEventListener('change', function() {
      _state.dayFilter=this.value;
      renderMatrix(jMatrix, uwMatrix, _state.matrixType, this.value, slaThreshold);
    });

    // Wire drill-down filters
    document.getElementById('drillDayBucket').addEventListener('change', function() { _state.drillDayBucket=this.value; loadDrillDown(1); });
    document.getElementById('drillBizType').addEventListener('change', function() { _state.drillBizType=this.value; loadDrillDown(1); });
    document.getElementById('btnDrillExport').addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const rows=await window.protrack.tat.exportDrillDown(_state.source, _state.filters);
      await window.protrack.export.toExcel('tat_drilldown', rows, 'TAT_DrillDown');
    });
  }

  // ── TAT MATRIX ───────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderMatrix(jData, qData, type, dayFilter, sla) {
    const data = type==='journey' ? jData : qData;
    const wrap = document.getElementById('tatMatrixWrap'); if (!wrap) return;
    const u = window.utils;

    const bizTypes = [...new Set(data.map(r=>r.business_type))].filter(Boolean).sort();
    let visibleDays = DAY_CATS;
    if (dayFilter && dayFilter!=='all') visibleDays=[dayFilter];

    // Remove empty rows for UW Queue (Day 5 hides when 0)
    const filtered = type==='uwqueue'
      ? visibleDays.filter(d=>d!=='5' || data.some(r=>r.day_cat==='5' && r.cnt>0))
      : visibleDays;

    // Column totals
    const colTotals = {};
    bizTypes.forEach(bt=>{ colTotals[bt]=data.filter(r=>r.business_type===bt).reduce((s,r)=>s+r.cnt,0); });
    const grandTotal=Object.values(colTotals).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);

    // SLA compliance per column
    const slaByCol={};
    bizTypes.forEach(bt=>{
      const within=data.filter(r=>r.business_type===bt&&(r.day_cat==='0'||r.day_cat==='1')).reduce((s,r)=>s+r.cnt,0);
      slaByCol[bt]=colTotals[bt]>0?Math.round(within/colTotals[bt]*1000)/10:0;
    });
    const grandSla=grandTotal>0?Math.round(data.filter(r=>r.day_cat==='0'||r.day_cat==='1').reduce((s,r)=>s+r.cnt,0)/grandTotal*1000)/10:0;

    const dayRowColor = d => d==='0'||d==='1'?'rgba(34,197,94,0.08)': d==='More than 5'?'rgba(239,68,68,0.08)':'rgba(245,158,11,0.06)';
    const dayTextColor= d => d==='0'||d==='1'?'#22c55e': d==='More than 5'?'#ef4444':'#f59e0b';

    wrap.innerHTML = `
      <table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:12px;min-width:600px">
        <thead>
          <tr style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.03)">
            <th style="text-align:left;padding:10px 14px;color:#64748b;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.06em;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)">Day Bucket</th>
            ${bizTypes.map(bt=>`<th style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;color:#64748b;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)">${u.esc(bt)}</th>`).join('')}
            <th style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;color:#3b82f6;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06);background:rgba(59,130,246,0.05)">Grand Total</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          ${filtered.map(d=>{
            const rowTotal=bizTypes.reduce((s,bt)=>s+(data.find(r=>r.business_type===bt&&r.day_cat===d)||{cnt:0}).cnt,0);
            if (rowTotal===0&&dayFilter==='all') return '';
            return `<tr style="background:${dayRowColor(d)};border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04)">
              <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-weight:700;color:${dayTextColor(d)}">${d}</td>
              ${bizTypes.map(bt=>{
                const row=data.find(r=>r.business_type===bt&&r.day_cat===d)||{cnt:0};
                const pct=colTotals[bt]>0?Math.round(row.cnt/colTotals[bt]*1000)/10:0;
                return `<td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;color:var(--text-primary)"><div style="font-weight:600">${u.fmtNum(row.cnt)}</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b">${u.fmtPct(pct)}</div></td>`;
              }).join('')}
              <td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;background:rgba(59,130,246,0.05)"><div style="font-weight:700;color:#3b82f6">${u.fmtNum(rowTotal)}</div></td>
            </tr>`;
          }).join('')}
        </tbody>
        <tfoot>
          <tr style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.03);border-top:2px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)">
            <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-weight:700;color:#94a3b8;font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase">SLA Compliance%</td>
            ${bizTypes.map(bt=>`<td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:700;color:${slaByCol[bt]>=70?'#22c55e':slaByCol[bt]>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444'}">${u.fmtPct(slaByCol[bt])}</td>`).join('')}
            <td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:800;color:${grandSla>=70?'#22c55e':grandSla>=50?'#f59e0b':'#ef4444'}">${u.fmtPct(grandSla)}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr style="border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.06)">
            <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-weight:700;color:#94a3b8;font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase">Grand Total</td>
            ${bizTypes.map(bt=>`<td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:600;color:#94a3b8">${u.fmtNum(colTotals[bt])}</td>`).join('')}
            <td style="text-align:right;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:800;color:#3b82f6;background:rgba(59,130,246,0.05)">${u.fmtNum(grandTotal)}</td>
          </tr>
        </tfoot>
      </table>`;
  }

  // ── SLA COMPLIANCE TREND ─────────────────────────────────
  function renderTrend(jTrend, qTrend, sla) {
    const u=window.utils; u.destroyChart('tatTrend');
    const cvs=document.getElementById('tatTrend'); if (!cvs) return;
    const allDates=[...new Set([...jTrend.map(r=>r.date),...qTrend.map(r=>r.date)])].filter(Boolean).sort();
    const jMap=Object.fromEntries(jTrend.map(r=>[r.date,r]));
    const qMap=Object.fromEntries(qTrend.map(r=>[r.date,r]));
    const step=Math.max(1,Math.floor(allDates.length/12));
    new Chart(cvs,{type:'line',data:{labels:allDates,datasets:[
      {label:'Journey TAT Compliance%',data:allDates.map(d=>{const r=jMap[d];return r&&r.tot>0?Math.round(r.ws/r.tot*1000)/10:null;}),borderColor:'#3b82f6',backgroundColor:'rgba(59,130,246,0.08)',borderWidth:2,pointRadius:2,fill:true,tension:0.3,spanGaps:true},
      {label:'UW Queue TAT Compliance%',data:allDates.map(d=>{const r=qMap[d];return r&&r.tot>0?Math.round(r.ws/r.tot*1000)/10:null;}),borderColor:'#22c55e',backgroundColor:'rgba(34,197,94,0.05)',borderWidth:2,pointRadius:2,fill:false,tension:0.3,spanGaps:true},
      {label:`SLA Target (${sla}d)`,data:allDates.map(()=>100),borderColor:'rgba(239,68,68,0.3)',borderWidth:1,borderDash:[4,4],pointRadius:0,fill:false}
    ]},options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,interaction:{intersect:false,mode:'index'},
      plugins:{legend:{labels:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11},padding:14}},
        tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>c.datasetIndex<2?` ${c.dataset.label}: ${u.fmtPct(c.raw)}`:null}}},
      scales:{x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:10},maxRotation:45,callback:(v,i)=>i%step===0?u.fmtDate(allDates[i]):''}},
              y:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11},callback:v=>v+'%'},min:0,max:100}}}});
  }

  // ── PRODUCT BAR ───────────────────────────────────────────
  function renderProductBar(data) {
    const u=window.utils; u.destroyChart('tatProductBar');
    const cvs=document.getElementById('tatProductBar'); if (!cvs||!data.length) return;
    new Chart(cvs,{type:'bar',data:{labels:data.map(r=>r.product_name),datasets:[{label:'Avg UW Queue TAT (days)',data:data.map(r=>r.avg_tat),backgroundColor:'rgba(99,102,241,0.7)',borderColor:'#6366f1',borderWidth:1,borderRadius:4,borderSkipped:false}]},
      options:{indexAxis:'y',responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{backgroundColor:'#1e1e3c',borderColor:'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)',borderWidth:1,callbacks:{label:c=>` ${u.fmtDays(c.raw)} avg · ${data[c.dataIndex].proposals} proposals`}}},
      scales:{x:{grid:{color:'rgba(255,255,255,0.04)'},ticks:{color:'#64748b',font:{size:11}}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:'#94a3b8',font:{size:11}}}}}});
  }

  // ── DRILL-DOWN ────────────────────────────────────────────
  async function loadDrillDown(page) {
    _state.drillPage=page;
    const u=window.utils;
    const result=await window.protrack.tat.getDrillDown(_state.source,_state.filters,{page,perPage:10,dayBucket:_state.drillDayBucket,bizType:_state.drillBizType});
    const meta=document.getElementById('drillMeta');
    if (meta) meta.textContent=`Showing ${u.fmtNum(result.total)} proposals · Day bucket: ${_state.drillDayBucket} · Biz type: ${_state.drillBizType}`;
    const tbody=document.getElementById('drillTbody');
    if (tbody) tbody.innerHTML=result.rows.length
      ? result.rows.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
          <td class="mono">${u.esc(r.proposal_no)}</td>
          <td><span class="badge blue">${u.esc(r.business_type||'-')}</span></td>
          <td style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8;max-width:180px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${u.esc(r.product_name||'-')}</td>
          <td class="text-right"><span style="font-weight:700;color:${Number(r.journey_days)>1?'#ef4444':'#22c55e'}">${u.fmtDays(r.journey_days)}</span></td>
          <td class="text-right"><span style="font-weight:700;color:${Number(r.uw_queue_days)>1?'#ef4444':'#22c55e'}">${u.fmtDays(r.uw_queue_days)}</span></td>
          <td><span class="badge ${r.sla_status==='Within SLA'?'green':'red'}">${r.sla_status}</span></td>
          <td style="font-size:11px">${u.esc(r.uw_name||'-')}</td>
        </tr>`).join('')
      : '<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#64748b">No proposals match the selected filters</td></tr>';
    u.renderPagination('drillPagination',{page,totalPages:result.totalPages,totalRows:result.total,perPage:10},loadDrillDown);
  }

  return { render };
})();


================================================================================
FILE: src/app/tabs/drilldown.js
================================================================================
'use strict';
window.tabDrilldown = (function () {
  let _source='history', _lastQuery='', _selectedProposal=null;

  async function render(source) {
    _source=source;
    const el=document.getElementById('tab-drilldown'); if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML=`
<div class="page-header"><div class="page-title">🔍 Proposal Drill-Down</div><div class="page-subtitle">Search by proposal number to view complete audit trail and UW history</div></div>
<div class="chart-card" style="margin-bottom:20px">
  <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px">
    <div class="search-wrap" style="flex:1">
      <span class="search-icon">🔍</span>
      <input class="search-input" id="ddSearch" placeholder="Enter full or partial proposal number (e.g. PPR/BT/28554/7030171549)" autocomplete="off">
    </div>
    <button class="btn btn-primary" id="ddSearchBtn">Search →</button>
  </div>
  <div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;margin-top:8px">💡 Press Enter or click Search. Partial numbers supported.</div>
  <div id="ddResults" style="margin-top:10px"></div>
</div>
<div id="ddDetail"></div>`;

    const input=document.getElementById('ddSearch');
    const btn=document.getElementById('ddSearchBtn');
    input.addEventListener('keydown', e=>{ if(e.key==='Enter') doSearch(); });
    btn.addEventListener('click', doSearch);
    if (_lastQuery) { input.value=_lastQuery; doSearch(); }
  }

  async function doSearch() {
    const input=document.getElementById('ddSearch');
    const query=(input?.value||'').trim();
    if (!query||query.length<2) { showMsg('Enter at least 2 characters to search.'); return; }
    _lastQuery=query;
    const results=await window.protrack.drilldown.search(_source, query);
    const resEl=document.getElementById('ddResults'); if (!resEl) return;

    if (!results||!results.length) {
      resEl.innerHTML=`<div style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;padding:8px 0">No proposals found matching "${window.utils.esc(query)}"</div>`;
      document.getElementById('ddDetail').innerHTML='';
      return;
    }

    if (results.length===1) {
      resEl.innerHTML=`<div style="color:#22c55e;font-size:12px;padding:4px 0">✅ 1 proposal found</div>`;
      loadDetail(results[0]);
    } else {
      resEl.innerHTML=`
        <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;margin-bottom:6px">${results.length} proposals found — select one:</div>
        <select class="ctrl-select" id="ddSelect" style="min-width:400px">
          ${results.map(p=>`<option value="${window.utils.esc(p)}">${window.utils.esc(p)}</option>`).join('')}
        </select>
        <button class="btn btn-secondary btn-sm" id="ddSelectBtn" style="margin-left:8px">View →</button>`;
      document.getElementById('ddSelectBtn').addEventListener('click',()=>{
        const sel=document.getElementById('ddSelect');
        if (sel) loadDetail(sel.value);
      });
    }
  }

  async function loadDetail(proposalNo) {
    _selectedProposal=proposalNo;
    const el=document.getElementById('ddDetail'); if (!el) return;
    el.innerHTML=window.utils.loading();
    const data=await window.protrack.drilldown.getDetail(_source, proposalNo);
    if (!data||data.notFound) { el.innerHTML=window.utils.emptyState('❓','Proposal Not Found',`No data found for ${proposalNo}`); return; }
    if (data.error) { el.innerHTML=window.utils.emptyState('❌','Error',data.error); return; }

    const u=window.utils;
    const sla=data.sla||1;
    const jBreached=data.journeyBreached, qBreached=data.uwQueueBreached;

    el.innerHTML=`
<!-- Proposal Header -->
<div class="chart-card" style="margin-bottom:14px">
  <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;justify-content:space-between;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:12px">
    <div>
      <div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:800;color:var(--text-primary);font-family:monospace;letter-spacing:0.02em">${u.esc(proposalNo)}</div>
      <div style="margin-top:8px;display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap">
        <span class="badge blue">${u.esc(data.bizType)}</span>
        <span class="badge grey">${u.esc(data.product)}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:20px;flex-wrap:wrap">
      <div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.06em;font-weight:700">Inward Date</div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-top:4px">${u.fmtDate(data.inwardDate)}</div></div>
      <div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.06em;font-weight:700">Current Bucket</div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-top:4px">${u.esc(data.currentBucket)}</div></div>
      <div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.06em;font-weight:700">Current Status</div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:${data.currentStatus?.toLowerCase().includes('accept')?'#22c55e':data.currentStatus?.toLowerCase().includes('reject')?'#ef4444':'#f59e0b'};margin-top:4px">${u.esc(data.currentStatus)}</div></div>
      <div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.06em;font-weight:700">Queue Movements</div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-top:4px">${data.queueMovements}</div></div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- SLA / TAT Metrics -->
<div class="kpi-grid kpi-grid-3" style="margin-bottom:14px">
  <div class="kpi-card ${jBreached?'':''}">
    <div class="kpi-label">Journey TAT <span class="kpi-icon">🛣️</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value" style="color:${jBreached?'#ef4444':'#22c55e'}">${u.fmtDays(data.journeyTat)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">${jBreached?'⚠️ Breached':'✅ Within SLA'} · Total days from inward date</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">UW Queue TAT <span class="kpi-icon">⏱️</span></div>
    <div class="kpi-value" style="color:${qBreached?'#ef4444':'#22c55e'}">${u.fmtDays(data.uwQueueTat)}</div>
    <div class="kpi-sub">${qBreached?'⚠️ Breached':'✅ Within SLA'} · Days in UW queue only</div>
  </div>
  <div class="kpi-card">
    <div class="kpi-label">Last UW <span class="kpi-icon">👤</span></div>
    ${data.lastUw
      ? `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:18px;line-height:1.2">${u.esc(data.lastUw.name)}</div><div class="kpi-sub">Action date: ${u.fmtDate(data.lastUw.date)}</div>`
      : `<div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:14px;color:#475569">No UW record</div><div class="kpi-sub">UW Productivity Sheet not uploaded</div>`}
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Two-panel: Audit Trail + UW Decisions -->
<div class="chart-grid chart-grid-2" style="margin-bottom:14px">
  <div class="data-table-wrap">
    <div class="data-table-header"><div>
      <div class="data-table-title">Audit Trail <span style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;font-weight:400">· ${data.auditTrail.length} queue entries</span></div>
      <div class="data-table-meta">Complete proposal journey · Chronological order</div>
    </div></div>
    <div style="overflow-x:auto">
      <table class="dt" style="font-size:11px">
        <thead><tr><th>Bucket</th><th>From</th><th>Decision</th><th>Queue Start</th><th>Queue End</th><th>Days</th><th>Status</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody>
          ${data.auditTrail.length
            ? data.auditTrail.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
                <td><span class="badge ${r.current_bucket?.includes('UW')?'blue':'grey'}">${u.esc(r.current_bucket||'-')}</span></td>
                <td style="color:#64748b">${u.esc(r.coming_from_bucket||'-')}</td>
                <td style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:10px">${u.esc(r.coming_with_decision||'-')}</td>
                <td style="color:#64748b">${u.fmtDateTime(r.queue_start_date)}</td>
                <td style="color:#64748b">${u.fmtDateTime(r.queue_end_date)}</td>
                <td class="text-right" style="color:${Number(r.no_of_days)>sla?'#ef4444':'#22c55e'};font-weight:700">${u.fmtDays(r.no_of_days)}</td>
                <td style="font-size:10px;color:#94a3b8">${u.esc(r.proposal_level_status_norm||r.proposal_level_status||'-')}</td>
              </tr>`).join('')
            : '<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#64748b">No audit trail available — upload Audit Log Report</td></tr>'}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>

  <div class="data-table-wrap">
    <div class="data-table-header"><div>
      <div class="data-table-title">UW Decisions <span style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;font-weight:400">· ${data.uwDecisions.length} action${data.uwDecisions.length!==1?'s':''}</span></div>
      <div class="data-table-meta">All underwriter actions on this proposal</div>
    </div></div>
    <div style="overflow-x:auto">
      <table class="dt" style="font-size:11px">
        <thead><tr><th>UW Name</th><th>Action Type</th><th>Date</th><th>Status</th></tr></thead>
        <tbody>
          ${data.uwDecisions.length
            ? data.uwDecisions.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
                <td style="font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap">${u.esc(r.uw_name)}</td>
                <td><span class="badge ${r.is_final?'green':'amber'}">${u.esc(r.action_type)}</span></td>
                <td style="color:#64748b">${u.fmtDate(r.action_date)}</td>
                <td><span class="badge ${r.is_status==='Clear'?'green':'amber'}">${r.is_status}</span></td>
              </tr>`).join('')
            : '<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#64748b">No UW records — upload UW Productivity Sheet</td></tr>'}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Export buttons -->
<div style="display:flex;gap:10px;justify-content:flex-end;margin-top:8px">
  <button class="btn btn-download" id="ddExportExcel">⬇ Download Excel</button>
  <button class="btn btn-secondary" id="ddExportPdf">📄 Export PDF</button>
</div>`;

    document.getElementById('ddExportExcel')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const data=await window.protrack.drilldown.exportExcel(_source, proposalNo);
      await window.protrack.export.toExcel('proposal_detail', data, `Proposal_${proposalNo.replace(/\//g,'_')}`);
    });
    document.getElementById('ddExportPdf')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const result=await window.protrack.export.toPdf('Drill-Down', {});
      if (result.success) window.utils.toast(`PDF saved to ${result.filePath}`,'success');
      else window.utils.toast(`PDF export failed: ${result.error}`,'error');
    });
  }

  function showMsg(msg) {
    const el=document.getElementById('ddResults'); if (el) el.innerHTML=`<div style="color:#f59e0b;font-size:12px;padding:4px 0">⚠️ ${msg}</div>`;
  }

  return { render };
})();


================================================================================

'use strict';
window.tabSettings = (function () {

  let _settings={}, _activeSection='security';

  async function render() {
    const el=document.getElementById('tab-settings'); if (!el) return;
    _settings = await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
    el.innerHTML=`
<div style="display:flex;gap:0;height:calc(100vh - 160px);overflow:hidden">
  <!-- Left Nav -->
  <div style="width:200px;min-width:200px;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border-subtle);border-radius:var(--radius-lg);padding:12px;margin-right:14px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px">
    ${[['security','🔒','Security'],['sla','⏱️','SLA Config'],['data','📊','Data Management'],['export','📄','Export Config'],['appearance','🎨','Appearance'],['about','ℹ️','About']].map(([id,icon,label])=>`
    <div class="nav-item ${id==='security'?'active':''}" data-section="${id}" onclick="window.tabSettings._switchSection('${id}')">
      <span>${icon}</span><span>${label}</span>
    </div>`).join('')}
  </div>
  <!-- Right Panel -->
  <div style="flex:1;overflow-y:auto;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border-subtle);border-radius:var(--radius-lg);padding:28px">
    <div id="settingsPanel"></div>
  </div>
</div>`;
    renderSection('security');
  }

  async function renderSection(id) {
    _activeSection=id;
    document.querySelectorAll('[data-section]').forEach(el=>el.classList.toggle('active',el.dataset.section===id));
    const panel=document.getElementById('settingsPanel'); if (!panel) return;
    const s=_settings;

    if (id==='security') {
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">Security</h2>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:24px">Protect Full History access with a PIN.</p>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">PIN Protection</label>
  <div class="radio-group">
    <label class="radio-option"><input type="radio" name="pinEnabled" value="true" ${s.security_pin_enabled==='true'?'checked':''}><span>Enabled</span></label>
    <label class="radio-option"><input type="radio" name="pinEnabled" value="false" ${s.security_pin_enabled!=='true'?'checked':''}><span>Disabled</span></label>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Set / Change PIN <span style="color:#64748b;font-weight:400">(4–6 digits)</span></label>
  <div style="display:flex;gap:10px">
    <input type="password" class="form-input" id="newPin" placeholder="New PIN" maxlength="6" style="max-width:160px">
    <input type="password" class="form-input" id="confirmPin" placeholder="Confirm PIN" maxlength="6" style="max-width:160px">
  </div>
  <div class="form-hint">Leave blank to keep existing PIN</div>
</div>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Auto-lock</label>
  <select class="ctrl-select" id="autolock" style="min-width:180px">
    ${[['0','Never'],['5','After 5 minutes'],['15','After 15 minutes'],['30','After 30 minutes'],['60','After 1 hour']].map(([v,l])=>`<option value="${v}" ${s.security_autolock_minutes===v?'selected':''}>${l}</option>`).join('')}
  </select>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" id="saveSecurityBtn">Save Changes</button>`;

      document.getElementById('saveSecurityBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const enabled=document.querySelector('input[name="pinEnabled"]:checked')?.value==='true';
        const newPin=document.getElementById('newPin').value;
        const confirm=document.getElementById('confirmPin').value;
        if (newPin && newPin!==confirm) { window.utils.toast('PINs do not match','error'); return; }
        if (newPin && (newPin.length<4||newPin.length>6||!/^\d+$/.test(newPin))) { window.utils.toast('PIN must be 4-6 digits','error'); return; }
        const r=await window.protrack.settings.saveMultiple({'security_pin_enabled':enabled.toString(),'security_autolock_minutes':document.getElementById('autolock').value});
        if (newPin) await window.protrack.settings.save('pin_hash_pending', newPin); // handled via PIN save handler
        _settings=await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
        window.utils.toast('Security settings saved','success');
      });
    }

    else if (id==='sla') {
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">SLA Configuration</h2>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:24px">Changing these values immediately affects all dashboard calculations.</p>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">SLA Threshold (days)</label>
  <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
    <input type="number" class="form-input" id="slaThreshold" value="${s.sla_threshold_days||'1'}" min="1" max="30" style="max-width:100px">
    <span style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px">days · Proposals exceeding this are flagged as breached</span>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Pending Rate% Warning Threshold</label>
  <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
    <input type="number" class="form-input" id="pendingThreshold" value="${s.pending_rate_warning_pct||'10'}" min="1" max="100" style="max-width:100px">
    <span style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px">% · UW Pending Rate above this shows red indicator</span>
  </div>
</div>
<div style="background:var(--amber-bg);border:1px solid var(--amber-border);border-radius:var(--radius-md);padding:12px 16px;margin-bottom:20px">
  <div style="color:#f59e0b;font-size:12px;font-weight:600">⚠️ Note: Changes take effect immediately across all tabs</div>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" id="saveSlaBtn">Save Changes</button>`;

      document.getElementById('saveSlaBtn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
        try {
          const sla=parseInt(document.getElementById('slaThreshold').value)||1;
          const pend=parseInt(document.getElementById('pendingThreshold').value)||10;
          const r=await window.protrack.settings.saveMultiple({sla_threshold_days:String(sla),pending_rate_warning_pct:String(pend)});
          if (!r||!r.success) { window.utils.toast('Save failed','error'); return; }
          _settings=await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
          if (window.appSettings) { window.appSettings.sla_threshold_days=String(sla); window.appSettings.pending_rate_warning_pct=String(pend); }
          window.utils.toast('SLA configuration saved','success');
        } catch(e) { window.utils.toast('Save failed: '+e.message,'error'); }
      });
    }

    else if (id==='data') {
      const history=await window.protrack.settings.getUploadHistory();
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">Data Management</h2>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:20px">Manage upload history and database location.</p>
<h3 style="font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-bottom:12px">Upload History</h3>
<div style="overflow-x:auto;margin-bottom:20px">
  <table class="dt" style="font-size:11px">
    <thead><tr><th>Batch ID</th><th>Type</th><th>Filename</th><th>Rows</th><th>Date Range</th><th>Uploaded</th><th>Action</th></tr></thead>
    <tbody>
      ${history.length
        ? history.map((r,i)=>`<tr class="${i%2===1?'alt':''}">
            <td class="mono" style="font-size:10px">${window.utils.esc(r.batch_id)}</td>
            <td><span class="badge ${r.type==='audit_log'?'blue':'green'}">${r.type==='audit_log'?'Audit Log':'UW Sheet'}</span></td>
            <td style="max-width:200px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${window.utils.esc(r.filename)}</td>
            <td class="text-right">${window.utils.fmtNum(r.rows)}</td>
            <td style="color:#64748b;font-size:10px">${r.date_from?window.utils.fmtDate(r.date_from)+' → '+window.utils.fmtDate(r.date_to):'-'}</td>
            <td style="color:#64748b;font-size:10px">${r.uploaded_at?r.uploaded_at.substring(0,16):'-'}</td>
            <td><button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="window.tabSettings._deleteBatch('${r.batch_id}','${window.utils.esc(r.filename)}')">Delete</button></td>
          </tr>`).join('')
        : '<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:#64748b">No uploads yet</td></tr>'}
    </tbody>
  </table>
</div>
<h3 style="font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-bottom:12px">Database Location</h3>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Database Folder</label>
  <div style="display:flex;gap:10px">
    <input type="text" class="form-input" id="dbPathInput" value="${window.utils.esc(s.db_path||'')}" placeholder="C:\\ProTrack\\Data">
    <button class="btn btn-secondary" id="browseDbBtn">Browse</button>
  </div>
  <div class="form-hint">Change where the database file is stored</div>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" id="changeDbPathBtn">Move Database</button>`;

      document.getElementById('browseDbBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const r=await window.protrack.dialog.selectFolder();
        if (r.success) document.getElementById('dbPathInput').value=r.folderPath;
      });
      document.getElementById('changeDbPathBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const newPath=document.getElementById('dbPathInput').value;
        if (!newPath) return;
        window.utils.modal({title:'Move Database',body:'This will copy your database to the new location. The app will restart. Continue?',confirmText:'Move',onConfirm:async()=>{
          const r=await window.protrack.settings.changeDbPath(newPath);
          if (r.success) window.utils.toast('Database moved successfully. Please restart the app.','success');
          else window.utils.toast('Move failed: '+r.error,'error');
        }});
      });
    }

    else if (id==='export') {
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">Export Configuration</h2>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:24px">Settings applied to every PDF export.</p>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Company Name</label>
  <input type="text" class="form-input" id="companyName" value="${window.utils.esc(s.export_company_name||'')}" placeholder="Tata AIG General Insurance Company">
  <div class="form-hint">Appears in PDF header and footer</div>
</div>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Company Logo Path</label>

    <input type="text" class="form-input" id="logoPath" value="${window.utils.esc(s.export_logo_path||'')}" placeholder="C:\\ProTrack\\logo.png">

  </select>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" id="saveExportBtn">Save Changes</button>`;

      document.getElementById('browseLogoBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async ()=>{const r=await window.protrack.dialog.selectFile([{name:'Images',extensions:['png','jpg','jpeg']}]);if(r.success)document.getElementById('logoPath').value=r.filePath;});
      document.getElementById('browseExportBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async ()=>{const r=await window.protrack.dialog.selectFolder();if(r.success)document.getElementById('exportPath').value=r.folderPath;});
      document.getElementById('saveExportBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async ()=>{
        await window.protrack.settings.saveMultiple({export_company_name:document.getElementById('companyName').value,export_logo_path:document.getElementById('logoPath').value,export_output_path:document.getElementById('exportPath').value,export_pdf_page_size:document.getElementById('pdfPageSize').value});
        _settings=await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
        if (window.appSettings) Object.assign(window.appSettings,_settings);

    else if (id==='appearance') {
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">Appearance</h2>

  <div class="radio-group">

  </div>

<div class="form-group">

    <label class="radio-option"><input type="radio" name="sidebarStyle" value="icons_only" ${s.appearance_sidebar_style==='icons_only'?'checked':''}><span>Icons only</span></label>
  </div>
</div>
<div class="form-group">
  <label class="form-label">Date Format</label>
  <select class="ctrl-select" id="dateFormat" style="min-width:200px">
    ${[['DD-MM-YYYY','DD-MM-YYYY (default)'],['MM-DD-YYYY','MM-DD-YYYY'],['YYYY-MM-DD','YYYY-MM-DD (ISO)']].map(([v,l])=>`<option value="${v}" ${(s.appearance_date_format||'DD-MM-YYYY')===v?'selected':''}>${l}</option>`).join('')}
  </select>
</div>
<button class="btn btn-primary" id="saveAppearanceBtn">Save Changes</button>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:11px;margin-top:12px">Theme and sidebar changes apply instantly.</p>`;

      document.getElementById('saveAppearanceBtn')?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const theme   = document.querySelector('input[name="theme"]:checked')?.value || 'dark';
        const sidebar = document.querySelector('input[name="sidebarStyle"]:checked')?.value || 'icons_labels';
        const dateFmt = document.getElementById('dateFormat').value;
        try {
          const r = await window.protrack.settings.saveMultiple({
            appearance_theme: theme,
            appearance_sidebar_style: sidebar,
            appearance_date_format: dateFmt
          });
          if (!r || !r.success) { window.utils.toast('Save failed — database error', 'error'); return; }
          _settings = await window.protrack.settings.getAll();
          if (window.appSettings) Object.assign(window.appSettings, _settings);
          // Apply immediately — no restart needed
          if (window.applyTheme)   window.applyTheme(theme);
          if (window.applySidebar) window.applySidebar(sidebar);
          window.utils.toast('Appearance updated', 'success');
        } catch(e) {
          window.utils.toast('Save failed: ' + e.message, 'error');
        }
      });
    }

    else if (id==='about') {
      const stats=await window.protrack.settings.getDbStats();
      const v=await window.protrack.app.getVersion();
      panel.innerHTML=`
<h2 style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">About ProTrack Analytics</h2>
<p style="color:#64748b;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:24px">System information</p>
${[
  ['APP VERSION',v.version||'2.0.0'],
  ['ELECTRON VERSION',v.electronVersion||'-'],
  ['TOTAL PROPOSALS IN DATABASE',stats.totalProposalRows?.toLocaleString()||'0'],
  ['UW ACTIONS IN DATABASE',stats.totalUwActions?.toLocaleString()||'0'],
  ['TOTAL UPLOAD BATCHES',stats.totalBatches?.toLocaleString()||'0'],
  ['DATABASE FILE SIZE',stats.dbSize||'-'],
  ['DATABASE PATH',stats.dbFile||'-'],
  ['DATA PERIOD',stats.dateFrom?`${stats.dateFrom?.substring(0,10)} → ${stats.dateTo?.substring(0,10)}`:'-'],
].map(([label,val])=>`
<div style="padding:14px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border-subtle)">
  <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.08em;margin-bottom:6px">${label}</div>
  <div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);font-family:${label.includes('PATH')||label.includes('VERSION')?'monospace':'inherit'};word-break:break-all">${window.utils.esc(String(val))}</div>
</div>`).join('')}
<div style="margin-top:20px;padding:14px 16px;background:var(--blue-bg);border:1px solid var(--blue-border);border-radius:var(--radius-md)">
  <div style="font-size:12px;color:#60a5fa;font-weight:600">Tata AIG General Insurance Company</div>
  <div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;margin-top:4px">ProTrack Analytics V2.0 · Retail Health Intelligence · All data stored locally</div>
</div>`;
    }
  }

  async function _deleteBatch(batchId, filename) {
    window.utils.modal({
      title:'Delete Upload Batch',
      body:`Delete all data from <strong>${filename}</strong>? This cannot be undone and will remove this data from Full History.`,
      confirmText:'Delete',danger:true,
      onConfirm:async()=>{
        const r=await window.protrack.settings.deleteBatch(batchId);
        if (r.success) { window.utils.toast('Batch deleted','success'); renderSection('data'); }
        else window.utils.toast('Delete failed: '+r.error,'error');
      }
    });
  }

  function _switchSection(id) { renderSection(id); }

  window.tabSettings = { render, _switchSection, _deleteBatch };
  return { render, _switchSection, _deleteBatch };
})();

  <script>
    async function init() {
      try {
        const stats=await window.protrack.settings.getDbStats();
        const info=document.getElementById('dbInfo');
        if (stats&&stats.totalProposalRows>0) {
          document.getElementById('dbInfoText').textContent=`${stats.totalProposalRows.toLocaleString()} proposals in DB`;
          info.style.display='flex';
        }
      } catch {}
      try {
        const v=await window.protrack.app.getVersion();
        document.getElementById('versionLabel').textContent=`v${v.version}`;
      } catch {}
    }

    document.getElementById('cardCurrent').addEventListener('click', async () => {
      await window.protrack.upload.clearSession();
      window.location.href='../app/index.html#current';
    });

    document.getElementById('cardHistory').addEventListener('click', async () => {
      try {
        const pinRequired=await window.protrack.settings.pinRequired ? await window.protrack.settings.pinRequired() : false;
        if (pinRequired) { showPinDialog(); return; }
      } catch {}
      window.location.href='../app/index.html#history';
    });

    function showPinDialog() {
      const overlay=document.createElement('div');
      overlay.className='pin-overlay';
      overlay.innerHTML=`
        <div class="pin-card">
          <div class="pin-title">🔒 Full History Access</div>
          <div class="pin-sub">Enter your PIN to continue</div>
          <input type="password" class="pin-input" id="pinInput" placeholder="• • • •" maxlength="6" autofocus>
          <button class="pin-btn" id="pinSubmit">Unlock →</button>
          <div class="pin-error" id="pinError"></div>
          <span class="pin-cancel" id="pinCancel">Cancel</span>
        </div>`;
      document.body.appendChild(overlay);
      document.getElementById('pinInput').focus();
      document.getElementById('pinSubmit').addEventListener('click', verifyPin);
      document.getElementById('pinInput').addEventListener('keydown', e=>{ if(e.key==='Enter') verifyPin(); });
      document.getElementById('pinCancel').addEventListener('click', ()=>overlay.remove());

      async function verifyPin() {
        const pin=document.getElementById('pinInput').value;
        const errEl=document.getElementById('pinError');
        if (!pin||pin.length<4) { errEl.textContent='Enter your 4-6 digit PIN'; return; }
        try {
          const r=await window.protrack.settings.verifyPin(pin);
          if (r&&r.success) { overlay.remove(); window.location.href='../app/index.html#history'; }
          else { errEl.textContent='Incorrect PIN. Try again.'; document.getElementById('pinInput').value=''; document.getElementById('pinInput').focus(); }
        } catch { errEl.textContent='Verification failed. Try again.'; }
      }
    }

    init();
  </script>
</body>
</html>

  <div class="setup-card">
    <div class="logo-row">
      <div class="logo-icon">P</div>
      <div class="logo-text">
        <h1>ProTrack Analytics</h1>
        <p>Retail Health Intelligence</p>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="setup-title">Welcome — First Time Setup</div>
    <div class="setup-subtitle">
      Choose a folder where ProTrack will store its database. This is a one-time step.
      The folder can be on any drive and can be changed later from Settings.
    </div>

    <div class="field-label">Database Folder</div>
    <div class="folder-row">
      <input type="text" class="folder-input" id="folderPath" placeholder="e.g. C:\ProTrack\Data" readonly>
      <button class="btn-browse" id="btnBrowse">Browse</button>
    </div>
    <div class="field-hint">All data will be stored as a single file (protrack.db) inside this folder.</div>

    <div class="error-msg" id="errorMsg"></div>

    <button class="btn-confirm" id="btnConfirm" disabled>Confirm and Open ProTrack</button>

    <div class="divider"></div>
    <div class="footer-note">
      ProTrack Analytics v2.0 &nbsp;|&nbsp; Tata AIG General Insurance Company<br>
      All data is stored locally on this machine. Nothing is sent to the internet.
    </div>
  </div>

  <script>
    const folderInput = document.getElementById('folderPath');
    const btnBrowse   = document.getElementById('btnBrowse');
    const btnConfirm  = document.getElementById('btnConfirm');
    const errorMsg    = document.getElementById('errorMsg');

    let selectedFolder = '';

    function showError(msg) {
      errorMsg.textContent = msg;
      errorMsg.classList.add('visible');
    }

    function hideError() {
      errorMsg.classList.remove('visible');
    }

    btnBrowse.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      const result = await window.protrack.setup.selectFolder();
      if (result.success) {
        selectedFolder = result.folderPath;
        folderInput.value = selectedFolder;
        btnConfirm.disabled = false;
        hideError();
      }
    });

    btnConfirm.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      if (!selectedFolder) return;
      hideError();
      btnConfirm.disabled = true;
      btnConfirm.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner"></span>Setting up database...';

      const result = await window.protrack.setup.saveConfig(selectedFolder);

      if (result.success) {
        btnConfirm.innerHTML = '<span class="spinner"></span>Opening ProTrack...';
        await window.protrack.setup.complete();
      } else {
        showError(result.error || 'Setup failed. Please try a different folder.');
        btnConfirm.disabled = false;
        btnConfirm.textContent = 'Confirm and Open ProTrack';
      }
    });
  </script>
</body>
</html>


================================================================================
FILE: LAUNCH.bat
================================================================================
@echo off
title ProTrack Analytics

echo.
echo  ====================================================
echo   ProTrack Analytics v2.0  -  Tata AIG
echo  ====================================================
echo.

:: Check if Electron is installed
if exist "node_modules\electron\dist\electron.exe" goto launch

echo  First run detected. Downloading Electron (approx 30 seconds)...
echo  This only happens ONCE.
echo.
call npm install --production 2>nul
if errorlevel 1 (
  echo.
  echo  ERROR: npm install failed. Make sure Node.js is installed.
  echo  Download Node.js from: https://nodejs.org
  pause
  exit /b 1
)

:launch
echo  Launching ProTrack Analytics...
echo.
node_modules\electron\dist\electron.exe .

@echo off
title Building ProTrack Analytics Installer

echo.
echo  ====================================================
echo   Building ProTrack Analytics Windows Installer
echo  ====================================================
echo.
echo  Installing build tools...
call npm install 2>nul
echo.
echo  Building installer (this takes 1-2 minutes)...
call npx electron-builder --win --x64
echo.
echo  Done! Your installer is in the dist\ folder.
echo  Share "dist\ProTrack Analytics Setup 2.0.0.exe" with users.
echo.
pause

FILE: diagnose.js

/**
 * ProTrack Analytics - Diagnostic Script
 * Run with:  node diagnose.js
 * This will create PROTRACK_DIAGNOSTIC_REPORT.txt on your Desktop
 */

const fs   = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const os   = require('os');
const { execSync, spawnSync } = require('child_process');

const lines = [];
const DESKTOP = path.join(os.homedir(), 'Desktop');
// Always save in the script folder too (guaranteed to work)
const REPORT_LOCAL = path.join(__dirname, 'PROTRACK_DIAGNOSTIC_REPORT.txt');
// Try Desktop first, fall back to script folder
const REPORT = fs.existsSync(DESKTOP) ? path.join(DESKTOP, 'PROTRACK_DIAGNOSTIC_REPORT.txt') : REPORT_LOCAL;

function log(msg) { console.log(msg); lines.push(msg); }
function section(title) { log(''); log('='.repeat(60)); log('  ' + title); log('='.repeat(60)); }
function ok(msg)   { log('  [OK]   ' + msg); }
function fail(msg) { log('  [FAIL] ' + msg); }
function warn(msg) { log('  [WARN] ' + msg); }
function info(msg) { log('  [INFO] ' + msg); }

function run(cmd) {
  try {
    return execSync(cmd, { encoding: 'utf-8', timeout: 10000 }).trim();
  } catch (e) {
    return null;
  }
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
log('');
log('  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗');
log('  ║    ProTrack Analytics  —  Diagnostic Report              ║');
log('  ║    ' + new Date().toLocaleString().padEnd(52) + '║');
log('  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝');

// ─── 1. SYSTEM ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('1. SYSTEM INFORMATION');
info('OS:          ' + os.type() + ' ' + os.release() + ' (' + os.arch() + ')');
info('Platform:    ' + process.platform);
info('Home:        ' + os.homedir());
info('Script dir:  ' + __dirname);
info('Node.js:     ' + process.version);
info('V8:          ' + process.versions.v8);
info('RAM:         ' + Math.round(os.totalmem() / 1024 / 1024 / 1024) + ' GB');

// ─── 2. NODE / NPM ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('2. NODE.JS & NPM');

const nodeVer = run('node --version');
if (nodeVer) {
  const maj = parseInt(nodeVer.replace('v',''));
  if (maj >= 18) ok('Node.js ' + nodeVer + ' (✓ meets requirement ≥18)');
  else fail('Node.js ' + nodeVer + ' — UPGRADE REQUIRED (need v18 or higher)');
} else {
  fail('Node.js NOT FOUND in PATH — install from https://nodejs.org');
}

const npmVer = run('npm --version');
if (npmVer) ok('npm ' + npmVer);
else fail('npm NOT FOUND');

// ─── 3. PROJECT STRUCTURE ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('3. PROJECT FOLDER STRUCTURE');
info('Looking in: ' + __dirname);

const requiredFiles = [
  'main.js',
  'preload.js',
  'package.json',
  'database/db-adapter.js',
  'database/ingest.js',
  'database/query.js',
  'database/schema.js',
  'ipc/handlers.js',
  'ipc/handlers/upload.js',
  'ipc/handlers/executive.js',
  'ipc/handlers/pipeline.js',
  'ipc/handlers/uw.js',
  'ipc/handlers/tat.js',
  'ipc/handlers/drilldown.js',
  'ipc/handlers/settings.js',
  'ipc/handlers/export.js',
  'src/landing/landing.html',
  'src/setup/setup.html',
  'src/app/index.html',
  'src/app/app.js',
  'src/app/utils.js',
  'src/styles/global.css',
  'src/vendor/chart.umd.min.js',
  'assets/icon.ico',
];

let missingFiles = 0;
for (const f of requiredFiles) {
  const full = path.join(__dirname, f);
  if (fs.existsSync(full)) {
    ok(f);
  } else {
    fail('MISSING: ' + f);
    missingFiles++;
  }
}
if (missingFiles === 0) ok('All ' + requiredFiles.length + ' required files present');
else fail(missingFiles + ' file(s) missing — re-extract the zip');

// ─── 4. DEPENDENCIES ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('4. NODE_MODULES / DEPENDENCIES');

const depsToCheck = [
  { name: 'sql.js',   key: 'sql.js',   file: 'node_modules/sql.js/dist/sql-wasm.wasm' },
  { name: 'xlsx',     key: 'xlsx',     file: 'node_modules/xlsx/xlsx.js' },
  { name: 'electron', key: 'electron', file: 'node_modules/electron/package.json' },
];

for (const dep of depsToCheck) {
  const full = path.join(__dirname, dep.file);
  if (fs.existsSync(full)) {
    const pkgPath = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', dep.key, 'package.json');
    let ver = '?';
    try { ver = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(pkgPath)).version; } catch {}
    ok(dep.key + '@' + ver);
  } else {
    fail(dep.key + ' — NOT INSTALLED. Run: npm install');
  }
}

// Check sql-wasm.wasm specifically (needed for sql.js in packaged app)
const wasmPath = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'sql.js', 'dist', 'sql-wasm.wasm');
if (fs.existsSync(wasmPath)) {
  const wasmSize = fs.statSync(wasmPath).size;
  ok('sql-wasm.wasm present (' + Math.round(wasmSize / 1024) + ' KB)');
} else {
  fail('sql-wasm.wasm MISSING — sql.js will fail to load');
}

// Check if electron binary exists
const electronBin = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'electron', 'dist', 'electron.exe');
const electronBinAlt = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'electron', 'dist', 'electron');
if (fs.existsSync(electronBin)) {
  const sz = fs.statSync(electronBin).size;
  ok('electron.exe present (' + Math.round(sz / 1024 / 1024) + ' MB)');
} else if (fs.existsSync(electronBinAlt)) {
  ok('electron binary present (Linux/Mac)');
} else {
  fail('Electron binary NOT FOUND at node_modules/electron/dist/electron.exe');
  warn('Run:  npm install   — to download the Electron binary');
}

// ─── 5. PACKAGE.JSON ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('5. PACKAGE.JSON VALIDATION');
try {
  const pkg = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(path.join(__dirname, 'package.json'), 'utf-8'));
  ok('package.json is valid JSON');
  info('name:    ' + pkg.name);
  info('version: ' + pkg.version);
  info('main:    ' + pkg.main);
  
  if (pkg.main && fs.existsSync(path.join(__dirname, pkg.main))) {
    ok('Entry point "' + pkg.main + '" exists');
  } else {
    fail('Entry point "' + pkg.main + '" DOES NOT EXIST');
  }

  const deps = Object.keys(pkg.dependencies || {});
  info('Dependencies: ' + deps.join(', '));
  
  if (deps.includes('better-sqlite3')) {
    fail('better-sqlite3 found in dependencies — this requires native compilation and WILL FAIL');
    warn('This package should use sql.js instead. Re-download the latest version.');
  } else {
    ok('No native modules (better-sqlite3 absent — correct)');
  }
} catch (e) {
  fail('package.json parse error: ' + e.message);
}

// ─── 6. MODULE LOAD TEST ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
section('6. MODULE LOAD TEST');

const modulesToTest = [
  'database/db-adapter.js',
  'database/schema.js',
  'database/ingest.js',
  'database/query.js',
  'ipc/handlers.js',
];

for (const mod of modulesToTest) {
  try {
    require(path.join(__dirname, mod));
    ok(mod + ' loads OK');
  } catch (e) {
    fail(mod + ' FAILED: ' + e.message);
  }
}

// Test sql.js init
log('');
info('Testing sql.js initialization (async)...');
const initSqlJs = require(path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'sql.js'));
const wasmFile  = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'sql.js', 'dist', 'sql-wasm.wasm');

initSqlJs({ locateFile: () => wasmFile }).then(SQL => {
  ok('sql.js WASM loaded successfully');

  // Quick DB test
  const { Database } = require(path.join(__dirname, 'database', 'db-adapter'));
  const schema = require(path.join(__dirname, 'database', 'schema'));
  const tmpDb = path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'protrack_diag_' + Date.now() + '.db');
  
  const db = new Database(tmpDb);
  db._db = new SQL.Database();  // Use in-memory for test
  db._save = () => {};          // Skip disk write in test
  
  schema.initialise(db);
  const row = db.prepare("SELECT value FROM app_settings WHERE key='sla_threshold_days'").get();
  ok('Database schema created, default settings: sla_threshold_days=' + (row ? row.value : '?'));
  
  try { fs.unlinkSync(tmpDb); } catch {}
  
  // ─── 7. ELECTRON CHECK ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  section('7. ELECTRON VERSION CHECK');
  
  const ePath = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'electron', 'dist', 'electron.exe');
  const ePathAlt = path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', '.bin', 'electron');
  
  let electronPath = null;
  if (fs.existsSync(ePath)) electronPath = ePath;
  else if (fs.existsSync(ePathAlt)) electronPath = ePathAlt;
  
  if (electronPath) {
    const result = spawnSync(electronPath, ['--version'], { encoding: 'utf-8', timeout: 8000 });
    if (result.stdout) {
      ok('Electron version: ' + result.stdout.trim());
    } else if (result.error) {
      fail('Electron failed to start: ' + result.error.message);
    } else {
      warn('Electron ran but produced no output (stderr: ' + (result.stderr || 'none') + ')');
    }
  } else {
    fail('Electron binary not found — run: npm install');
  }

  // ─── 8. CONFIG / APPDATA ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  section('8. APP DATA / PREVIOUS CONFIG');
  
  const appDataDirs = [
    path.join(os.homedir(), 'AppData', 'Roaming', 'protrack-analytics'),
    path.join(os.homedir(), 'AppData', 'Roaming', 'ProTrack Analytics'),
    path.join(os.homedir(), 'AppData', 'Local', 'protrack-analytics'),
  ];
  
  let foundAppData = false;
  for (const d of appDataDirs) {
    if (fs.existsSync(d)) {
      foundAppData = true;
      info('AppData found: ' + d);
      const files = fs.readdirSync(d);
      info('Contents: ' + files.join(', '));
      const cfgPath = path.join(d, 'config.json');
      if (fs.existsSync(cfgPath)) {
        try {
          const cfg = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(cfgPath, 'utf-8'));
          ok('config.json found: dbPath=' + cfg.dbPath);
          if (cfg.dbPath && fs.existsSync(cfg.dbPath)) {
            ok('Database folder exists: ' + cfg.dbPath);
          } else {
            warn('Database folder configured but DOES NOT EXIST: ' + cfg.dbPath);
            warn('App will show setup screen on next launch.');
          }
        } catch (e) {
          warn('config.json found but cannot read: ' + e.message);
        }
      } else {
        info('No config.json — app will show first-run setup screen');
      }
    }
  }
  if (!foundAppData) {
    info('No AppData folder found — this is normal for first run');
  }

  // ─── 9. LAUNCH TEST ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  section('9. TRY LAUNCHING ELECTRON');
  
  if (electronPath) {
    info('Attempting to start Electron for 5 seconds...');
    const result = spawnSync(electronPath, [
      __dirname,
      '--enable-logging',
      '--log-level=0'
    ], {
      encoding: 'utf-8',
      timeout: 6000,
      env: { ...process.env, ELECTRON_ENABLE_LOGGING: '1' }
    });
    
    const stdout = (result.stdout || '').trim();
    const stderr = (result.stderr || '').trim();
    
    if (result.status === 0 || result.signal === 'SIGTERM') {
      ok('Electron started and exited normally');
    } else if (result.error && result.error.code === 'ETIMEDOUT') {
      ok('Electron is running (timed out waiting = still alive = GOOD!)');
    } else {
      warn('Electron exit code: ' + result.status);
    }
    
    if (stdout) { info('STDOUT:'); stdout.split('\n').slice(0,20).forEach(l => info('  ' + l)); }
    if (stderr) { info('STDERR:'); stderr.split('\n').slice(0,30).forEach(l => info('  ' + l)); }
  } else {
    warn('Skipping launch test — Electron not installed');
  }

  // ─── 10. SUMMARY ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  section('10. SUMMARY & RECOMMENDED ACTIONS');
  
  const electronInstalled = fs.existsSync(path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'electron', 'dist', 'electron.exe'));
  const sqlJsInstalled    = fs.existsSync(path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'sql.js', 'package.json'));
  const xlsxInstalled     = fs.existsSync(path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'xlsx', 'package.json'));
  const missingBsqlite3   = !fs.existsSync(path.join(__dirname, 'node_modules', 'better-sqlite3'));
  
  if (!sqlJsInstalled || !xlsxInstalled || !electronInstalled) {
    log('');
    fail('ACTION REQUIRED: Run the following command in this folder:');
    log('');
    log('      npm install');
    log('');
    log('  Then double-click LAUNCH.bat again.');
  } else if (!missingBsqlite3) {
    log('');
    fail('ACTION REQUIRED: You have better-sqlite3 installed which causes the crash.');
    log('  Fix: delete node_modules folder, then run: npm install');
  } else {
    log('');
    ok('All dependencies present. If app still does not open:');
    info('1. Check STDERR output in section 9 above for the crash reason');
    info('2. Make sure no antivirus is blocking electron.exe');
    info('3. Try running: node_modules\\electron\\dist\\electron.exe .');
    info('   in this folder, and look at the error message');
  }

  // ─── WRITE REPORT ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  section('REPORT SAVED');
  const report = lines.join('\n') + '\n';
  fs.writeFileSync(REPORT_LOCAL, report, 'utf-8');
  if (REPORT !== REPORT_LOCAL) {
    try { fs.writeFileSync(REPORT, report, 'utf-8'); } catch {}
  }
  log('Report saved to:');
  log('  ' + REPORT_LOCAL + '  (always)');
  if (REPORT !== REPORT_LOCAL) log('  ' + REPORT + '  (Desktop)');
  log('');
  log('  PLEASE SEND THIS FILE to your developer.');
  log('');

}).catch(e => {
  fail('sql.js FAILED TO LOAD: ' + e.message);
  fail('Stack: ' + e.stack);
  
  section('REPORT SAVED');
  const report = lines.join('\n') + '\n';
  try { 
    fs.writeFileSync(REPORT_LOCAL, report, 'utf-8'); 
    log('Report saved: ' + REPORT_LOCAL); 
  } catch {}
});
